Aesrael

Aesrael is a [High Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf") who is encountered at a camp west of [Sunderstone Gorge](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunderstone_Gorge "Skyrim:Sunderstone Gorge") during the quest [Once A Hunter](/wiki/Skyrim:Once_A_Hunter "Skyrim:Once A Hunter"). He grew up as an orphan and gave up his life as a notorious member of the [Crimson Dirks](/wiki/Skyrim:Crimson_Dirks "Skyrim:Crimson Dirks") bandit gang, now living at a camp with his wolf [Dusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Dusk "Skyrim:Dusk"). He is hostile and will attack on sight.

Aesrael wears [Hide Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Armor "Skyrim:Hide Armor") and [Hide Boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots"). He wields a leveled bow, carries 50 steel arrows, a random amount of [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), [Aesrael's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Aesrael%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Aesrael's Journal") and [a key to his chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Aesrael%27s_Key "Skyrim:Aesrael's Key"), and has a 25% chance to carry a [lockpick](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick"). The key is needed for the related quest to unlock the chest containing the [Elven Hunter Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Hunter_Armor "Skyrim:Elven Hunter Armor") and a copy of *[The Crimson Dirks, v7](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Crimson_Dirks,_v7 "Skyrim:The Crimson Dirks, v7")*.

He is accompanied by Dusk, who will likely detect you before he does and attack.

## Related Quests

- **[Once A Hunter](/wiki/Skyrim:Once_A_Hunter "Skyrim:Once A Hunter")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Elven_Hunter "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Elven Hunter"): Track down a hunter with a dangerous past.

Aeta

**Aeta**, a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [child](/wiki/Skyrim:Child "Skyrim:Child"), is the daughter of [Oslaf](/wiki/Skyrim:Oslaf "Skyrim:Oslaf") and [Finna](/wiki/Skyrim:Finna "Skyrim:Finna"). She lives in her family's [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Oslaf%27s_House "Skyrim:Oslaf's House") in [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village"). She is also one of the few villagers, along with Finna, [Nikulas](/wiki/Skyrim:Nikulas_(Dragonborn) "Skyrim:Nikulas (Dragonborn)"), [Frea](/wiki/Skyrim:Frea "Skyrim:Frea"), and [Storn](/wiki/Skyrim:Storn_Crag-Strider "Skyrim:Storn Crag-Strider"), not under Miraak's control after you exit the Temple of Miraak.

She wears a unique set of dark brown [child's clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Child%27s_Clothes_(Dragonborn) "Skyrim:Child's Clothes (Dragonborn)") with an apparent dusting of snow on the shoulders, and a pair of unique [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shoes_(xx03c81a) "Skyrim:Shoes (xx03c81a)"). She carries the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Oslaf%27s_House_Key "Skyrim:Oslaf's House Key") to her house and a selection of [food and toys](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Child "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"). She is much more like her mother, as she is friendly towards strangers, unlike her father.

## Dialogue

When spoken to she can say:

:   *"I want to be a great hunter like [Wulf](/wiki/Skyrim:Wulf_Wild-Blood "Skyrim:Wulf Wild-Blood"). I practice stalking prey on the rabbits and the foxes in the woods."*
:   *"Mother worries when I walk too far from the village. She says a dragon might snatch me up, but I'm not afraid."*
:   *"The elders talk of great cities much bigger than our village, but why would anyone need so many buildings?"*

### Conversations

Aeta may be seen talking to her father about her first hunt:

:   **Aeta**: *"Papa, when can I go on my first hunt?"*
:   **Oslaf**: *"I've told you before, little cub, you're not old enough yet."*
:   **Aeta**: *"I just want to see. I promise not to get in the way of the hunters, and I'm not afraid of the beasts in the forest."*
:   **Oslaf**: *"I have given my answer, little cub. I know you are brave and have the heart of a great she-wolf, but all things have a time and place."*
:   **Aeta**: *"Yes, papa."*

## Quest-Related Events

If spoken to during the [Gardener of Men](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gardener_of_Men "Skyrim:The Gardener of Men") while Storn is being sacrificed:

:   *"What's happening to Storn?"*

Once Storn is dead:

:   *"What does it mean? What was that? What happened to him?"*
:   *"Leave me alone."*

She will approach the body to pay her respects.

:   *"It can't be... please, All-Maker, send him back to us..."*

## Notes

- Aeta will be sent to [Honorhall Orphanage](/wiki/Skyrim:Honorhall_Orphanage "Skyrim:Honorhall Orphanage") and can be [adopted](/wiki/Skyrim:Adoption "Skyrim:Adoption") if both her parents are killed.[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire")
  - This is not possible until the completion of [At The Summit of Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:At_the_Summit_of_Apocrypha "Skyrim:At the Summit of Apocrypha"), as her [father](/wiki/Skyrim:Oslaf "Skyrim:Oslaf") is marked essential until then.
    - If you adopt Aeta, you won't be able to move her back to Solstheim. This includes [Severin Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Severin_Manor "Skyrim:Severin Manor") in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").
- Her dialogue for seeing a dead body (*"Oh no! By the gods! This can't be happening!"*) is the same as other children, even though the Skaal believe in a single god.
- Aeta is the only child that can be found on Solstheim.

## Bugs

- Once at Honorhall, Aeta may be unadoptable, repeating *"I must get back to the village"* instead of adoption dialogue, despite the player having approval from [Constance](/wiki/Skyrim:Constance_Michel "Skyrim:Constance Michel"). Speaking to Aeta at all before speaking to Constance may trigger this, causing the dialogue to persist even after getting permission.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.3, fixes this bug.
  - Reloading the save at the entrance to the orphanage and speaking to Constance first should fix this.
- Sometimes, after being adopted, she cannot be interacted with like a normal child, instead repeating *"I must get back to the village."* She will still refer to you as "Mama/Papa" in passing and will initiate gift/game dialogue, but cannot be activated manually.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.3, fixes this bug.

Afflicted Refugee

An Afflicted Refugee uses Vile Vapor

**Afflicted Refugees** can be [encountered](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Hook.2C_Afflicted_Refugee_Headed_to_High_Rock "Skyrim:World Interactions") wandering [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"). They have unusually red skin and the ability to [vomit poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Vile_Vapor "Skyrim:Vile Vapor") at close range.

Their inventories are fully leveled, but they usually wear [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes").

## Related Quests

- **[The Only Cure](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Only_Cure "Skyrim:The Only Cure")**: Slay an apostate [worshipper](/wiki/Skyrim:Orchendor "Skyrim:Orchendor") for the Daedra Lord [Peryite](/wiki/Lore:Peryite "Lore:Peryite").

## Dialogue

When approached they will say:

:   *"Are you finished ogling the grotesque? I suppose I should be grateful you didn't simply attack me."*
:   **Your skin... Are you ill?**
:   *"I am one of the Afflicted. I'd have been dead from this plague a year ago if not for [Peryite](/wiki/Lore:Peryite "Lore:Peryite")'s protection."*
:   **Where are you going?**
:   *"Returning to [High Rock](/wiki/Lore:High_Rock "Lore:High Rock"). Our shepherd lost his way, and I fear Peryite's wrath may consume those who remain with him. Kesh could tell you more. I just want out of Skyrim as quickly as possible."*

This will start a miscellaneous objective: Find Kesh at the Peryite Shrine.

If spoken to again:

:   **I have more questions.**
:   *"And I have no more time for talking. Go speak with Kesh if you're so curious."*

## Bugs

- The refugees may continuously respawn, overriding other random encounters. **?**

Afflicted

The **Afflicted** are a collection of Bretons 'blessed' by [Peryite](/wiki/Lore:Peryite "Lore:Peryite") with a wasting disease. For whatever reason the Daedric Prince chose to then isolate them in [Bthardamz](/wiki/Skyrim:Bthardamz "Skyrim:Bthardamz"), where you are sent during the Daedric quest [The Only Cure](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Only_Cure "Skyrim:The Only Cure"). They have unusually red skin and the ability to [vomit poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Vile_Vapor "Skyrim:Vile Vapor") at close range. When the quest is completed, various **Afflicted Remnants** may be found roaming Skyrim and they will attack you on sight. The Afflicted are weak adversaries at most levels, but can overwhelm in groups of casters.

## Related Quests

- **[The Only Cure](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Only_Cure "Skyrim:The Only Cure")**: Slay an apostate [worshipper](/wiki/Skyrim:Orchendor "Skyrim:Orchendor") for the Daedra Lord [Peryite](/wiki/Lore:Peryite "Lore:Peryite").

## Notes

- Afflicted inside Bthardamz cannot respawn, since the interior of the ruin is set not to respawn. The ones outside, however, can respawn if you leave the dungeon long enough during and after The Only Cure.
  - Version 2.1.2 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") prevents the ones outside the dungeon from respawning.

## Bugs

- Several Afflicted don't spawn during The Only Cure because the parent marker for them is never enabled.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.7, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Aftershock

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-College of Winterhold.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-College_of_Winterhold.png) | **Put an end to the rupture caused by the Eye of Magnus.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Tolfdir](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir "Skyrim:Tolfdir") |
| Location(s): | [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)"), Radiant location |
| Reward: | Leveled gold |
| ID: | MGR30 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [The Eye of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Eye_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Eye of Magnus") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [The Eye of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Eye_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Eye of Magnus") | | |

Magic Anomalies emerging from the rupture

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak with [Tolfdir](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir "Skyrim:Tolfdir").
2. Travel to location where the rupture is and defeat enemies in its vicinity.
3. Return for your reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

This quest is initiated from [Tolfdir](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir "Skyrim:Tolfdir") at the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") after becoming Arch-Mage. When asked *"Is there anything I should be aware of?"* Tolfdir will respond that there is some sort of magical disturbance which seems to be related to the Eye of Magnus, and will provide a quest location.

Travel to the quest location given. The map marker will point you to any one of twenty-seven locations in Skyrim (there are three possible locations in each hold). Defeat the [Magic Anomalies](/wiki/Skyrim:Magic_Anomaly "Skyrim:Magic Anomaly") and return to Tolfdir for a leveled gold reward. However, if the rupture occurred in [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)"), then you do not receive anything, as the College gets no thanks from the already unhappy citizens.

### Reward

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 500 |
| 10–19 | 750 |
| 20–29 | 1,000 |
| 30–39 | 1,250 |
| 40+ | 1,500 |

## Notes

- Although Tolfdir suggests that you bring the [Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:Staff of Magnus") with you, it is not required to complete the quest.
- You may encounter Magic Anomalies in the wilderness without accepting the quest from Tolfdir. The Magic Anomalies will never disappear or change their location until you destroy them.
- One of the possible sites for a magical rupture to appear is located right next to [Windstad Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Windstad_Manor "Skyrim:Windstad Manor").[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire")
- Magic Anomalies scale with you and on higher levels will all have grand souls.
- This quest may be repeated as many times as you like by asking Tolfdir if there is anything you should be aware of.

## Bugs

- If you come across the Magic Anomalies before speaking to Tolfdir then the quest cannot be completed.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.3, addresses this issue. The quest will automatically start at stage 20 upon defeating all Magic Anomalies. You can then return to Tolfdir for your reward and the quest will end normally.
- The rupture may be randomly placed intersecting water, if this is the case then it cannot be completed as the rift does not properly show up and anomalies do not spawn.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- Sometimes Tolfdir does not offer the dialogue option "Is there anything I should be aware of?" to start the quest. The dialogue might appear after a few days. **?**
  -  This can be fixed with the console command `setstage MGR30 0` to make the dialogue appear.

## Quest Stages

| Aftershock (MGR30) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | There have been reports of some sort of magical anomaly in Skyrim. Tolfdir fears it is a side-effect of Ancano's meddling with the Eye of Magnus, and has asked that I look into it. He suggested I take the Staff of Magnus with me, just in case. *Objective 10:* Close the Rupture |
| 20 |  | I have found and shut down the magical anomaly Tolfdir was worried about. I should return to him and let him know it's been dealt with. *Objective 20:* Return to Tolfdir |
| 200 | ☑ | A magical anomaly was reported in Skyrim; it seems to have been connected to Ancano's meddling with the Eye of Magnus. I successfully shut it down before it could become a greater problem. |
| 201 | ☑ |  |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MGR30 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MGR30`.

Agent Lorcalin

**Agent Lorcalin** is a [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor") [wizard](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Wizard_(class) "Skyrim:Thalmor Wizard (class)") that can be found near a [shrine of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines#Shrine_of_Talos "Skyrim:Shrines") in [White River Gorge](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River "Skyrim:White River"), but only after you've approached the shrine. He is carrying out his [orders](/wiki/Skyrim:Lorcalin%27s_Orders "Skyrim:Lorcalin's Orders") from [Elenwen](/wiki/Skyrim:Elenwen "Skyrim:Elenwen") to hunt down any "heretics" at the shrine. He and a [Thalmor soldier](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Soldier "Skyrim:Thalmor Soldier") will appear at the shrine once you get close to it, but will not be present before then.

He wears the standard [robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Hooded_Thalmor_Robes "Skyrim:Hooded Thalmor Robes"), [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Boots "Skyrim:Thalmor Boots"), and [gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Gloves "Skyrim:Thalmor Gloves") of a Thalmor wizard, and wields either a steel, elven, or glass [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger"), depending on [your level](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor#Leveled_Equipment "Skyrim:Thalmor"). He also carries his orders and a random selection of [gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Gems "Skyrim:Gems"), [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"), [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), and gold.

## Related Quests

- **[Elisif's Tribute](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif%27s_Tribute "Skyrim:Elisif's Tribute")**: Take Torygg's war horn to the Shrine of Talos.

## Bugs

- Agent Lorcalin and his escort may be seen insta-spawning on top of the shrine instead of ambushing you properly.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.8, addresses this issue. They now have added travel packages to force them to walk up from where they are initially enabled.

A male Breton battlemage

The **Aggressive Adventurer** is a hostile NPC [randomly encountered](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Aggressive_Adventurer "Skyrim:World Interactions") in the wilderness. They will simply be named by their race when you see them in gameplay.

Agmaer

Agmaer as a Dawnguard member

**Agmaer** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)") initially found in [Dayspring Canyon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dayspring_Canyon "Skyrim:Dayspring Canyon") on his way to join the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)"). He wants to become a [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") hunter but is too nervous to enter [Fort Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Fort Dawnguard") alone and will instead accompany you to see [Isran](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran "Skyrim:Isran"). He will move on to become one of the first recruits of the Dawnguard and will, after completing the quest [Prophet](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet_(Dawnguard) "Skyrim:Prophet (Dawnguard)"), be available as a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers").

Before becoming a member of the Dawnguard, Agmaer wears a set of farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#000261c0 "Skyrim:Clothes") with a pair of [hide bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Bracers "Skyrim:Hide Bracers") and a pair of [hide boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots"). He carries random [leveled bandit loot](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists "Skyrim:Leveled Lists") and a [torch](/wiki/Skyrim:Torch "Skyrim:Torch"), and also has a 25% chance of carrying 1-9 gold. He is equipped with an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe") which he refers to as his Pa's axe.

When you return from Dimhollow Crypt after the quest [Awakening](/wiki/Skyrim:Awakening "Skyrim:Awakening"), Agmaer will be a full-fledged member of the Dawnguard and don the clothes to match the position, including brown [Dawnguard heavy armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Dawnguard Heavy Armor") with [Dawnguard boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Boots "Skyrim:Dawnguard Boots") and [Dawnguard gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Dawnguard Gauntlets"), and is now equipped with a [Dawnguard war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_War_Axe "Skyrim:Dawnguard War Axe") and a [crossbow](/wiki/Skyrim:Crossbow "Skyrim:Crossbow"). He will also have a new routine in Fort Dawnguard. He owns one of the cots in the northern section on the ground floor and sleeps there between 8pm and 4am. After he wakes up he walks over to the western dining area where he hangs out all day long, eating, relaxing, or wandering around.

## Related Quests

- **[Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(quest) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (quest)")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Speak with the leader of the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)").
- **[Kindred Judgment](/wiki/Skyrim:Kindred_Judgment "Skyrim:Kindred Judgment")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Confront [Lord Harkon](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord_Harkon "Skyrim:Lord Harkon").
- **[Destroying the Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Destroying_the_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Destroying the Dawnguard")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Kill the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)") leaders.

### Dawnguard

*"I'm, uh... my name is Agmaer, sir."*

*"Uh, crossbow? I've never..."*

As you enter Dayspring Canyon, you will find the young farmer standing near the central lake, obviously undecided on whether to see Isran or not. When he notices you he will say:

:   *"Oh, hey there! You here to join the Dawnguard, too? Truth is, I'm a little nervous. I've never done anything like this before. I hope you don't mind if I walk up with you. Hey, uh, don't tell Isran I was afraid to meet him by myself. Not the best first impression for a new vampire hunter, I guess. You've probably killed lots of vampires, huh? I'm sure Isran will sign you right up. Not sure he'll take me. I hope so."*

If you talk to Agmaer on the way to Fort Dawnguard, he will say:

:   *"I heard what's going on. The vampires, the Dawnguard, all of it. I wanted to help, so here I am."*

When he arrives at the foot of the fort, he will stop and admire the view:

:   *"That must be it. Fort Dawnguard... Wow. Bigger than I expected. Where is everybody? This place looks almost deserted."*

Just before reaching the entrance, he will say:

:   *"I guess this is it. Wish me luck."*

Once inside, you will find Agmaer respectfully waiting while Isran has a discussion with [Vigilant Tolan](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigilant_Tolan "Skyrim:Vigilant Tolan") about the destruction of the [Hall of the Vigilants](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Vigilant "Skyrim:Hall of the Vigilant"). If you approach Agmaer he will only whisper:

:   *"You go ahead. I'll talk to Isran in a minute."*

He will then stay in the background while you talk to Isran and he sends you to [Dimhollow Crypt](/wiki/Skyrim:Dimhollow_Crypt "Skyrim:Dimhollow Crypt"). Isran will then turn to Agmaer:

**Isran**: *"You there, boy. Stop skulking in the shadows and step up here. What's your name?"*
**Agmaer**: *"I'm, uh... my name is Agmaer, sir."*
**Isran**: *"Do I look like a 'sir' to you, boy? I'm not a soldier, and you're not joining the army."*
**Agmaer**: *"Yes, si... Isran."*
**Isran**: *"Didn't I tell you to step forward? Hmm... Farm boy, eh? What's your weapon?"*
**Agmaer**: *"Uh, my weapon? I mostly just use my pa's axe, when wolves are attacking the goats or something."*
**Isran**: *"'My pa's axe', Stendarr preserve us. Don't worry, I think we can make a Dawnguard out of you. Here, take this crossbow and let's see how you shoot."*
**Agmaer**: *"Uh, crossbow? I've never..."*
**Isran**: *"Yes, a crossbow. Best thing for killing vampires. Just take a few shots at those crates over there."*

When speaking with Agmaer at this point, he will explain why he wants to join the Dawnguard:

:   **Why did you join the Dawnguard?**
:   *"I've heard the rumors around Skyrim. I know something's going on. And I've seen the vampires. I felt I had two choices. I could either live in fear of the night, or I could help do something to help protect my people."*

When exiting conversation he will say either:

:   *"Keep your neck covered!"*
:   *"Take care."*

### Kindred Judgment

When it is time to confront [Lord Harkon](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord_Harkon "Skyrim:Lord Harkon") during the quest [Kindred Judgement](/wiki/Skyrim:Kindred_Judgment "Skyrim:Kindred Judgment"), Agmaer will listen to Isran's speech in the main hall along with the other Dawnguard members. When Isran gives the order, he will travel halfway across [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") to [Castle Volkihar](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Keep "Skyrim:Volkihar Keep") and will participate in the joint effort to kill all residing vampires, while shouting:

:   *"Victory to the Dawnguard!"*
:   *"We'll secure the castle. You just get to their master!"*

When all is said and done, he will sheathe his weapon and walk all the way back to Fort Dawnguard and live there indefinitely with the other members. If you interact with him at this time he will state, "Isran will never admit it, but I'm sure he's proud of you."

## Notes

- When Agmaer shoots the steel bolts at the targets during his initial training, they never disappear. Agmaer will continue to shoot bolts until you return from any Dawnguard quest. This is a good way to get a lot of steel bolts early.

## Bugs

- If the [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") [add-on](/wiki/Skyrim:Add-ons "Skyrim:Add-ons") is installed, when asking him to follow you, Agmaer may have the same dialogue as [Talvas Fathryon](/wiki/Skyrim:Talvas_Fathryon "Skyrim:Talvas Fathryon").
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 1.0.2, fixes this bug.
- Agmaer may not regenerate after entering bleedout because he inherited stats from the bandit templates where the bleedout override checkbox was enabled.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.0.8, fixes this bug.
- If you have killed [Durak](/wiki/Skyrim:Durak "Skyrim:Durak") before entering [Dayspring Canyon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dayspring_Canyon "Skyrim:Dayspring Canyon"), when you first meet Agmaer, he will be hostile to you.

# Skyrim:Agna

## Overview

| Agna (RefID: 000A737F) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Location | [Hillgrund's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Hillgrund%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Hillgrund's Tomb") | | |
| Race | [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") | Gender | Female |
| Level | 1 | Class | [Bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000A737F | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000A9599 |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 0 (**Dead**) | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 25 |
| Voice Type | [FemaleNord](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleNord "Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleNord") | | |

Agna lying dead in [Hillgrund's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Hillgrund%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Hillgrund's Tomb")

**Agna** is a dead [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)") and [Golldir](/wiki/Skyrim:Golldir "Skyrim:Golldir")'s aunt, whom you help look for if you accept the side quest he offers, [Ancestral Worship](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancestral_Worship "Skyrim:Ancestral Worship"), outside [Hillgrund's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Hillgrund%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Hillgrund's Tomb"). She went into the tomb in attempt to stop the necromancer [Vals Veran](/wiki/Skyrim:Vals_Veran "Skyrim:Vals Veran") from defiling her ancestors, but met her untimely end before reaching him.

She wears a leveled [light cuirass](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#light "Skyrim:Armor") with light boots, and may also wear light gauntlets and/or a light shield. She would have wielded a leveled [one-handed weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:One-Handed_Weapons "Skyrim:One-Handed Weapons") and carries a random selection of [beverages](/wiki/Skyrim:Food#Beverages "Skyrim:Food"), [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"), [lockpicks](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick"), [jewelry](/wiki/Skyrim:Jewelry "Skyrim:Jewelry"), [gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Gems "Skyrim:Gems"), [ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingots "Skyrim:Ingots"), tools, and gold.

## Related Quests

- **[Ancestral Worship](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancestral_Worship "Skyrim:Ancestral Worship")**: Help [Golldir](/wiki/Skyrim:Golldir "Skyrim:Golldir") save his aunt and stop a [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Vals_Veran "Skyrim:Vals Veran") from defiling his [ancestral barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hillgrund%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Hillgrund's Tomb").

# Skyrim:Agni

## Overview

| Agni (RefID: 0001AA5F) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Home City | [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") | | |
| House | [Falion's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Falion%27s_House "Skyrim:Falion's House") | | |
| Race | [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") | Gender | Female |
| Level | 4 | Class | [Child](/wiki/Skyrim:Child_(class) "Skyrim:Child (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0001AA5F | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000135E5 |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 65 | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 0 |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 80 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing"), [Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") | | |
| Race Details | [Child](/wiki/Skyrim:Child "Skyrim:Child") | | |
| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | No Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") | Unaggressive |
| Voice Type | [FemaleChild](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleChild "Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleChild") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [CrimeFactionHjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionHjaalmarch "Skyrim:CrimeFactionHjaalmarch"); [MorthalFalionsHouseFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:MorthalFalionsHouseFaction "Skyrim:MorthalFalionsHouseFaction"); [TownMorthalFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:TownMorthalFaction "Skyrim:TownMorthalFaction") | | |

Agni sitting in [Falion's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Falion%27s_House "Skyrim:Falion's House")

**Agni** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [child](/wiki/Skyrim:Child "Skyrim:Child") living in [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"). She was taken in by the resident wizard [Falion](/wiki/Skyrim:Falion "Skyrim:Falion") after the loss of both her parents, and is currently training to be his apprentice. Due to this, she doesn't share the same opinion of him as the rest of the town. She can be seen running around with the other children early in the morning, but mostly stays with Falion in his house during the day.

She gets up at 7am and stays home until 8am, when she goes outside to play with [Virkmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Virkmund "Skyrim:Virkmund"). At 1pm, she returns to Falion's house and wanders around the place, sometimes [conversing](#Conversations) with him. Agni heads to bed at 9pm.

She wears [child's clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Child%27s_Clothes "Skyrim:Child's Clothes") and a pair of [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000e80a8 "Skyrim:Clothing"), and is equipped with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"). She carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Falion%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Falion's House") to [Falion's house](/wiki/Skyrim:Falion%27s_House "Skyrim:Falion's House"), a selection of [food and toys](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Child "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"), and a small amount of gold.

## Dialogue

When she is spoken to she can potentially say:

:   *"Do you like magic? Falion says I'm good at learning. I like learning about magic."*
:   *"My mother and father died years ago. Falion takes care of me now."*
:   *"I asked Falion if someday I could learn from the [mages](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)") in [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"), but he doesn't like that idea."*

## Conversations

Agni may be seen having some random conversations with Falion in his house, as outlined below:

:   **Agni**: *"When I grow up, will I go to the College in Winterhold?"*
:   **Falion**: *"No, I don't think that will be necessary."*
:   **Agni**: *"But I'm learning about magic, and that's what they do there. Shouldn't I go?"*
:   **Falion**: *"The College is not the only place to learn about magic."*
:   **Agni**: *"But you went there, didn't you? Isn't that where you learned?"*
:   **Falion**: *"I was there only for a short time. Much of what I have learned has been on my own. And I will teach you. You have no reason to go there."*
:   **Agni**: *"But..."*
:   **Falion**: *"That is enough."*

:   **Falion**: *"Have you been working on your concentration?"*
:   **Agni**: *"Yes sir, I have."*
:   **Falion**: *"Good. Concentration is paramount when dealing with magical forces."*
:   **Agni**: *"Why?"*
:   **Falion**: *"Because an unfocused mind will almost certainly be obliterated. Destroyed by the forces you attempt to control and yield."*
:   **Agni**: *"Oh."*
:   **Falion**: *"Have no fear. I believe it is within you to excel in your studies. But you must learn to concentrate!"*
:   **Agni**: *"Yes, sir."*

:   **Agni**: *"I had a bad dream again last night."*
:   **Falion**: *"Oh?"*
:   **Agni**: *"I dreamt that you went away. You made monsters."*
:   **Falion**: *"It's just a dream, child. Nothing more."*
:   **Agni**: *"It was scary. It was like it was real!"*
:   **Falion**: *"Hush now. Think no more of it."*

:   **Agni**: *"Is it true that you kill [deer](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer "Skyrim:Deer") and eat their hearts?"*
:   **Falion**: *"What? Where did you hear such a thing?"*
:   **Agni**: *"I don't know. Someone in town said it."*
:   **Falion**: *"It's not true, I assure you."*
:   **Agni**: *"Okay."*
:   **Falion**: *"Don't believe everything you hear, child."*

# Skyrim:Agnis

## Overview

| Agnis (RefID: 00020045) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |

| Other Information | | | |

| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 60 | | |

| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [BanditFriendFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:BanditFriendFaction "Skyrim:BanditFriendFaction"); [The Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:DarkBrotherhoodFaction "Skyrim:DarkBrotherhoodFaction"); [FavorExcludedFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:FavorExcludedFaction "Skyrim:FavorExcludedFaction") | | |

Agnis

**Agnis**, a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [citizen](/wiki/Skyrim:Citizen_(class) "Skyrim:Citizen (class)"), can be found inside [Fort Greymoor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Greymoor "Skyrim:Fort Greymoor"). She acts as the joyful maid to whoever holds Fort Greymoor, although she gives the fort commander a hard time in her *[Complaint Letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Complaint_Letter "Skyrim:Complaint Letter")*. [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir") will give you a [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") contract to assassinate her.

She has her own quarters in the fort, in the northeastern wing, and she sleeps there every night between midnight and 8am. The rest of her time is spent cleaning the surrounding area and neighboring dinner hall, occasionally resting on a chair, eating or taking a nap.

Agnis wears a set of [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#000261c0 "Skyrim:Clothes"), [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000261bd "Skyrim:Boots"), and [gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Gloves#000261c1 "Skyrim:Gloves"). She also keeps a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger") on her person, to defend herself in case Fort Greymoor's many masters and visitors prove to be less than friendly.

## Related Quests

- **[Kill Agnis](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Agnis "Skyrim:Kill Agnis")**: Kill Agnis in [Fort Greymoor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Greymoor "Skyrim:Fort Greymoor").

## Dialogue

Agnis lives a strange existence of a servant to whoever holds Fort Greymoor, with her not caring about who that may be. Attempting to speak to her before starting the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") quest [Kill Agnis](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Agnis "Skyrim:Kill Agnis") will have her offer some comments on her peculiar life:

:   *"I just cook, and clean, and do whatever it is they ask of me."*
:   *"I can't even keep track of all the people who have been in and out of this fort. They come, they go. I barely notice."*
:   *"Hard enough to keep up with who owns this fort. One side takes over, the other runs away. I tell them, "I ain't leaving! I come with the place!" Ha!"*
:   *"I remember one morning, long time ago, I woke up and the place was run by some [Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc"). Went to bed that night, it was all [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"). Don't matter to me."*
:   *"Now, then. I been gabbin' long enough. Too much cleanin' to do."*

### Kill Agnis

If you come to her to fulfill the Brotherhood's contract, speaking to her will have her say:

:   *"You fighter types are always underfoot. You want me to clean? Then scat!"*

Which will give you the opportunity to respond from three topics:

| Topic | Dialogue |
| --- | --- |
| **"You've cleaned your last room, servant."** | *"But I have many more rooms to clean. Fort Greymoor is quite large, and rather filthy if I do say."* |
| **"Sleep now, old woman. Embrace the Void."** | *"Sleep? I can't sleep now! There's too much to be done. And what's this Void you're rambling on about?"* |
| **"(Remain silent)"** | *"I swear, you people are an odd bunch. Please, just step aside, that I may return to my duties!"* |

## Notes

- If she is nearby when bandits occupying the fort are engaged in combat she will fight the bandits with you.
- Agnis belonging to the Dark Brotherhood faction can cause you to get expelled from the Dark Brotherhood if she gets attacked at the wrong time.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.7, fixes this bug.

Agrane Peryval

Agrane Peryval is a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") merchant who can be found at his campsite north of the [Windward Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Windward_Ruins "Skyrim:Windward Ruins"), just outside [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"). You will be directed to him as part of the related quest, although you do not need to purchase anything from him.

He wears a set of [Saturalia clothing](/wiki/Skyrim:Saturalia_Clothes "Skyrim:Saturalia Clothes"), which consists of boots, gloves, clothes, and a hat, and wields an [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven "Skyrim:Elven") mace. He also carries a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") and a selection of [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"). Additionally, he knows the spell [Fast Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fast_Healing "Skyrim:Fast Healing").

## Related Quests

- **[Saturalia Preparation](/wiki/Skyrim:Saturalia_Preparation "Skyrim:Saturalia Preparation")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Saturalia_Holiday_Pack "Skyrim:Saturalia Holiday Pack"): Track down a traveling merchant to take part in end-of-year festivities.

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in Agrane's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be pickpocketed or stolen. They are [restocked](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") every two days.

| 3 | [Saturalia Boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Saturalia_Boots "Skyrim:Saturalia Boots") |  |

Agrius

**Agrius** is a dead [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)") found in the first part of [Halldir's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Halldir%27s_Cairn "Skyrim:Halldir's Cairn"). His dead body is found along with those of his friends, [Vidgrod](/wiki/Skyrim:Vidgrod "Skyrim:Vidgrod") and [Raen](/wiki/Skyrim:Raen "Skyrim:Raen"), next to the magical cairn. According to [his journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Agrius%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Agrius's Journal"), he and his friends were in a bandit gang but were kicked out and took refuge in Halldir's Cairn. He was the last of them to be possessed by [Halldir](/wiki/Skyrim:Halldir "Skyrim:Halldir").

He wears a randomly determined set of [light armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Light_Armor "Skyrim:Armor"); at all levels, there is always a 50% chance he will wear [fur shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Shoes "Skyrim:Fur Shoes") and a set of [fur armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Armor "Skyrim:Fur Armor"), while the other 50% can differ; at level 1-5 it can be [hide boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots") and/or [hide armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Armor "Skyrim:Hide Armor"), at level 6-18, it can be [leather boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots") and/or [leather armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Armor "Skyrim:Leather Armor"), and at level 19-28 it can be [scaled boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Boots "Skyrim:Scaled Boots") and/or [scaled armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Armor "Skyrim:Scaled Armor") or [scaled horn armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Horn_Armor "Skyrim:Scaled Horn Armor"). Additionally, he has a 50% chance of wearing a set of leveled gauntlets, again randomly determined; it can always be [fur bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Bracers "Skyrim:Fur Bracers") but, at level 1-5, there is a 50% chance it can be [hide bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Bracers "Skyrim:Hide Bracers"), at level 6-18 it can be [leather bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Bracers "Skyrim:Leather Bracers") and at level 19, it can be [scaled bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Bracers "Skyrim:Scaled Bracers"). Lastly, there is a 20% chance of him carrying a leveled shield, up to elven quality at level 12.

His weapon of choice is random and leveled as well (up to elven quality at level 22) and can be either a [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"), a [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword") or a [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe"). He also carries a bit of random loot, food and drink, with a slim chance of a [lockpick](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") and/or some gold.

Agrius' body, along with his two friends, is consumed by Halldir to make his three elemental copies during your fight with him.

## Bugs

- Unlike the bodies of Vidgrod and Raen, Agrius' body is not removed after Halldir consumes their souls to summon his elemental copies.

Ahjisi

**Ahjisi**, a [Khajiit](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit "Skyrim:Khajiit") [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)"), is one of the hunters who shows up in [Bloated Man's Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloated_Man%27s_Grotto "Skyrim:Bloated Man's Grotto") hunting [Sinding](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinding "Skyrim:Sinding").

She is part of a tougher group that will only be normally encountered if you choose to help Sinding. They spawn on the path you already traveled from the entrance after speaking with Sinding. If you choose to hunt, then Sinding goes forward into the weaker group with [Rissing](/wiki/Skyrim:Rissing "Skyrim:Rissing"), but if you choose to help him this tougher group will charge forward and attack.

Ahjisi wears a set of [hide armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Armor "Skyrim:Hide Armor") with a matching pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots"). In combat, she relies on two [steel daggers](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger") and a [long bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Bow "Skyrim:Long Bow") with ten [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow"). She also carries two leveled [damage health](/wiki/Skyrim:Damage_Health "Skyrim:Damage Health") [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poison "Skyrim:Poison").

## Related Quests

- **[Ill Met By Moonlight](/wiki/Skyrim:Ill_Met_By_Moonlight "Skyrim:Ill Met By Moonlight")**: Participate in the Daedric Prince [Hircine](/wiki/Skyrim:Hircine "Skyrim:Hircine")'s Great Hunt.

Ahkari

**Ahkari** is a [Khajiit](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit "Skyrim:Khajiit") [pawnbroker](/wiki/Skyrim:Pawnbroker "Skyrim:Pawnbroker") that leads one of three Khajiit [trade caravans](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit_Traders "Skyrim:Khajiit Traders") owned by [Ri'saad](/wiki/Skyrim:Ri%27saad "Skyrim:Ri'saad"). Her caravan stops at [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") and [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"), and includes [Zaynabi](/wiki/Skyrim:Zaynabi "Skyrim:Zaynabi"), [Dro'marash](/wiki/Skyrim:Dro%27marash "Skyrim:Dro'marash"), and [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo").

Ahkari wears a set of [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes#00086991 "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") and a pair of [fine boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Boots#00086993 "Skyrim:Fine Boots"). She is equipped with a [steel war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_War_Axe "Skyrim:Steel War Axe"), and carries a selection of [upper-class items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Rich "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Dialogue

When spoken to:

:   *"So many refuse to talk to us. They call us thieves and smugglers. I am glad to see that you are not such a one."*

:   :   **Have you had trouble with the locals?**
    :   *"Mostly it is the [Nords](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord"). They do not like outsiders in their land, and so we are forbidden to enter the cities. When they look upon us, they see only pickpockets and [skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma") dealers. It is most unfair, but we do our best to ignore them."*

:   :   **How long have you been in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim")?**
    :   *"Not long, in truth. I came to Skyrim after I found myself unwelcome in both [Elsweyr](/wiki/Lore:Elsweyr "Lore:Elsweyr") and [Cyrodiil](/wiki/Lore:Cyrodiil "Lore:Cyrodiil"). I seem to have an unfortunate talent for getting myself involved in misunderstandings with the law. Ri'saad was able to look past that, and it was he who helped to set me up with a trade caravan. Now I work for him."*

## Notes

- The *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")* incorrectly lists Ahkari as an adept-level [trainer](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Skyrim:Trainers") in [Pickpocket](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket").
- According to a *[smuggler's note](/wiki/Skyrim:Smugglers%27_Note "Skyrim:Smugglers' Note")* in an unmarked location around the back of Whiterun, Ahkari may be involved in illegal skooma trade. This note is odd for two reasons, however: Ahkari does not travel to Whiterun on her trade route, nor does she have any obvious relation to the ['seer'](/wiki/Skyrim:Olava_the_Feeble "Skyrim:Olava the Feeble") mentioned by the note.

## Bugs

- Ahkari's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest") is hidden in [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") but it can be accessed if you know where to look. It is located on the east side of Dawnstar between some rocks just a few paces directly south of Irgnir's House, just to the left of [Iron Breaker Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron-Breaker_Mine "Skyrim:Iron-Breaker Mine"). The chest is buried under the snow so it's not visible unless you move your cross-hairs over it. You can take loot from the hidden chest without incurring a bounty, even though what you're actually looting is her current inventory. If you sell her an item, you can head back over to the chest and find it within; if you buy items from her, the gold is also added to the chest.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
- Sometimes if the game doesn't load properly in Dawnstar and/or Riften, she and her crew would not raise camp. So, they will stand when they stay. **?**
- Sometimes if the game doesn't load perfectly in Dawnstar and/or Riften, she and her crew will stay for more than supposed three days. **?**
- Sometimes the caravan can get stuck just off the road between Riften and Windhelm near the Wild Animal Den. **?**
  - Making Kharjo a follower sometimes fixes this.
  -  If you cannot find Ahkari, you can move her to your location by entering the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") commands `prid 7434a` followed by `moveto player`. Using this command outside her normal route may confuse her AI, so it’s best to use this near her campsite outside Dawnstar or Riften.
- The caravan accompanying Ahkari might show up at either Riften or Dawnstar without her. The other Khajiit stand in place but she is nowhere to be found. **?**
  - Fast travelling somewhere and then back may fix this, as well as waiting at their current location.

Ahlam

**Ahlam**, a [Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard "Skyrim:Redguard") [priestess](/wiki/Skyrim:Priest "Skyrim:Priest"), is a healer at the [Temple of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Temple of Kynareth") in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). She is the wife of [Nazeem](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazeem "Skyrim:Nazeem"), who owns [Chillfurrow Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Chillfurrow_Farm "Skyrim:Chillfurrow Farm"). If [Arcadia](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcadia "Skyrim:Arcadia") is killed, Ahlam will take over running [Arcadia's Cauldron](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcadia%27s_Cauldron "Skyrim:Arcadia's Cauldron").

The couple never sets foot on the farm, but are permanent residents of the [Drunken Huntsman](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Drunken_Huntsman "Skyrim:The Drunken Huntsman") and Ahlam sleeps there every night between midnight and 9am. While her self-satisfied husband spends all of his time belittling the citizens of Whiterun, Ahlam uses her healing skills in the Temple of Kynareth from 9am to 9pm, interrupted only by a breath of fresh air near the Gildergreen tree between noon and 4pm. She spends her evenings in the upstairs area of the Huntsman, looking at her lazy husband while he sleeps.

While her husband is obviously wealthy, Ahlam makes a more humble appearance and wears farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#000209a6 "Skyrim:Clothes") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000209a5 "Skyrim:Boots"). She carries an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), along with a selection of [common items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"). She also carries the [key to Wintersand Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Wintersand_Manor "Skyrim:Key to Wintersand Manor").

## Dialogue

When spoken to she can potentially say:

:   *"Looking for my husband Nazeem? Check the Jarl's backside. That's usually where he stuffs himself these days."*
:   *"If you run into my husband Nazeem, remind him that he's not married to himself."*
:   *"Men are all alike, from Skyrim to Hammerfell. They care only for war and politics, and treat their women like cattle."*
:   *"Are you married? You look the type. Make sure you treat your wife with the respect she deserves."* (Only if you are male)
:   *"Here you stand, talking to a married woman. Why? Am I that interesting? Or perhaps there are other things on your mind."*

If Nazeem is dead, she expresses self-pity about her status as a widow with:

:   *"Here you stand, talking to a still grieving widow. Why? Am I that interesting? Or perhaps there are other things on your mind."*

## Conversations

Inside the Temple of Kynareth, Ahlam often takes the opportunity to complain about her useless husband to fellow healer and employer, [Danica Pure-Spring](/wiki/Skyrim:Danica_Pure-Spring "Skyrim:Danica Pure-Spring"), who will do her best to comfort her. Danica always starts the conversation and chooses between a number of random statements and Ahlam will do the same, as seen in the table below:

| Speaker | Conversation |
| --- | --- |
| Danica | *"Something wrong, Ahlam?"* |
| *"Are you alright, Ahlam? You haven't seemed yourself today."* |
| *"What's wrong, dear friend? You seem... distracted today."* |
| Ahlam | *"Oh, it's Nazeem. He's been spending more and more time fawning over the Jarl. I swear, we're hardly ever home at the same time anymore."* |
| *"It's nothing, I just... It's Nazeem. How did we get to this point, Danica? Is there no love left between us?"* |
| *"Hmm? Oh, well... To be honest, I was just thinking of Nazeem. The gap between us seems to be widening. He is just so... self-absorbed."* |
| Danica | *"Now, now, my friend. You must look on the bright side. If soldiers storm the city, there's a good chance your husband may get killed."* |
| *"If you don't mind me saying so, Ahlam, your husband is a damn fool. Any moment spent thinking about him is a moment wasted."* |
| *"Ahlam, let's be honest. Your husband is an arrogant, domineering buffoon. These are the words you used to describe him to me... remember?"* |
| *"Oh dearest, who cares? So your husband is a lout. The work you do here, with me, is invaluable. The people of Whiterun know your true worth."* |
| Ahlam | *"But it's more than that. Nazeem is obsessed with this civil war, as is all of Skyrim. I swear, it will consume us all."* |
| *"Maybe Nazeem's obsession has merit. This civil war seems so big, so unceasing... I'm afraid, Danica. Afraid for us all."* |
| *"Ha! Well, when you put it like that, it certainly puts things into perspective. But enough wallowing. And thank you, Danica."* |
| *"Oh, you are terrible. You do know that, right? Ha ha ha ha ha."* |

## Unused Dialogue

In the [Creation Kit](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Creation_Kit "Skyrim Mod:Creation Kit"), earlier versions of Ahlam's greetings can be found:

| Final | Early |
| --- | --- |
| *"Looking for my husband Nazeem? Check the Jarl's backside. That's usually where he stuffs himself these days."* | *"Looking for my husband? Have you checked the jarl's backside? That's usually where he stuffs himself these days."* |
| *"Are you married? You look the type. Make sure you treat your wife with the respect she deserves."* | *"My dearest Nazeem is a very rich, very important man. His reflection tells him as much every morning."* |
| *"Here you stand, talking to a married woman. Why? Am I that interesting? Or perhaps there are other things on your mind."* | *"There are those, like my husband, who feel the war is a noble endeavor. Everything is noble from the safety of your own home."* |

## Notes

- Nazeem and Ahlam were originally meant to live in their own house, Wintersand Manor, rather than bunk at The Drunken Huntsman. A related faction, a key, location data, and locklist a still exist for the house in the game's data.
  - In a [design document](/wiki/General:Skyrim_Cities%27_Design_Excerpts "General:Skyrim Cities' Design Excerpts"), two large houses, presumably manors, were shown to be located next to [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach") as part of a "Nobles District". In the final game, only Dragonsreach exists at the very top layer of the city, being the only building actually part of the Cloud District.
- The *[Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard")* DLC adds a duplicate of Ahlam to the files. This duplicate is internally known as `DLC1TestAngry`, and is almost completely identical to Ahlam. However, the duplicate doesn't have any dialogue, and her mood is set to "Angry", rather than "Neutral". It's unknown for what purpose this test NPC was made exactly.

## Bugs

- Ahlam carries the [key to Wintersand Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Wintersand_Manor "Skyrim:Key to Wintersand Manor"), but Wintersand Manor is nowhere to be found in Skyrim.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.4, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Ahtar

## Overview

| Ahtar (RefID: 000198B0) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Home City | [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") | | |

| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [CrimeFactionHaafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionHaafingar "Skyrim:CrimeFactionHaafingar"); [Favor104QuestGiverFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:Favor104QuestGiverFaction "Skyrim:Favor104QuestGiverFaction"); [PotentialFollowerFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:PotentialFollowerFaction "Skyrim:PotentialFollowerFaction"); [SolitudeJalasHouseFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:SolitudeJalasHouseFaction "Skyrim:SolitudeJalasHouseFaction"); [TownSolitudeFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:TownSolitudeFaction "Skyrim:TownSolitudeFaction") | | |

Ahtar by his desk in the jail

Roggvir's execution

**Ahtar** is a [Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard "Skyrim:Redguard") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior2H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior2H") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") where he works as public executioner and warden of the [Castle Dour Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour_Dungeon "Skyrim:Castle Dour Dungeon"). He recently let [one of his prisoners](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Hargar "Skyrim:Captain Hargar") escape and will [task you](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Bandit_Leader "Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader") with killing the escapee. In return, Ahtar will not only reward you, he will also become available as a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers").

When first entering Solitude, you will witness Ahtar carrying out his duties as executioner when he decapitates [Roggvir](/wiki/Skyrim:Roggvir "Skyrim:Roggvir") while numerous citizens cheer. After the execution, Ahtar will return to his job in the depths of Castle Dour dungeon where he wanders around from 8am to 8pm. He spends the evening inside the [Winking Skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Winking_Skeever "Skyrim:The Winking Skeever"). When the clock strikes midnight he heads down to the [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Jala%27s_House "Skyrim:Jala's House") of local merchant [Jala](/wiki/Skyrim:Jala "Skyrim:Jala") for eight hours of sleep.

Ahtar is equipped with the rare [headsman's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Headsman%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Headsman's Axe") and wears the unobtainable [executioner's robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Executioner%27s_Robes "Skyrim:Executioner's Robes"), [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Unobtainable_Items#000cf8b0 "Skyrim:Unobtainable Items"), and [gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Unobtainable_Items#Gloves "Skyrim:Unobtainable Items"). He carries an [Orcish sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Sword "Skyrim:Orcish Sword"), the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Jala%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Jala's House") to Jala's house, the [Castle Dour dungeon key](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour_Dungeon_Key "Skyrim:Castle Dour Dungeon Key"), a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic"), and a selection of [middle-class items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Kill the Bandit Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Bandit_Leader "Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader")**: Do a favor by slaying a bandit leader. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Rebuilding the Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebuilding_the_Blades "Skyrim:Rebuilding the Blades")**: Recruit new members for the [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades").

### Kill the Bandit Leader

If you speak to him directly, he will ask:

:   *"You wouldn't be a sellsword, would you? I have a little problem you could solve."*
:   **What's this problem you have?**
:   *"I may have accidentally let a prisoner escape. The leader of one of those bandit groups. I told everyone he died during questioning, and I need you to track him down and make sure he doesn't show up to disprove that."*

:   :   **I'll do it.**

        :   *"Good. I'll have a sack of coin waiting for you when you get back."*

:   :   **Forget it.**

        :   *"Suit yourself."*

If spoken to again before the bandit is dead:

:   *"Remember. I need that bandit dead. Not alive."*

When you return from [Broken Oar Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Oar_Grotto "Skyrim:Broken Oar Grotto") after killing Captain Hargar, he will be grateful and say:

:   *"That's a load off my mind. Here's your pay."*

## Dialogue

If spoken to right after the execution of Roggvir, he'll appear unaffected:

:   *"That makes Twenty-Three."*

When approached he can potentially say:

:   *"Mind yourself in my city, friend/lass. This here axe in full swing is a right terrible sight..."*
:   *"You stay out of trouble, now. The Castle Dour dungeon can break even the strongest will."*
:   *"Not much work being a jailor. Long as you can ignore the pleading and all that."*
:   *"Ain't many visitors come to the dungeon. Every now and then [Sybille Stentor](/wiki/Skyrim:Sybille_Stentor "Skyrim:Sybille Stentor") will come by looking for... volunteers."*

If spoken to directly:

:   **You were the one who executed that man...**
:   *"Aye. I'm the headsman here in Solitude. It's my job"*

    :   **Do they keep you busy?**
    :   *"Depends on what you mean by "busy." I'm also the head jailor in the dungeon here. Quiet job, usually."*

:   **When's your next execution?**
:   *"Ain't got one. But I'd fancy a chance at that [Jaree-Ra](/wiki/Skyrim:Jaree-Ra "Skyrim:Jaree-Ra")'s scrawny neck. Filthy [Argonian](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian "Skyrim:Argonian") never would have set foot in this city, if [High King Torygg](/wiki/Skyrim:Torygg "Skyrim:Torygg") was still alive. I can tell you that."*

If you have killed Jaree-Ra:

:   **I took care of him and the Blackblood Marauders.**
:   *"Good man/lass."*

When exiting conversation he can potentially say:

:   *"Keep your head about you."*
:   *"Just watch yourself. You don't want to meet me on the job."*

## Notes

- Ahtar is marked internally as "courting" Jala, and the two are marked as allies (not actually lovers). He also sleeps in her house but the two will never acknowledge each other or speak of their relationship to you. Neither will anyone else in town.
  - Ahtar is also marked as a friend of [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke"), another relationship that never gets adressed by anyone in-game.
- If you have already killed [Captain Hargar](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Hargar "Skyrim:Captain Hargar"), either during the quest [Lights Out!](/wiki/Skyrim:Lights_Out! "Skyrim:Lights Out!") from [Jaree-Ra](/wiki/Skyrim:Jaree-Ra "Skyrim:Jaree-Ra") or by clearing out the grotto without a specific quest, Ahtar will no longer give you the quest [Kill the Bandit Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Bandit_Leader "Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader"), and as such, can not become a follower through these means. You will then have to increase his disposition in another way (such as through a radiant event) in order to have him become a follower.

## Bugs

- Ahtar's AI schedule gets broken due to his eat package checking for Roggvir's execution still being active and because his jail marker was placed incorrectly. As a result, he'd be stuck inside Jala's house unable to exit once the execution was over and he went home for the first time. This could result in you being unable to talk to him to finish the 'Kill the Bandit Leader' quest.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.6, fixes this bug.
  - If you break into Jala's house while he is supposed to be there (i.e. at night) and then leave, this sometimes fixes his AI and allows him to leave the house normally. You may need to be detected by him and have him order you to leave the house. Also, this fix may sometimes be temporary.

- During his daily routine, headsman Ahtar was supposed to engage in conversation with the imprisoned [Bjartur](/wiki/Skyrim:Bjartur "Skyrim:Bjartur"). However, the two conversations will never be heard due to several developer oversights:
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.

:   **Ahtar**: *"Rest up, scum. Probably getting executed tomorrow."*
:   **Bjartur**: *"Yeah, you said that yesterday."*
:   **Ahtar**: *"Come now. You'll want to show up in Sovngarde refreshed. You got an eternity of merrimakin' ahead of you."* **or**
     *"Guess the headsman's been busy with all your friends. Ha ha ha ha ha!"*

:   **Bjartur**: *"Hey, jailor! What I don't understand is why you're siding with the Imperials."*
:   **Ahtar**: *"Shut up, scum."*
:   **Bjartur**: *"I mean, the Redguards fought off the Aldmeri and the Empire, and now Hammerfell is an independent state. That's all we Nords want for Skyrim!"*
:   **Ahtar**: *"I said shut up, scum!"*
:   **Bjartur**: *"So it's okay if your people rebel against the Empire, but not mine?"*
:   **Ahtar**: *"They aren't my "people." I'm with the Empire because they pay me. And that means I'm out here, and you're in there. So shut up, scum!"*

# Skyrim:Aia Arria

## Overview

| Aia Arria (RefID: 000198D0) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Home City | [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") | | |
| Location | [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College") | | |
| Race | [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") | Gender | Female |
| Level | 6 | Class | [Bard](/wiki/Skyrim:Bard_(class) "Skyrim:Bard (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000198D0 | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0001325C |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 89 | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 72 |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 64 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration"), [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") | | |

| Voice Type | [FemaleSultry](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleSultry "Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleSultry") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [CrimeFactionHaafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionHaafingar "Skyrim:CrimeFactionHaafingar"); [JobBardFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:JobBardFaction "Skyrim:JobBardFaction"); [SolitudeBardsCollegeFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:SolitudeBardsCollegeFaction "Skyrim:SolitudeBardsCollegeFaction"); [TownSolitudeFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:TownSolitudeFaction "Skyrim:TownSolitudeFaction") | | |

Aia Arria

**Aia Arria** is an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") [bard](/wiki/Skyrim:Bard_(class) "Skyrim:Bard (class)") at the [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). According to her teacher, [Pantea Ateia](/wiki/Skyrim:Pantea_Ateia "Skyrim:Pantea Ateia"), Aia is the only student at the College with actual talent, a fact that Aia takes great pride in.

At 4am, she will wake up and go to a class in the Bards College. She will move to a different class at 8am and again at 2pm. She will go to the market at 6pm; however, she also goes to sleep at 6pm, which is a bug in her schedule.

Aia wears a set of farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000261c0 "Skyrim:Clothing") along with a [cowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#00017696 "Skyrim:Clothing") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000261bd "Skyrim:Clothing"). She carries her [key to the Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Bards_College "Skyrim:Key to Bards College"), a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute"), a [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute"), and a selection of [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"). She also wields an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and carries a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic").

## Dialogue

When approached she can potentially say:

:   *"Lady Ateia says my voice is second only to hers. But she's selling me short."*
:   *"Few can resist my charms. Even fewer are worthy of them."*
:   *"Oh, if you haven't heard Dean Pantea sing, you should."*
:   *"I can't understand why Jorn would want to join the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"). Soldiers only appreciate one thing, and it isn't music."*

She will exit conversation with:

:   *"We should talk again sometime."*

Unless you have completed [Tending the Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Tending_the_Flames "Skyrim:Tending the Flames"), in which case she will say:

:   *"Always glad to talk to a bard."*

## Conversations

During the lessons at the Bards College, she may be seen having random conversations with her instructors.

:   **Pantea**: *"You there. Have you performed your voice exercises today?"*
:   **Aia**: *"Always! Perfection takes dedication, after all!"*
:   **Pantea**: *"Yes, well, see that you keep at it. That is all."*

:   **[Inge Six-Fingers](/wiki/Skyrim:Inge_Six_Fingers "Skyrim:Inge Six Fingers")**: *"Your solo performance is about a week away. I expect to hear your early rendition tomorrow, understand?"*
:   **Aia**: *"At this point, I hardly see how your advice would improve it. It's flawless."*
:   **Inge**: *"I'll be the judge of that. Now, back to your practice."*

She was also supposed to converse with [Giraud Gemane](/wiki/Skyrim:Giraud_Gemane "Skyrim:Giraud Gemane"), but due to a [bug](/wiki/Skyrim:Giraud_Gemane#bugs "Skyrim:Giraud Gemane"), her line will never be heard.

:   **Giraud Gemane**: *"Pardon me, but I trust you've been working on your poem, on the classical heroes of Skyrim, yes?"*
:   **Aia**: *"Must it be written? Poetry is so dull when it isn't set to music."*
:   **Giraud**: *"I'm sure it will be fine. Just don't be late."*

She can also be found talking to her fellow students, such as [Jorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorn "Skyrim:Jorn"):

:   **Jorn**: *"What're you going to do after you graduate? I'm thinking of joining the Legion. I hear they're looking for skalds. Just think. Me - a war bard."*
:   **Aia**: *"Lady Ateia has already arranged for me to perform in the court of the Jarl of Falkreath."*
:   **Jorn**: *"You'd better hope the war's over by then. The Stormcloaks would eat you alive!"*
:   **Aia**: *"Hmph. Music tames the most savage beasts. Even Nords."*

Or the unpopular [Illdi](/wiki/Skyrim:Illdi "Skyrim:Illdi"):

:   **Illdi**: *"Alaf keeps making eyes at me."*
:   **Aia**: *"You should tell him to mind his own business."*
:   **Illdi**: *"Aia. You're so mean. I don't think he means anything by it."*
:   **Aia**: *"Have it your way, then."*

[Pantea Ateia](/wiki/Skyrim:Pantea_Ateia "Skyrim:Pantea Ateia") can also be heard complimenting her:

:   **Pantea**: *"Your performance has been excellent lately Aia. You still need training but one day you will make an adequate singer."*
:   **Aia**: *"Yes, Dean. Thank you."*

When shopping at the market, Aia may speak to [Addvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Addvar "Skyrim:Addvar"):

:   **Aia**: *"Salmon looks good today."*
:   **Addvar**: *"Speaking of sounding good, I've heard a couple of your classmates on the street recently."*
:   **Aia**: *"As long as they're playing instruments they're passable. You don't want to hear them sing."*

Or to fruit vendor [Jala](/wiki/Skyrim:Jala "Skyrim:Jala"):

:   **Aia**: *"There's nothing quite like a good vegetable."*
:   **Jala**: *"Vegetables are the food of the Divines."*
:   **Aia**: *"I've heard stanger*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *things,*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *are eaten over at the [Temple of the Divines](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_the_Divines "Skyrim:Temple of the Divines")."*

## Notes

-  Version 1.2.5 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") changes the starting time of her market visit from 6pm to 4pm, so she will be there until 7pm. This change was made due to the unwieldy setup of Bards College-related AI packages, and due to the fact that Aia has no dialogue for the classes at this hour, so it appears as if she wasn't intended to partake in said classes, implying she would more likely be found away from the college.

## Bugs

- Aia can't sleep due to her sleep package being listed below her default sandbox package.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.5, fixes this bug.
- Her sleep package `BardsCollegeSleepEditorLoc18x8` also interferes with her market visiting AI, as both packages are expected to start at 6pm.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.5, addresses this issue. Aia has been given the package `BardsCollegeSleepEditorLoc22x8` like Jorn in its place, making her sleep from 10pm to 8am, so her sleep schedule doesn't interfere with her market visit.
- Considerable dialogue was written for Addvar and his various customers. Unfortunately, they were recorded in [Jala](/wiki/Skyrim:Jala "Skyrim:Jala")'s voice. Aia's dialogue is mixed with Jala's other dialogue. See [Addvar Bugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Addvar#Bugs "Skyrim:Addvar") for this dialogue.
