| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 50 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | **[Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration")**, **[Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration")**, [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration"), [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") | | |
| Perks | [Augmented Frost](/wiki/Skyrim:Augmented_Frost "Skyrim:Augmented Frost") (rank 1); [Augmented Shock](/wiki/Skyrim:Augmented_Shock "Skyrim:Augmented Shock") (rank 1); [Mage Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Mage_Armor "Skyrim:Mage Armor") (rank 1); [Magic Resistance](/wiki/Skyrim:Magic_Resistance "Skyrim:Magic Resistance") (rank 1); [Recovery](/wiki/Skyrim:Recovery "Skyrim:Recovery") (rank 1); [Regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Regeneration "Skyrim:Regeneration") | | |
| Class Details | [CombatMageConjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatMageConjurer "Skyrim:CombatMageConjurer") | | |
| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | No Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") | Unaggressive |
| Voice Type | [MaleEvenToned](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleEvenToned "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleEvenToned") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [CrimeFactionReach](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionReach "Skyrim:CrimeFactionReach"); [MarkarthKeepFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:MarkarthKeepFaction "Skyrim:MarkarthKeepFaction"); [MarkarthWizardFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:MarkarthWizardFaction "Skyrim:MarkarthWizardFaction"); [ServicesMarkarthCastleWizard](/wiki/Skyrim:ServicesMarkarthCastleWizard "Skyrim:ServicesMarkarthCastleWizard"); [TownMarkarthFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:TownMarkarthFaction "Skyrim:TownMarkarthFaction") | | |

Aicantar

**Aicantar** is a [High Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf") [conjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatMageConjurer "Skyrim:CombatMageConjurer"), and is the nephew of [Calcelmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Calcelmo "Skyrim:Calcelmo").

Like his uncle, Aicantar is heavily involved in [Dwemer](/wiki/Lore:Dwemer "Lore:Dwemer") research, where he often spends time by his uncle's side or, in some cases, in Calcelmo's [Dwemer Museum](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Museum#Dwemer_Museum "Skyrim:Dwemer Museum"). However, he does not share all of his uncle's zeal for research.

He wears [blue mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Blue Mage Robes") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0006b46c "Skyrim:Clothing"), and is equipped with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"). He carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Museum_Key "Skyrim:Dwemer Museum Key") to the [Dwemer Museum](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Museum "Skyrim:Dwemer Museum"), a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Nchuand-Zel "Skyrim:Key to Nchuand-Zel") to [Nchuand-Zel](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel "Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel"), and a selection of [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

He normally remains in [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep") with his uncle.

During the quest [Hard Answers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hard_Answers "Skyrim:Hard Answers"), Aicantar will be present at Calcelmo's Laboratory, where unlike the guards, he will not be hostile, but evidently distressed by your breaking in. However, once you reach the Wizard's Tower, he will arrive with [Captain Aquilius](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Aquilius "Skyrim:Captain Aquilius") and two Wizard's Guards after you have duplicated the writing on Calcelmo's Stone, having alerted them to the presence of an intruder. All four will be hostile to you on sight, but you may choose not to engage them and run outside, as they will not follow. He will remain in the tower until [the next quest](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pursuit "Skyrim:The Pursuit") in the Thieves Guild questline begins. Provided he is still alive following Hard Answers, he will return to his normal place at Calcelmo's side and will not remember your presence in the laboratory.

## Related Quests

- **[Hard Answers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hard_Answers "Skyrim:Hard Answers")**: Help translate [Gallus's journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallus%27s_Encoded_Journal "Skyrim:Gallus's Encoded Journal").

- This NPC is one of many potential quest givers or quest targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_NPCs "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Hard Answers

When you enter Calcelmo's Tower you can overhear him talking to the guards:

:   **Wizard's Guard**: *"Sir, are you serious?"*
:   **Aicantar**: *"You heard me, captain- our work must not be disturbed. Kill any intruders on sight. Call for backup if you need it. But let no one through."*
:   **Wizard's Guard**: *"...As you say, sir."*

If Aicantar is alive when you make a rubbing of Calcelmo's Stone, he will burst into the room with his guards and [Captain Aquilius](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Aquilius "Skyrim:Captain Aquilius"):

:   **Aicantar**: *"Accidents like this just don't happen. Someone is trying to sabotage my uncle's research."*
:   **Aquilius**: *"I...all right. If there is a thief, he won't leave this tower alive. But shouldn't we inform Master Calcelmo?"*
:   **Aicantar**: *"I'll deal with my uncle. Just...go! Scour this place from top to bottom!"*
:   **Aquilius**: *"All right men, spread out and search the tower. No telling who - or what - we're dealing with here."*

## Dialogue

When spoken to he can say:

:   *"I'm Calcelmo's nephew. I help him around the laboratory."*
:   *"Don't let my uncle go on about his theories. You'll be here all night."*
:   *"I try not to think about how my uncle got all the [Dwemer Centurion](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Centurion "Skyrim:Dwarven Centurion") parts."*
:   *"I'm afraid to touch half of the things we keep in the tower."*

When exiting a conversation he can say:

:   *"Goodbye. Be careful if you head into the ruins."*
:   *"Back to my studies, then."*

## Conversations

Aicantar may also be seen having random conversations with his uncle:

**Aicantar**: *"Uncle Calcelmo...."*
**Calcelmo**: *"What is it nephew? Can't you see I'm trying to think here?"*
**Aicantar**: *"I just wanted to know if you needed anything."*
**Calcelmo**: *"Um, no. Nothing. Nothing at all."*
**Aicantar**: *"Are you sure?"*
**Calcelmo**: *"Stop bothering me Aicanter*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]*!"*

**Calcelmo**: *"Next season, nephew. Next season for sure...."*
**Aicantar**: *""Next season for sure..." What? Uncle Calcelmo, I don't understand what you mean."*
**Calcelmo**: *"The excavation, Aicantar! Right after I finish my book. We'll start excavating Nchuand-Zel again."*
**Aicantar**: *"Could I maybe, skip the excavation, Uncle Calcelmo? I, uh, I just think you won't need me."*
**Calcelmo**: *"Nonsense, you're a vital part of my research team. You'll be there, have no fear! Now, I don't want to hear another word of protest."*

## Spells

Aicantar knows the following spells:

- [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration")
  - [Oakflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Oakflesh "Skyrim:Oakflesh")
  - [Stoneflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Stoneflesh "Skyrim:Stoneflesh")
- [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration")
  - [Conjure Flame Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Flame_Atronach "Skyrim:Conjure Flame Atronach")
  - [Raise Zombie](/wiki/Skyrim:Raise_Zombie "Skyrim:Raise Zombie")
  - [Reanimate Corpse](/wiki/Skyrim:Reanimate_Corpse "Skyrim:Reanimate Corpse")
- [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction")
  - [Chain Lightning](/wiki/Skyrim:Chain_Lightning "Skyrim:Chain Lightning")
  - [Fireball](/wiki/Skyrim:Fireball "Skyrim:Fireball")
  - [Firebolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Firebolt "Skyrim:Firebolt")
  - [Lightning Bolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Lightning_Bolt "Skyrim:Lightning Bolt")
  - [Incinerate](/wiki/Skyrim:Incinerate "Skyrim:Incinerate")
  - [Thunderbolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Thunderbolt "Skyrim:Thunderbolt")
- [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration")
  - [Close Wounds](/wiki/Skyrim:Close_Wounds "Skyrim:Close Wounds")
  - [Fast Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fast_Healing "Skyrim:Fast Healing")
  - [Steadfast Ward](/wiki/Skyrim:Steadfast_Ward "Skyrim:Steadfast Ward")

## Notes

- After the Hard Answers quest is finished, he may sometimes not rejoin Calcelmo in Understone Keep, instead remaining in the Wizard's Tower for the rest of the game.[*verification needed — what causes this to happen? (see [talk page](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Aicantar#Conflicting_information))*]
- Aicantar is identified as the backup Court Wizard, in case Calcelmo dies. However, since Calcelmo is essential and doesn't have a scripted death, Aicantar never provides merchant services during normal gameplay.
  - He has set of dialogue that comes with his new position. He would instead greet you with: *"Oh, excuse me. With my uncle gone, things are a bit of a mess."* He would offer a look at his wares with: *"Did you need something? A staff? Some enchanting materials?"* or *"I'm not half the wizard my uncle was, but I still have a few spells worth buying."*
- If you [reanimate](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Thrall "Skyrim:Dead Thrall") Aicantar then lose him, he may reappear from thin air and drop dead after [Hard Answers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hard_Answers "Skyrim:Hard Answers") is complete.
- Adopted male children who are living in Markarth may comment *"Aicantar let me see his museum. It's really nice."*
- The author of *[Before the Ages of Man](/wiki/Skyrim:Before_the_Ages_of_Man "Skyrim:Before the Ages of Man")* is named Aicantar of Shimerene. However, they are likely not the same person, as Aicantar of Shimmerene was the "Sapiarch of Indoctrination" and authored propaganda for the First Aldmeri Dominion in the mid-Second Era.

## Bugs

- The guards in Calcelmo's Tower may accuse Aicantar of trespassing, even though he is Calcelmo's nephew.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.3, addresses this issue. They weren't assigned the proper factions.

# Skyrim:Ainethach

Ainethach

**Ainethach** is a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") [miner](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner_(class) "Skyrim:Miner (class)") and the owner of [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten") and its two mines, [Sanuarach Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanuarach_Mine "Skyrim:Sanuarach Mine") and [Fenn's Gulch Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Fenn%27s_Gulch_Mine "Skyrim:Fenn's Gulch Mine"). He has two adult children named [Rondach](/wiki/Skyrim:Rondach "Skyrim:Rondach") and [Voada](/wiki/Skyrim:Voada "Skyrim:Voada") who work in [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep") as the [chef's](/wiki/Skyrim:Anton_Virane "Skyrim:Anton Virane") assistants.

As one of the few native Reachmen to own land in [the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach"), Ainethach is frequently hassled by both the [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") and Nords of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"), who both accuse him of having a secret agenda against their respective groups. His mine also makes him a target for the machinations of [Thonar Silver-Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Thonar_Silver-Blood "Skyrim:Thonar Silver-Blood"), the leader of the Reach's wealthiest and most influential family. You will encounter him during one such time, as [mercenaries](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver-Blood_Mercenary "Skyrim:Silver-Blood Mercenary") hired by the Silver-Bloods, led by [Atar](/wiki/Skyrim:Atar "Skyrim:Atar"), are trying to force him to sell the mine by shutting it down under the pretext of Forsworn activity nearby. You can either aid Ainethach by getting rid of the mercenaries or convince Ainethach to sell his mine to the Silver-Bloods.

Upon raising his disposition, he will become a potential candidate for [marriage](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage").

When you first enter Karthwasten, you will find Ainethach along with two of his miners, [Ragnar](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragnar "Skyrim:Ragnar") and [Lash gra-Dushnikh](/wiki/Skyrim:Lash_gra-Dushnikh "Skyrim:Lash gra-Dushnikh"), having an [argument](#Sanuarach_Mine) with Atar and his fellow sellswords. After this event is over, he will resume his normal routine. Ainethach begins his day by waking up at 7am and leaving [Karthwasten Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten_Hall "Skyrim:Karthwasten Hall") to head outside. He will then spend the next 12 hours working on the exterior of his home, either using a hammer to repair the house or sweeping his balcony. He may also be found taking a break at the table or seated on one of the benches found outside his house. After spending all morning and afternoon outside, Ainethach will head inside his house at 7pm. He will spend the next 5 hours relaxing inside his home, until he goes to sleep at midnight.

Ainethach wears a set of [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes#000cee80 "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") and matching [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Boots#000cee82 "Skyrim:Fine Boots"). He is equipped with a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger") and carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Karthwasten_Hall "Skyrim:Key to Karthwasten Hall") to Karthwasten Hall and a selection of [upper-class items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Rich "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Sanuarach Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanuarach_Mine_(quest) "Skyrim:Sanuarach Mine (quest)")**: End the dispute over [Sanuarach Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanuarach_Mine "Skyrim:Sanuarach Mine").
- **[The Heart of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heart_of_Dibella "Skyrim:The Heart of Dibella")**: Find a new [Sybil](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjotra "Skyrim:Fjotra") for the [Temple of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Temple of Dibella").
- **[The Bonds of Matrimony](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bonds_of_Matrimony "Skyrim:The Bonds of Matrimony")**: Find someone in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") to [marry](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage").

## Dialogue

His potential greetings are:

:   *"I'm one of the few native sons of the Reach that owns land. It doesn't make me very popular."*
:   *"If the Forsworn aren't attacking my town, the Nords are trying to force me off it."*
:   *"Finally, both of my mines are open again. Time for everyone to get back to work."*

If spoken to directly:

:   **Are you in charge here?**
:   *"My family has owned Karthwasten for generations. Rare for anyone in the Reach that isn't a Nord. Not that it does me any good. Nords think I'm working for the Forsworn. Forsworn think I'm working for the Nords."*

### Sanuarach Mine

.jpg)

*"I want you sellswords out of my mine."*

As soon as you enter Karthwasten for the first time, you will find Ainethach arguing with Atar about the occupation of his sellswords inside Sanuarach Mine:

**Ainethach**: *"I want you sellswords out of my mine."*
**Atar**: *"Watch your tongue, native. We'll leave when we're sure there's no Forsworn here."*
**Ainethach**: *"Oh, and when would that be, I wonder? When I sell my land to the Silver-Bloods?"*
**Atar**: *"The Silver-Bloods have made you a very generous offer for this pile of dirt. I suggest you take it."*

If you talk to the miners that are currently out of work, they will express their frustration and desire for Ainethach to deal with the situation. You can ask Ainethach if he is having trouble with the mine:

:   **Trouble with the mine?**
:   *"Robbery is what it is. The Silver-Bloods are trying to muscle in on my land. Forsworn attack the mines, and suddenly all these sellswords show up to 'help.' They won't let anyone work until I sell it off."*

You will then have two responses to choose from:

:   **What if I convince them to leave?**

    :   *"You can try, but I'd keep your sword-arm ready if things get ugly."*
:   **That's too bad.**

    :   *"You're telling me."*

:   **Who are the Silver-Bloods?**
:   *"A family of thieves. Running their corrupt empire from Markarth. The Silver-Blood family own half the Reach, and they won't stop until they own all of it."*

If you told Ainethach that you will help, you must now head inside Sanuarach Mine. You can either use persuasion to convince Atar and his men to leave, or use force to clear them from the mine. After, you can return to Ainethach and tell him that the sellswords won't be a problem now:

:   **Those sellswords won't be a problem now.**
:   *"That won't be the last we hear from the Silver-Bloods, but at least we can get back to work. Thank you. You've done a good thing for me and my workers. Here. This is for you."*

He will then give you your [reward](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanuarach_Mine_(quest)#Reward "Skyrim:Sanuarach Mine (quest)"), a leveled amount of gold.

Rather than helping Ainethach, you can aid Atar in persuading Ainethach to sell the mine instead. If you confront Ainethach and tell him that you think he should sell the mine:

:   **I think you should sell the mine.**
:   *"No. This is my land. You expect me to just hand it over to those Silver-Blood thugs?"*

You must then choose one of the following options to persuade him to sell his land:

| Option | Response |
| --- | --- |
| **They won't stop until you do. (Persuade)** | **Passed**: *"You're right. They always get what they want, somehow. Fine. Tell Atar I'll sell."*   **Failed**: *"Someone has to stand up to them. I won't sell."* |
| **Look. I'll give you a fair price. (Bribe)** | **Passed**: *"That's more gold than they're offering. Fine. I'll sell."*   **Failed**: *"This isn't about the money."* |
| **You do or you get hurt. (Intimidate)** | **Passed**: *"Easy. I'll sell. Just don't hurt anyone."* |
| **Forget it, then.** | *"Let's do that."* (no action is taken) |

Once you have persuaded him to sell the mine, you can return to Atar to tell him about your success. Atar will then proceed to give you your share of the cut, which is the same amount of leveled gold you receive if you help Ainethach.

### The Heart of Dibella

During [The Heart of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heart_of_Dibella "Skyrim:The Heart of Dibella"), if you tell him that you are looking for a [young girl](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjotra "Skyrim:Fjotra") that lives around here, he will reply by directing you to [Enmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Enmon "Skyrim:Enmon"):

:   **I'm looking for a young girl who lives around here.**
:   *"Oh, my. You'll want to talk to Enmon about that."*

## Rumors

The citizens of Karthwasten will often mention Ainethach in conversation. [Mena](/wiki/Skyrim:Mena "Skyrim:Mena") may direct you to Ainethach if you try to talk to her:

:   *"Ainethach's in charge of Karthwasten. You should bother him."*

Her husband Enmon will sometimes brush you off with a similar statement:

:   *"You should talk to Ainethach. He's in charge."*

Ragnar will often talk about his boss, saying:

:   *"I'm Ainethach's right-hand man. I help supervise the mines."*
:   *"Not many Nords would work for a Reachman, but Ainethach is a good man."*

If Ainethach dies, Ragnar will question the future of Karthwasten:

:   *"Ainethach is dead. What will happen to Karthwasten now?"*

Lash will also comment on his death:

:   *"Ainethach's dead, but that doesn't mean we can stop working."*

## Bugs

- Ainethach's dialogue at the end of the Sanuarach Mine quest does not exit with a goodbye flag.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.9, fixes this bug.

| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | No Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") | Aggressive |
| Voice Type | [MaleBrute](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleBrute "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleBrute") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [DLC2dunFrostmoonWerewolvesFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:DLC2dunFrostmoonWerewolvesFaction "Skyrim:DLC2dunFrostmoonWerewolvesFaction") | | |

Akar sitting on his bed

**Akar** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [werewolf](/wiki/Skyrim:EncClassWerewolf "Skyrim:EncClassWerewolf") living under [Frostmoon Crag](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostmoon_Crag "Skyrim:Frostmoon Crag"). He is a member of the Frostmoon Pack and brother to [Majni](/wiki/Skyrim:Majni "Skyrim:Majni"), the pack leader.

Akar wears [fur armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Armor "Skyrim:Fur Armor") with matching [bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Bracers "Skyrim:Fur Bracers") and [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Shoes "Skyrim:Fur Shoes"). He wields a leveled [weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons") in combat which can be up to [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven "Skyrim:Elven") in quality.

## Dialogue

When you approach him, he can greet you with:

:   *"Grr..."*
:   *"What?"*
:   *"Hmph."*

If spoken to directly:

:   **Who are you?**
:   *"Akar. Majni's brother. I hunt. He talks. Go talk to him."*
:   **You hunt? What do you hunt?**
:   *"[Deer](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer "Skyrim:Deer"). [Sabers](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabre_Cat "Skyrim:Sabre Cat"). [Rieks](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling "Skyrim:Riekling"). [Boar](/wiki/Skyrim:Bristleback "Skyrim:Bristleback"). [Bear](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear "Skyrim:Bear"). I hunt soon. Go bother Majni."*

# Skyrim:Alain Dufont

## Overview

| Alain Dufont (RefID: 000D2AFF) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Location | [Raldbthar](/wiki/Skyrim:Raldbthar "Skyrim:Raldbthar") | | |

Alain Dufont

**Alain Dufont** is a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") bandit leader residing in [Raldbthar](/wiki/Skyrim:Raldbthar "Skyrim:Raldbthar").

The previous lover of [Muiri](/wiki/Skyrim:Muiri "Skyrim:Muiri"), it turns out that he was only exploiting her and her friendship with the Shatter-Shield clan in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). He robbed the Shatter-Shields while they were vulnerable and mourning for their daughter's death, and fled, leaving Muiri behind to take the blame. Desperately wanting revenge for her ruined reputation and shattered friendship, Muiri [contacted](/wiki/Skyrim:Mourning_Never_Comes "Skyrim:Mourning Never Comes") the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") to end Alain's deceiving ways.

He wields a [frost](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Damage "Skyrim:Frost Damage")-enchanted [warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Warhammer "Skyrim:Warhammer") named [Aegisbane](/wiki/Skyrim:Aegisbane "Skyrim:Aegisbane") and wears [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000cee80 "Skyrim:Clothing") along with a pair of [fine boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000cee82 "Skyrim:Clothing").

As a target of a Dark Brotherhood assassination, Alain can be found either cooking or sitting in the main chamber of the Ruins of Raldbthar at any hour of the day; he will never be asleep during this time.

## Related Quests

- **[Mourning Never Comes](/wiki/Skyrim:Mourning_Never_Comes "Skyrim:Mourning Never Comes")**: Help [Muiri](/wiki/Skyrim:Muiri "Skyrim:Muiri") get her revenge.

### Mourning Never Comes

When he notices you in the room:

:   *"Well. You must have all those annoying gods on your side to have made it this far, whoever you are. Even I have to admit, that's pretty impressive."*

If you talk to Alain, you will be given only three dialogue options. Be aware that only one can be chosen as each ends the conversation:

| Your Options | Dialogue |
| --- | --- |
| **Muiri says goodbye. Forever.** | *"Muiri? Muiri? So, what, you're the cow's champion? Oh, now that is rich. Well then, champion, let's get this over with."* |
| **You will die as you lived. An arrogant joke.** | *"A joke? Alain Dufont... a joke? I am a king on my throne, and you, my friend... you will die slowly, and painfully."* |
| **(Remain silent)** | *"Ha! My opponent is so paralyzed with terror, no words will come. Let's be done with it, then!"* |

If you kill Alain before talking to Muiri first, she will be disappointed over how the transaction played out and will pay you anyway. You won't be able to gain her [bonus](/wiki/Skyrim:Muiri%27s_Ring "Skyrim:Muiri's Ring") for killing [Nilsine Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Nilsine_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:Nilsine Shatter-Shield"), though.

## Notes

- Alain was originally intended to act as an opponent in the [removed Windhelm arena](/wiki/Skyrim:Test_Cells#WindhelmPitWorldspace "Skyrim:Test Cells"), provided he hadn't already been killed. However, Alain just remains in Raldbthar since the arena was not implemented in the final game. There are still multiple leftovers that point to this in the final game:
  - Alain doesn't sandbox in Raldbthar, he's just stationary until he gets into combat. This is due to his default sandbox package being set to only be active when he's in the Windhelm Barracks cell. A place where he can never be found under normal circumstances. The Barracks were originally the Bloodworks, the underworks of the arena.
  - His class is still set to Prisoner.
  - At all times, a barrel in the cell area of the Windhelm Barracks holds the [Lotus Extract](/wiki/Skyrim:Lotus_Extract "Skyrim:Lotus Extract") poison, which Muiri normally only hands to you when she sends you on your way to kill Alain during the quest.
  - His taunting dialogue is internally still known as `DB03AlainPitTauntResponse`, the "Pit" portion there referring to "The Pit", the name of the arena.
  - His dialogue also wasn't changed from when he was a Pit opponent, in one line he calls you his "opponent", which was meant to be even more literal. The same goes for the "cow's champion" line. The line where he refers to how far you've come was also meant for a different context. Rather than your progress through the Dwarven ruin, Alain was referring to you surviving a multitude of previous arena fights.
- If you approach Alain or talk to him before the quest has been started, he will say *"I don't know how you got this far, but you'll go no farther"* and proceed to attack.
- Alain can be found in Raldbthar at all times before you need to deal with him the quest. If the quest hasn't yet been started, there is a chance that he won't turn hostile towards you. His guards, however, will always attack on sight.
- Although you can retrieve Aegisbane from Alain's corpse, you'll never get the option to properly return it to the Shatter-Shields.
- Originally, it seems that [Nilsine Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Nilsine_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:Nilsine Shatter-Shield") didn't play a role in the quest at all, or at least not a major one. Earlier dialogue for Muiri in the Creation Kit confirms that instead of killing Nilsine, the optional quest objective was to kill Alain during a Pit match, while the normal objective was to just kill him.
- [Unused NPC](/wiki/Skyrim:Unused_NPCs "Skyrim:Unused NPCs") [Huki Seven-Swords](/wiki/Skyrim:Huki_Seven-Swords "Skyrim:Huki Seven-Swords") still has dialogue referring to him in his original role.
- After his death, Windhelm guards may comment as you pass, *"Hey! You're the one who killed Alain Dufont, up in Raldbthar. Oh yeah, word about that got around. Man was a piece of bandit trash, is what I hear."*
  - They might also refer to him if they see you carrying Aegisbane, saying *"That hammer... Why that's Aegisbane, heirloom of Clan Shatter-Shield! Last I heard, it was stolen by a couple of swindlers. Alain and... Muiri. Yeah."*

## Bugs

- During Mourning Never Comes, Alain Dufont's initial dialogue cuts off before you are allowed to give a response and he enters combat before he's supposed to.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.7, addresses this issue. It was incorrectly set as a goodbye response, and the script never should have been added to it.

# Skyrim:Alchemist's Shack

## Overview

| Special Features | |

Alchemist's Shack

The **Alchemist's Shack** is a small [shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Shacks "Skyrim:Shacks") south of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead").

## Related Quests

- **[Pets of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Pets_of_Skyrim_(quest) "Skyrim:Pets of Skyrim (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Pets_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Pets of Skyrim"): Find trained pets around Skyrim.

## Walkthrough

The shack is a dilapidated single-story building with its doors and windows missing. It can be seen from the road between [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") and [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead"). There is a wattle-fenced garden to the rear, with an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs") to the right of the rear doorway. A barrel containing random ingredients is between the shack and the lab, with two samples of [hawk feathers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hawk_Feathers "Skyrim:Hawk Feathers") and a [red mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower") on top. A [blue mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"), three [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell"), three [jazbay grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes"), a [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade"), two [scaly pholiota](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaly_Pholiota "Skyrim:Scaly Pholiota"), and two [spiky grass](/wiki/Skyrim:Grass_Pod "Skyrim:Grass Pod") grow in the garden, and a [birds' nest](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg") is in front to the west. This is a good area to find [blue butterflies](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Butterfly "Skyrim:Blue Butterfly") and [butterflies](/wiki/Skyrim:Butterfly "Skyrim:Butterfly") during the day and [luna moths](/wiki/Skyrim:Luna_Moth "Skyrim:Luna Moth") at night.

With the [Pets of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Pets_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Pets of Skyrim") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creations "Skyrim:Creations") installed, the rabbit [Thistle](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_(creature) "Skyrim:Thistle (creature)") can be found in the garden and can be tamed with carrots.

The shack's interior

As you enter through the front doorway you will find two shelving units; the one on your right contains a [Potion of Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions#Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potions"), two books, and some clutter. The shelving unit in front of you contains a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), a sample of [glow dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Glow_Dust "Skyrim:Glow Dust"), two [carrots](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot"), three [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"), and a [butterfly in a jar](/wiki/Skyrim:Butterfly_in_a_Jar "Skyrim:Butterfly in a Jar"). The jar can only be found in this shack and respawns with the rest of the shack. Between the two shelving units is a barrel containing [uncommon ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") and a basket containing two [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"). To your left as you enter is a bed (unowned). Next to this is an end table holding an [alchemist's journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemist%27s_Journal_(shack) "Skyrim:Alchemist's Journal (shack)") and an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel") containing [common ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"). This end table does not respawn, and can be useful as a storage option. To the right of the rear exit is a bucket containing a sample of [blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort") and hanging above are a [garlic braid](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") and a sample of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam").

## Notes

- The items will respawn over time, except for the end table beside the bed.
- Two [wolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf "Skyrim:Wolf") often spawn on the road shortly before the shack, as well as some [goats](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat "Skyrim:Goat") further up the road from Helgen, who often attract the attention of the wolves. Up the mountain to the left of the shack is a trail which is full of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberry "Skyrim:Snowberry") and an Iron Ore vein. Be careful up the mountain pass, as a [Snow Bear](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear "Skyrim:Bear") makes its home there, regardless of your character level. This is the only place a Snow Bear will always spawn.

A dead alchemist at Evergreen Grove

**Alchemists** are dead [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") [conjurers](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjurer_(class) "Skyrim:Conjurer (class)") found throughout Skyrim. They all wear [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots") and [Black Mage Robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Black Mage Robes"). They all carry a [nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot"), a rare [ingredient](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"), and a leveled [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger"). There is one in a cell in [Fort Greenwall](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Greenwall "Skyrim:Fort Greenwall"), one in a hanging cage outside of [Fort Dunstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dunstad "Skyrim:Fort Dunstad"), one at the giant camp [Cradlecrush Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Cradlecrush_Rock "Skyrim:Cradlecrush Rock"), one on a rock in a river near [Talking Stone Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Talking_Stone_Camp "Skyrim:Talking Stone Camp"), and one on a sunken altar at [Evergreen Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Evergreen_Grove "Skyrim:Evergreen Grove"). They can be a good source of ingredients in the beginning of the game.

The dead female alchemist in Clearpine Pond

This **Alchemist** is a [High Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf") [conjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjurer_(class) "Skyrim:Conjurer (class)") found at [Clearpine Pond](/wiki/Skyrim:Clearpine_Pond "Skyrim:Clearpine Pond") up against a fallen tree. She wears [black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Black Mage Robes") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000c5d12 "Skyrim:Boots"). She carries a [nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot"), a [rare ingredient](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"), a leveled [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger"), and a copy of the [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[De Rerum Dirennis](/wiki/Skyrim:De_Rerum_Dirennis "Skyrim:De Rerum Dirennis")*. Beside her is an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel") containing one common, uncommon, and rare ingredients each, with a 25% chance of containing one random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), [of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), or [of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"). There are also two [taproots](/wiki/Skyrim:Taproot "Skyrim:Taproot") and a [blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort") found beside her, along with an empty [flower basket](/wiki/Skyrim:Flower_Basket "Skyrim:Flower Basket").

## Notes

- One more alchemist (see BaseID 00099805 above) is found in [Volkihar Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Keep "Skyrim:Volkihar Keep") after [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") is installed, on a table in [Ronthil's](/wiki/Skyrim:Ronthil "Skyrim:Ronthil") quarters.
- Strangely, both types of Alchemists know the spells [Conjure Familiar](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Familiar "Skyrim:Conjure Familiar"), [Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Flames "Skyrim:Flames"), [Oakflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Oakflesh "Skyrim:Oakflesh"), and [Lesser Ward](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Ward "Skyrim:Lesser Ward"), even though they are dead and cannot use them.

| Level | 1 | Class | [Conjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjurer "Skyrim:Conjurer") |

| Respawns | Yes | | |

A dead alchemist found in the Altar of Thrond

Three **alchemists** can be found dead in Solstheim.

|  |
| --- |
| - One is found inside the [Altar of Thrond Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Altar_of_Thrond "Skyrim:Altar of Thrond"). - The second is found at the [Wreck of the Strident Squall](/wiki/Skyrim:Wreck_of_the_Strident_Squall "Skyrim:Wreck of the Strident Squall") on the lowest level, the stairs to which are partially concealed underwater. - The third is lying facedown on an [unmarked island](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places#Giant_Nirnroot_Island "Skyrim:Unmarked Places") with giant [nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot") plants in the far northeast part of the game map (north of [Frossel](/wiki/Skyrim:Frossel "Skyrim:Frossel")). |

All three alchemists wear leveled, enchanted robes; from level 1-7, it will be [black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Black Mage Robes"). From level 8 and up, the enchantments will match your level, and will fortify either [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction"), [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration"), or [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration"). From level 10, there is also a 25% chance the robes will have a [regenerate magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Regenerate_Magicka "Skyrim:Regenerate Magicka") enchantment. Lastly, all of them wear the same type of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000c5d12 "Skyrim:Boots").

They all carry a sample of nirnroot, some random, rare [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"), and a leveled [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") (up to glass quality at level 18).
