# Skyrim:Alchemy Labs

## Overview

This article is about alchemy labs used to make potions and poisons. For the player-built home addition related to the Hearthfire add-on, see [Alchemy Laboratory](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Laboratory "Skyrim:Alchemy Laboratory").

An Alchemy Lab

**Alchemy Labs** are places where it is possible to perform [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy"). A category listing all places where alchemy labs can be found is available at [Category:Skyrim-Places-Alchemy Labs](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Alchemy_Labs "Category:Skyrim-Places-Alchemy Labs").

### Eastmarch

-  **[Ansilvund Excavation](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund_Excavation "Skyrim:Ansilvund Excavation")** — A medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") north of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") and [necromancers](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") led by [Lu'ah Al-Skaven](/wiki/Skyrim:Lu%27ah_Al-Skaven "Skyrim:Lu'ah Al-Skaven"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ansilvund)
-  **[Cragwallow Slope](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragwallow_Slope "Skyrim:Cragwallow Slope")** — A medium-sized [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southeast of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") home to [conjurers](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjurer "Skyrim:Conjurer") and [atronachs](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach "Skyrim:Atronach"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Cragwallow+Slope)
-  **[Cronvangr Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Cronvangr_Cave "Skyrim:Cronvangr Cave")** — A medium-sized [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southwest of [Kynesgrove](/wiki/Skyrim:Kynesgrove "Skyrim:Kynesgrove") containing [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") and [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Cronvangr+Cave)
-  **[Eastmarch Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Eastmarch Imperial Camp")** — An [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Camps "Skyrim:Imperial Camps") in [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch"), located southeast of [Mzulft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzulft "Skyrim:Mzulft") and north of [Stony Creek Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Stony_Creek_Cave "Skyrim:Stony Creek Cave"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Eastmarch+Imperial+Camp)
-  **[Fort Amol](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Amol "Skyrim:Fort Amol")** — A medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") southwest of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") initially occupied by [warlocks](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock "Skyrim:Warlock"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Amol)
-  **[Mistwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch "Skyrim:Mistwatch")** — A medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") east of [Darkwater Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Crossing "Skyrim:Darkwater Crossing") containing the [Mistwatch Bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch_Bandit "Skyrim:Mistwatch Bandit") and their [leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Leader "Skyrim:Bandit Leader"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mistwatch)
-  **[Mzulft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzulft "Skyrim:Mzulft")** — A large [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") south-southeast of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") containing [Dwarven automatons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Automatons "Skyrim:Dwarven Automatons"), [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"), and [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mzulft)
-  **[Narzulbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Narzulbur "Skyrim:Narzulbur")** — An [Orc stronghold](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Strongholds "Skyrim:Orc Strongholds") in the east of [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"), southeast of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Narzulbur)
-  **[Palace of the Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:Palace_of_the_Kings "Skyrim:Palace of the Kings")** — A large [castle](/wiki/Skyrim:Castles "Skyrim:Castles") at the far end of the Valunstrad district in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Palace+of+the+Kings)
-  **[Sacellum of Boethiah](/wiki/Skyrim:Sacellum_of_Boethiah "Skyrim:Sacellum of Boethiah")** — The [shrine](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Shrines "Skyrim:Daedric Shrines") to the [Daedric Prince](/wiki/Lore:Daedric_Princes "Lore:Daedric Princes") [Boethiah](/wiki/Lore:Boethiah "Lore:Boethiah"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sacellum+of+Boethiah)
-  **[Snapleg Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Snapleg_Cave "Skyrim:Snapleg Cave")** — A medium-sized [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") northwest of [Rift Watchtower](/wiki/Skyrim:Rift_Watchtower "Skyrim:Rift Watchtower") occupied by [hags](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag "Skyrim:Hag") and [monsters](/wiki/Skyrim:Monsters "Skyrim:Monsters"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Snapleg+Cave)
-  **[Stony Creek Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Stony_Creek_Cave "Skyrim:Stony Creek Cave")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southeast of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Stony+Creek+Cave)
-  **[Uttering Hills Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Uttering_Hills_Cave "Skyrim:Uttering Hills Cave")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southwest of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Uttering+Hills+Cave)
- **[The White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(place) "Skyrim:The White Phial (place)")** — The alchemical shop located on the north side of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm")'s market district. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+White+Phial)

### Falkreath

-  **[Anise's Cabin](/wiki/Skyrim:Anise%27s_Cabin "Skyrim:Anise's Cabin")** — A small [shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Shacks "Skyrim:Shacks") west-southwest of [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Anise%27s+Cabin)
-  **[Bloodlet Throne](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodlet_Throne "Skyrim:Bloodlet Throne")** — A small [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") southwest of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") containing [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"), [wolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf "Skyrim:Wolf"), [gargoyles](/wiki/Skyrim:Gargoyle "Skyrim:Gargoyle"), and [death hounds](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_Hound "Skyrim:Death Hound"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bloodlet+Throne)
-  **[Cracked Tusk Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Cracked_Tusk_Keep "Skyrim:Cracked Tusk Keep")** — A medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") west of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") containing [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") and [hunters](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Hunter "Skyrim:Orc Hunter") led by [Ghunzul](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghunzul "Skyrim:Ghunzul"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Cracked+Tusk+Keep)
-  **[Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary")** — An active [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") sanctuary west of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dark+Brotherhood+Sanctuary)
- **[Dead Man's Drink](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Drink "Skyrim:Dead Man's Drink")** — An [inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Inns "Skyrim:Inns") in the town of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"). It is owned by [Valga Vinicia](/wiki/Skyrim:Valga_Vinicia "Skyrim:Valga Vinicia"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dead+Man%27s+Drink)
-  **[Falkreath Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Falkreath Stormcloak Camp")** — A [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Camps "Skyrim:Stormcloak Camps") in [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold"), located east of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Falkreath+Stormcloak+Camp)
- **[Grave Concoctions](/wiki/Skyrim:Grave_Concoctions "Skyrim:Grave Concoctions")** — A store in [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") specializing in [alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") and home for [Zaria](/wiki/Skyrim:Zaria "Skyrim:Zaria") who runs the store. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Grave+Concoctions)
-  **[Haemar's Shame](/wiki/Skyrim:Haemar%27s_Shame "Skyrim:Haemar's Shame")** — A medium-sized [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") east of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") containing [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Haemar%27s+Shame)
-  **[Hag Rock Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag_Rock_Redoubt "Skyrim:Hag Rock Redoubt")** — A small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") south of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") containing [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hag+Rock+Redoubt)
-  **[Ilinalta's Deep](/wiki/Skyrim:Ilinalta%27s_Deep "Skyrim:Ilinalta's Deep")** — A medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") north of the [Lady Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lady_Stone "Skyrim:The Lady Stone") containing [necromancers](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ilinalta%27s+Deep)
-  **[Knifepoint Ridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Knifepoint_Ridge "Skyrim:Knifepoint Ridge")** — A small [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Camps "Skyrim:Camps") and [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron "Skyrim:Iron") and [corundum](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum "Skyrim:Corundum") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") northwest of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Knifepoint+Ridge)
-  **[Southfringe Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Southfringe_Sanctum "Skyrim:Southfringe Sanctum")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southeast of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") containing the conjurer [Bashnag](/wiki/Skyrim:Bashnag "Skyrim:Bashnag") and his [coven](/wiki/Skyrim:Spellsword_(NPC) "Skyrim:Spellsword (NPC)"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Southfringe+Sanctum)
-  **[Sunderstone Gorge](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunderstone_Gorge "Skyrim:Sunderstone Gorge")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") north-northwest of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") containing [warlocks](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock "Skyrim:Warlock") and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sunderstone+Gorge)
-  **[Twilight Sepulcher](/wiki/Skyrim:Twilight_Sepulcher "Skyrim:Twilight Sepulcher")** — The location of the Pilgrim's Path and main entrance to [Nocturnal's](/wiki/Skyrim:Nocturnal "Skyrim:Nocturnal") Ebonmere portal, resting place for the [Skeleton Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton_Key "Skyrim:Skeleton Key"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Twilight+Sepulcher)

### Haafingar

- **[Angeline's Aromatics](/wiki/Skyrim:Angeline%27s_Aromatics "Skyrim:Angeline's Aromatics")** — The [alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") shop in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Angeline%27s+Aromatics)
- **[Castle Dour](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour")** — A large [fortress](/wiki/Skyrim:Castles "Skyrim:Castles") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") which acts as the headquarters of the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") and residence of the [Emperor](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II_(real) "Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (real)") in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Castle+Dour)
- **[Darkfall Passage](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkfall_Passage "Skyrim:Darkfall Passage")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A small cave only accessible through [Darkfall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkfall_Cave "Skyrim:Darkfall Cave") serving as the only access to the [Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale").
-  **[Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — An isolated region in northwestern Skyrim once inhabited by the [Snow Elves](/wiki/Lore:Snow_Elf "Lore:Snow Elf") worshipping the god [Auri-El](/wiki/Lore:Auri-El "Lore:Auri-El"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Forgotten+Vale+%28DG%29)
-  **[Haafingar Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Haafingar Stormcloak Camp")** — A [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Camps "Skyrim:Stormcloak Camps") in [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar"), located northeast of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") and south of the [Statue to Meridia](/wiki/Skyrim:Statue_to_Meridia "Skyrim:Statue to Meridia"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Haafingar+Stormcloak+Camp)
-  **[The Katariah](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Katariah "Skyrim:The Katariah")** — The personal transport vessel of the Emperor, [Titus Mede II](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II_(real) "Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (real)"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Katariah)
- **[Potema's Catacombs](/wiki/Skyrim:Potema%27s_Catacombs "Skyrim:Potema's Catacombs")** — A series of catacombs designed to house the [Wolf Queen](/wiki/Skyrim:Queen_Potema "Skyrim:Queen Potema") of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Temple+of+the+Divines)
-  **[Volkihar Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Keep "Skyrim:Volkihar Keep")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A large [fortress](/wiki/Skyrim:Castles "Skyrim:Castles") on an island far northwest of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") connected to [Castle Volkihar](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Volkihar "Skyrim:Castle Volkihar") which serves as the [Volkihar vampire clan](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Vampire_Clan "Skyrim:Volkihar Vampire Clan")'s home. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Castle+Volkihar+%28DG%29)

### Hjaalmarch

-  **[Fort Snowhawk](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Snowhawk "Skyrim:Fort Snowhawk")** — A medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") west of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") initially occupied by [necromancers](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Snowhawk)
-  **[Hjaalmarch Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch Stormcloak Camp")** — A [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Camps "Skyrim:Stormcloak Camps") in [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch"), located east of [Ustengrav](/wiki/Skyrim:Ustengrav "Skyrim:Ustengrav") and west of [Mzinchaleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzinchaleft "Skyrim:Mzinchaleft"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hjaalmarch+Stormcloak+Camp)
-  **[Labyrinthian](/wiki/Skyrim:Labyrinthian "Skyrim:Labyrinthian")** — A large [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") southeast of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"), [trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll "Skyrim:Troll"), [wisps](/wiki/Skyrim:Wisp "Skyrim:Wisp"), and the [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") [Morokei](/wiki/Skyrim:Morokei_(creature) "Skyrim:Morokei (creature)"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Labyrinthian)
-  **[Lost Valkygg](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Valkygg "Skyrim:Lost Valkygg")** — A small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Dwellings "Skyrim:Nordic Dwellings") northeast of [Labyrinthian](/wiki/Skyrim:Labyrinthian "Skyrim:Labyrinthian") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lost+Valkygg)
-  **[Movarth's Lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Movarth%27s_Lair "Skyrim:Movarth's Lair")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") north-northeast of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") containing [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") led by [Movarth Piquine](/wiki/Skyrim:Movarth_Piquine "Skyrim:Movarth Piquine"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Movarth%27s+Lair)
- **[Thaumaturgist's Hut](/wiki/Skyrim:Thaumaturgist%27s_Hut "Skyrim:Thaumaturgist's Hut")** — An [alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") shop in [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Thaumaturgist%27s+Hut)

### The Pale

-  **[Dawnstar Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dawnstar Sanctuary")** — A disused [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") sanctuary on the shore of the [Sea of Ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Sea_of_Ghosts "Skyrim:Sea of Ghosts") near [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dawnstar+Sanctuary)
-  **[Forsaken Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsaken_Cave "Skyrim:Forsaken Cave")** — A medium-sized [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") west of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") and leveled [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Forsaken+Cave)
-  **[Fort Dunstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dunstad "Skyrim:Fort Dunstad")** — A large [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") south of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") initially occupied by [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Dunstad)
-  **[Hall of the Vigilant](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Vigilant "Skyrim:Hall of the Vigilant")** — A secluded [lodge](/wiki/Skyrim:Shacks "Skyrim:Shacks") south-southwest of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"), home to the [Vigilants of Stendarr](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigilants_of_Stendarr "Skyrim:Vigilants of Stendarr"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hall+of+the+Vigilant)
-  **[Irkngthand](/wiki/Skyrim:Irkngthand "Skyrim:Irkngthand")** — A large [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") west of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"), [Dwarven automatons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Automatons "Skyrim:Dwarven Automatons"), [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"), [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), and [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Irkngthand)
- **[The Mortar and Pestle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mortar_and_Pestle "Skyrim:The Mortar and Pestle")** — The alchemy shop in [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"), between [Brina's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Brina%27s_House "Skyrim:Brina's House") and [Beitild's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Beitild%27s_House "Skyrim:Beitild's House"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Mortar+and+Pestle)
-  **[Nightcaller Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightcaller_Temple "Skyrim:Nightcaller Temple")** — A small [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") on the clifftop overlooking [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Nightcaller+Temple)
-  **[Pale Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Pale_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Pale Imperial Camp")** — An [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Camps "Skyrim:Imperial Camps") in [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale"), located west of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") and northwest of [Mzinchaleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzinchaleft "Skyrim:Mzinchaleft"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Pale+Imperial+Camp)

### The Reach

-  **[Blind Cliff Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Blind_Cliff_Cave "Skyrim:Blind Cliff Cave")** — A medium-sized [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southwest of [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten") along the banks of the [Karth River](/wiki/Skyrim:Karth_River "Skyrim:Karth River") containing [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Blind+Cliff+Cave)
- **[Burguk's Longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Burguk%27s_Longhouse "Skyrim:Burguk's Longhouse")** — The longhouse of [Chief Burguk](/wiki/Skyrim:Chief_Burguk "Skyrim:Chief Burguk"), located in the Orc stronghold of [Dushnikh Yal](/wiki/Skyrim:Dushnikh_Yal "Skyrim:Dushnikh Yal"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Burguk%27s+Longhouse)
-  **[Darkfall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkfall_Cave "Skyrim:Darkfall Cave")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") south of [Mor Khazgur](/wiki/Skyrim:Mor_Khazgur "Skyrim:Mor Khazgur") containing [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider") and [trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll "Skyrim:Troll"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Darkfall+Cave+%28DG%29)
-  **[Deepwood Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Deepwood_Vale "Skyrim:Deepwood Vale")** — A large [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") west of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") containing [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Deepwood+Redoubt)
-  **[Dushnikh Yal](/wiki/Skyrim:Dushnikh_Yal "Skyrim:Dushnikh Yal")** — A prosperous [Orc stronghold](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Strongholds "Skyrim:Orc Strongholds") in the southwest of [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"), southeast of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dushnikh+Yal)
-  **[Fort Sungard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Sungard "Skyrim:Fort Sungard")** — A large [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") east-southeast of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") initially occupied by [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Sungard)
- **[The Hag's Cure](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Hag%27s_Cure "Skyrim:The Hag's Cure")** — An apothecary in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") owned and operated by [Bothela](/wiki/Skyrim:Bothela "Skyrim:Bothela"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Hag%27s+Cure)
-  **[Hag's End](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag%27s_End "Skyrim:Hag's End")** — A small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") west of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") containing a [hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven"), [hags](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag "Skyrim:Hag"), and [witches](/wiki/Skyrim:Witch "Skyrim:Witch"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hag%27s+End)
-  **[Hag Rock Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag_Rock_Redoubt "Skyrim:Hag Rock Redoubt")** — A small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") south of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") containing [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hag+Rock+Redoubt)
-  **[Harmugstahl](/wiki/Skyrim:Harmugstahl "Skyrim:Harmugstahl")** — A small [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") north of [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten") containing the warlock [Kornalus](/wiki/Skyrim:Kornalus "Skyrim:Kornalus") and his enchanted [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Harmugstahl)
-  **[Karthspire Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthspire_Camp "Skyrim:Karthspire Camp")** — A large [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Camps "Skyrim:Camps") and cave east of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Karthspire)
-  **[Mor Khazgur](/wiki/Skyrim:Mor_Khazgur "Skyrim:Mor Khazgur")** — An [Orc stronghold](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Strongholds "Skyrim:Orc Strongholds") in the far northwest of [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"), west of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") and north of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mor+Khazgur)
-  **[Reach Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Reach_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Reach Stormcloak Camp")** — A [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Camps "Skyrim:Stormcloak Camps") in [the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach"), located west of [Liar's Retreat](/wiki/Skyrim:Liar%27s_Retreat "Skyrim:Liar's Retreat") and northeast of [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Reach+Stormcloak+Camp)
-  **[Shrine to Peryite](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_to_Peryite "Skyrim:Shrine to Peryite")** — The [shrine](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Shrines "Skyrim:Daedric Shrines") to the [Daedric Prince](/wiki/Lore:Daedric_Princes "Lore:Daedric Princes") [Peryite](/wiki/Lore:Peryite "Lore:Peryite"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Shrine+to+Peryite)
-  **[Sundered Towers](/wiki/Skyrim:Sundered_Towers "Skyrim:Sundered Towers")** — A small pair of linked ruined [Nordic towers](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Towers "Skyrim:Nordic Towers") southeast of [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten") containing [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") and [hagravens](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sundered+Towers)
-  **[Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep")** — An ancient Dwarven keep built into the mountainside, used as a palace by the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Understone+Keep)
-  **[Valthume](/wiki/Skyrim:Valthume "Skyrim:Valthume")** — A medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") southeast of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"), and the [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") [Hevnoraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Hevnoraak_(creature) "Skyrim:Hevnoraak (creature)"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Valthume)

### The Rift

-  **[Alchemist's Shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemist%27s_Shack "Skyrim:Alchemist's Shack")** — A small [shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Shacks "Skyrim:Shacks") south of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Alchemist%27s+Shack)
-  **[Avanchnzel](/wiki/Skyrim:Avanchnzel "Skyrim:Avanchnzel")** — A medium-sized [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") west of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") containing [Dwarven automatons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Automatons "Skyrim:Dwarven Automatons"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Avanchnzel)
- **[Black-Briar Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Manor "Skyrim:Black-Briar Manor")** — The Black-Briars' residence in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Black-Briar+Manor)
-  **[Boulderfall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Boulderfall_Cave "Skyrim:Boulderfall Cave")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") northwest of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") containing [necromancers](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Boulderfall+Cave)
-  **[Darklight Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Darklight_Tower "Skyrim:Darklight Tower")** — A medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") southwest of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") containing [hagravens](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven"), [hags](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag "Skyrim:Hag"), and [witches](/wiki/Skyrim:Witch "Skyrim:Witch"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Darklight+Tower)
- **[Elgrim's Elixirs](/wiki/Skyrim:Elgrim%27s_Elixirs "Skyrim:Elgrim's Elixirs")** — A damp alchemist's shop located on the lower level, by the canal that flows through the center of the city of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). Owned and run by [Elgrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Elgrim "Skyrim:Elgrim") and his wife [Hafjorg](/wiki/Skyrim:Hafjorg "Skyrim:Hafjorg"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Elgrim%27s+Elixirs)
-  **[Forelhost](/wiki/Skyrim:Forelhost "Skyrim:Forelhost")** — A medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") southeast of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") containing [Dragon Cultists](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Cultist "Skyrim:Dragon Cultist"), [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"), and the [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") [Rahgot](/wiki/Skyrim:Rahgot_(creature) "Skyrim:Rahgot (creature)"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Forelhost)
-  **[Fort Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Fort Dawnguard")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A large [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") southeast of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") which serves as the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)")'s base of operations. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Dawnguard+%28DG%29)
-  **[Largashbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur "Skyrim:Largashbur")** — An accursed [Orc stronghold](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Strongholds "Skyrim:Orc Strongholds") beset by [giants](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") in the southeast of [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"), west-southwest of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Largashbur)
-  **[Mistveil Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistveil_Keep "Skyrim:Mistveil Keep")** — A castle located at the southern end of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mistveil+Keep)
- **[The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon")** — A [tavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Inns "Skyrim:Inns") that is part of the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)")'s headquarters. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Ratway)
- **[The Ratway](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ratway "Skyrim:The Ratway")** — A network of sewer tunnels running beneath [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"), and home to the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Ratway)
-  **[Redwater Den](/wiki/Skyrim:Redwater_Den "Skyrim:Redwater Den")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A [shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Shacks "Skyrim:Shacks") northwest of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") and [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Redwater+Den+%28DG%29)
-  **[Rift Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Rift_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Rift Imperial Camp")** — An [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Camps "Skyrim:Imperial Camps") in [the Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift"), located south of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") and west of the [Ruins of Bthalft](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruins_of_Bthalft "Skyrim:Ruins of Bthalft"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Rift+Imperial+Camp)
-  **[Sarethi Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Sarethi_Farm "Skyrim:Sarethi Farm")** — A farm east of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") that cultivates [Nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sarethi+Farm)
-  **[Shroud Hearth Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Shroud_Hearth_Barrow "Skyrim:Shroud Hearth Barrow")** — A medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") east of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Shroud+Hearth+Barrow)
-  **[Tolvald's Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolvald%27s_Cave "Skyrim:Tolvald's Cave")** — A large [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") northeast of [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone") containing [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"), [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"), [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), and [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Tolvald%27s+Cave)

### Solstheim DB

-  **[Altar of Thrond](/wiki/Skyrim:Altar_of_Thrond "Skyrim:Altar of Thrond")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A [landmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Landmarks "Skyrim:Landmarks") west of the [Temple of Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:Temple of Miraak") next to a small cave containing [hagravens](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Altar+of+Thrond)
-  **[Ashfall's Tear](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashfall%27s_Tear "Skyrim:Ashfall's Tear")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal") — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") north of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") containing a hidden [Tribunal Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Tribunal_Temple "Skyrim:Tribunal Temple") shrine to the goddess [Almalexia](/wiki/Lore:Almalexia "Lore:Almalexia"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Ashfall%27s+Tear+%28CC%29)
-  **[Ashfallow Citadel](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashfallow_Citadel "Skyrim:Ashfallow Citadel")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small Imperial [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") east of [Highpoint Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Highpoint_Tower "Skyrim:Highpoint Tower") and northwest of the [Sun Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Sun_Stone "Skyrim:Sun Stone") being used as a base of operations by the [Morag Tong](/wiki/Skyrim:Morag_Tong "Skyrim:Morag Tong"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Ashfallow+Citadel)
-  **[Bloodskal Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodskal_Barrow "Skyrim:Bloodskal Barrow")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") north of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") containing [reavers](/wiki/Skyrim:Reaver "Skyrim:Reaver"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Bloodskal+Barrow)
-  **[Damphall Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Damphall_Mine "Skyrim:Damphall Mine")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron "Skyrim:Iron") and [silver](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver "Skyrim:Silver") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") north of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") containing [reavers](/wiki/Skyrim:Reaver "Skyrim:Reaver"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Damphall+Mine)
- **[Edla's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Edla%27s_House "Skyrim:Edla's House")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — The home of [Edla](/wiki/Skyrim:Edla "Skyrim:Edla") and her son [Nikulas](/wiki/Skyrim:Nikulas_(Dragonborn) "Skyrim:Nikulas (Dragonborn)") in [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Edla%27s+House)
-  **[Highpoint Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Highpoint_Tower "Skyrim:Highpoint Tower")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") east of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") containing [albino spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Albino_Spider "Skyrim:Albino Spider"), [ash spawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Spawn "Skyrim:Ash Spawn"), and [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth")'s former apprentice [Ildari Sarothril](/wiki/Skyrim:Ildari_Sarothril "Skyrim:Ildari Sarothril"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Highpoint+Tower)
- **[Ienth Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ienth_Farm "Skyrim:Ienth Farm")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — The home of [Garyn Ienth](/wiki/Skyrim:Garyn_Ienth "Skyrim:Garyn Ienth") and [Milore Ienth](/wiki/Skyrim:Milore_Ienth "Skyrim:Milore Ienth") in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Ienth+Farm)
-  **[Raven Rock Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock_Mine "Skyrim:Raven Rock Mine")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small [ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony "Skyrim:Ebony") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") in northern [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") initially containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"), and the [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") [Zahkriisos](/wiki/Skyrim:Zahkriisos_(creature) "Skyrim:Zahkriisos (creature)"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Raven+Rock+Mine)
- **[Shaman's Hut](/wiki/Skyrim:Shaman%27s_Hut "Skyrim:Shaman's Hut")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — The home of shaman [Storn Crag-Strider](/wiki/Skyrim:Storn_Crag-Strider "Skyrim:Storn Crag-Strider") and his daughter [Frea](/wiki/Skyrim:Frea "Skyrim:Frea") in [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Shaman%27s+Hut)
- **[Tel Mithryn Apothecary](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_Apothecary "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn Apothecary")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — The home of the apothecary [Elynea Mothren](/wiki/Skyrim:Elynea_Mothren "Skyrim:Elynea Mothren") in [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(settlement) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (settlement)"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Tel+Mithryn+Apothecary)
-  **[Temple of Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:Temple of Miraak")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A [Nordic temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Temples "Skyrim:Temples") west of [Thirsk Mead Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Thirsk_Mead_Hall "Skyrim:Thirsk Mead Hall") containing [cultists](/wiki/Skyrim:Cultist "Skyrim:Cultist"), [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Temple+of+Miraak)

### Whiterun Hold

- **[Arcadia's Cauldron](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcadia%27s_Cauldron "Skyrim:Arcadia's Cauldron")** — An [alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") shop in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun")'s market area. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Arcadia%27s+Cauldron)
-  **[Broken Fang Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Fang_Cave "Skyrim:Broken Fang Cave")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southeast of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead") containing [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") and [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Broken+Fang+Cave)
-  **[Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach")** — The residence of the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold"), the hold's seat of political power, and the location of the hold's jail. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dragonsreach)
-  **[Drelas' Cottage](/wiki/Skyrim:Drelas%27_Cottage "Skyrim:Drelas' Cottage")** — An isolated [cottage](/wiki/Skyrim:Shacks "Skyrim:Shacks") at the foot of a mountain in northern [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold"), and south of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Drelas%27+Cottage)
-  **[Dustman's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dustman%27s_Cairn "Skyrim:Dustman's Cairn")** — A medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") northwest of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") containing [Silver Hands](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Hand "Skyrim:Silver Hand"), [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), and [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dustman%27s+Cairn)
-  **[Fellglow Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellglow_Keep "Skyrim:Fellglow Keep")** — A medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") east-northeast of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") containing [warlocks](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock "Skyrim:Warlock"), [atronachs](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach "Skyrim:Atronach"), and [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"), and the mages' leader, [the Caller](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Caller "Skyrim:The Caller"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fellglow+Keep)
-  **[Honningbrew Meadery](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Meadery "Skyrim:Honningbrew Meadery")** — A small [meadery](/wiki/Skyrim:Settlements "Skyrim:Settlements") southeast of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") owned by [Sabjorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabjorn "Skyrim:Sabjorn"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Honningbrew+Meadery)
-  **[Rannveig's Fast](/wiki/Skyrim:Rannveig%27s_Fast "Skyrim:Rannveig's Fast")** — A small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") east-northeast of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead") containing [subjugated ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Subjugated_Ghost "Skyrim:Subjugated Ghost") and [Sild the Warlock](/wiki/Skyrim:Sild_the_Warlock "Skyrim:Sild the Warlock"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Rannveig%27s+Fast)
- **[Sleeping Giant Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping_Giant_Inn "Skyrim:Sleeping Giant Inn")** — A small [inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Inns "Skyrim:Inns") and tavern in the town of [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sleeping+Giant+Inn)
-  **[Valtheim Towers](/wiki/Skyrim:Valtheim_Towers "Skyrim:Valtheim Towers")** — A small pair of linked ruined [Nordic towers](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Towers "Skyrim:Nordic Towers") east of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Valtheim+Towers)
-  **[White River Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River_Watch "Skyrim:White River Watch")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") east-southeast of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") containing the [White River](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River "Skyrim:White River") [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=White+River+Watch)
-  **[Whiterun Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Whiterun Stormcloak Camp")** — A [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Camps "Skyrim:Stormcloak Camps") in [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold"), located south of the [Ritual Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ritual_Stone "Skyrim:The Ritual Stone") and east of [White River Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River_Watch "Skyrim:White River Watch"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Whiterun+Stormcloak+Camp)

### Winterhold

-  **[Alftand](/wiki/Skyrim:Alftand "Skyrim:Alftand")** — A large [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") southwest of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") containing [Dwarven automatons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Automatons "Skyrim:Dwarven Automatons"), [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"), [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), and [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Alftand)
- **[Arch-Mage's Quarters](/wiki/Skyrim:Arch-Mage%27s_Quarters "Skyrim:Arch-Mage's Quarters")** — The area within the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") in which its current Arch-Mage resides. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Arch-Mage%27s+Quarters)
- **[Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach")** — An immense, naturally lit [cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") inhabited by hordes of [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") and containing the ruins of a [Dwemer](/wiki/Lore:Dwemer "Lore:Dwemer") [city](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Blackreach)
- **[Hall of Countenance](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Countenance "Skyrim:Hall of Countenance")** — The main living and sleeping quarters for most of the higher ranked mages of the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hall+of+Countenance)
-  **[Hob's Fall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Hob%27s_Fall_Cave "Skyrim:Hob's Fall Cave")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") west of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") containing [necromancers](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hob%27s+Fall+Cave)
-  **[Journeyman's Nook](/wiki/Skyrim:Journeyman%27s_Nook "Skyrim:Journeyman's Nook")** — A small [outdoor Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Dwellings "Skyrim:Nordic Dwellings") southeast of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") containing a [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Journeyman%27s+Nook)
- **[The Midden](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Midden "Skyrim:The Midden")** — A medium-sized dungeon underneath the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") containing the [Atronach Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge "Skyrim:Atronach Forge") and home to the [Augur of Dunlain](/wiki/Skyrim:Augur_of_Dunlain "Skyrim:Augur of Dunlain"), a former mage of the college. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Midden)
-  **[Mount Anthor](/wiki/Skyrim:Mount_Anthor "Skyrim:Mount Anthor")** — A mountaintop [dragon lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs") south-southwest of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mount+Anthor)
-  **[Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Saarthal "Skyrim:Saarthal")** — A medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") southwest of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Saarthal)
-  **[Winterhold Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Winterhold Imperial Camp")** — An [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Camps "Skyrim:Imperial Camps") in [Winterhold Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)"), located southeast of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") and northwest of [Frostflow Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostflow_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Frostflow Lighthouse"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Winterhold+Imperial+Camp)

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Tundra+Homestead+%28CC%29)

- With the [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") add-on, you can build a lab in any of your constructed homes, either in the [Main Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Main_Hall "Skyrim:Main Hall"), or by building an [Alchemy Laboratory](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Laboratory "Skyrim:Alchemy Laboratory").[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire")

## Bugs

- You may clip through the alchemy lab, and appear to be standing in the middle. This has no effect on exiting or using the table. **?**
- Sometimes after making many potions the lab doesn't let you select more ingredients. This is fixed simply by leaving it and then selecting it again. **?**
- Very rarely, the alchemy lab will be invisible; if it is on a tabletop, only the bare surface of the table will appear, and if the lab is a freestanding piece of furniture such as the one in the Midden, the whole piece will be invisible and any items stacked on top will appear to be suspended in midair. The lab will still be visible to the cursor and can be interacted with as normal, although the animation will also show the lab as invisible.

# Skyrim:Alchemy Tutorial

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Learn the basics of potion making.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Radiant](#Radiant_Options) |
| Location(s): | [Radiant](#Radiant_Options) |
| Reward: | a [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") |
| ID: | TutorialAlchemy |

Blisterwort and Wheat: Restore Health

## Radiant Options

This is a radiant quest which you can receive from any of the following people.

| QuestGiver | QuestGiverHome |
| --- | --- |
| [Arcadia](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcadia "Skyrim:Arcadia") | [Arcadia's Cauldron](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcadia%27s_Cauldron "Skyrim:Arcadia's Cauldron") ([Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun")) |
| [Orgnar](/wiki/Skyrim:Orgnar "Skyrim:Orgnar") | [Sleeping Giant Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping_Giant_Inn "Skyrim:Sleeping Giant Inn") ([Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood")) |
| [Zaria](/wiki/Skyrim:Zaria "Skyrim:Zaria") | [Grave Concoctions](/wiki/Skyrim:Grave_Concoctions "Skyrim:Grave Concoctions") ([Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath")) |

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Ask for permission to use the alchemy lab.
2. Combine the ingredients at an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs") to create a potion.

### The Recipe

Ask any of the quest givers if you can use the [alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") lab located in their shop or inn, as the case may be. They will all consent with the same reply, *"Long as you clean up. You know how to use it right? Mix a couple of ingredients together, see what happens. A little [Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") and [Blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort") makes a healing potion, if you didn't know. We have plenty of ingredients for sale, too."*
This is just a suggestion, crafting any potion will complete the quest objective, you can buy [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") directly from the quest giver.

### Crafting the Potion

Once your ingredients are collected, approach the alchemy lab and select at least two of them. Note that to succeed into crafting a potion, each ingredient must share an [alchemical effect](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Effects "Skyrim:Alchemy Effects") with another. Confirm the crafting and create a potion to complete the quest. After this, the effect will be added to the Alchemy menu if you don't have it already.

## Quest Stages

| Alchemy Tutorial (TutorialAlchemy) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Craft a potion |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 20, 100.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage TutorialAlchemy stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest TutorialAlchemy`.

# Skyrim:Aldepius

## Overview

Aldepius as a Solitude guard

**Aldepius** is an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") soldier found at [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge"). His status as a new recruit was questioned by a [guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard_(Alternative_Armors_-_Steel_Soldier) "Skyrim:Guard (Alternative Armors - Steel Soldier)") stationed with Aldepius, who questioned his older age and curiosity relating to who the bandit informant was. Upon finding out that no one with the name Aldepius was listed on the garrison roster, the guard [wrote about](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard%27s_Note_on_Aldepius "Skyrim:Guard's Note on Aldepius") his intent to confront Aldepius at Dragon Bridge, subsequently getting murdered by him.

After discovering the murdered guard, the [Dragonborn](/wiki/Lore:Dragonborn "Lore:Dragonborn") can find a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Aldepius%27_Confession "Skyrim:Aldepius' Confession") by Aldepius confessing to the murder and revealing his true identity as [Peladius](/wiki/Skyrim:Peladius "Skyrim:Peladius"), a bandit whose group was betrayed, leading to him joining the guard to find out who was responsible. Stating that there was no honor in what he has done, he now seeks an honorable death from the Dragonborn.

As Aldepius, he wears a set of [Solitude guard armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Specialty_Gear#Guard_Equipment "Skyrim:Specialty Gear"), as well as a pair of Imperial bracers and boots. Once the Dragonborn encounters him as Peladius, he wears a full set of [steel soldier armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Soldier_Armor "Skyrim:Steel Soldier Armor") and wields a [long bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Bow "Skyrim:Long Bow") and [Steel Sword of Embers](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Sword_of_Embers "Skyrim:Steel Sword of Embers"). He also carries 30 [steel arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Arrow "Skyrim:Steel Arrow") and a [potion of plentiful healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Healing").

Aldepius as a Stormcloak guard

Aldepius's choice of armor depends on whether or not the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") or the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") are in charge of Haafingar.

## Related Quests

- **[Over the Edge](/wiki/Skyrim:Over_the_Edge "Skyrim:Over the Edge")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Steel_Soldier "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Steel Soldier"): A criminal has sensed his past catching up with him.

## Notes

- Aldepius/Peladius can only be encountered with the [Alternative Armors - Steel Soldier](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Steel_Soldier "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Steel Soldier") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club").

## Bugs

- During the [Prophet](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet "Skyrim:Prophet") quest, you can ask Aldepius about a [Moth Priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dexion_Evicus "Skyrim:Dexion Evicus") visiting Dragon Bridge. He will respond with generic guard dialogue, but since his voice type is different from the other guards he will remain silent.
  - The [Official Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch"), version 1.6.1130.0, fixes this bug.

Alding

**Alding** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H"). Along with [Gjuk](/wiki/Skyrim:Gjuk "Skyrim:Gjuk") and [Irlof](/wiki/Skyrim:Irlof "Skyrim:Irlof"), he forms the crew of [Blood Horker](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_Horker "Skyrim:Blood Horker") Captain [Stig Salt-Plank](/wiki/Skyrim:Stig_Salt-Plank "Skyrim:Stig Salt-Plank"). He and the rest of the crew only exist during [Rise in the East](/wiki/Skyrim:Rise_in_the_East "Skyrim:Rise in the East"), after you give the logbook to [Orthus Endario](/wiki/Skyrim:Orthus_Endario "Skyrim:Orthus Endario"), where they are found in the [Windpeak Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Windpeak_Inn "Skyrim:Windpeak Inn"), partaking in their regular "festivities".

After the initial scene plays out, he will be found sitting in place at a bench inside of the inn, enjoying a tankard of mead or eating bread.

He only wears a [roughspun tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Roughspun_Tunic "Skyrim:Roughspun Tunic") with some [footwraps](/wiki/Skyrim:Footwraps "Skyrim:Footwraps").

## Related Quests

- **[Rise in the East](/wiki/Skyrim:Rise_in_the_East "Skyrim:Rise in the East")**: Help the [East Empire Company](/wiki/Lore:East_Empire_Company "Lore:East Empire Company") take care of some [pirates](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_Horker "Skyrim:Blood Horker").

## Conversations

When you enter the inn, you will find him and Stig harassing the local bard and barmaid, [Karita](/wiki/Skyrim:Karita_(bard) "Skyrim:Karita (bard)"):

**Karita**: *"You beasts are the worst."*
**Stig**: *"Come now, dearie, surely we aren't all that bad."*
**Karita**: *"Just... leave me alone! I've brought your mead, now drink it and shut your filthy mouths."*
**Alding**: *"Oh, we've got other things in mind for our mouths, sweetie."*

## Bugs

- While Stig mentions he and his crew will be retreating to Hammerfell, they actually remain in the Windpeak Inn for the rest of the game.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.1, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Alduin's Bane

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Main.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Main.png) | **Exploit the Time-Wound to learn [Dragonrend](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonrend "Skyrim:Dragonrend") and defeat [Alduin](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin") at the [Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:Throat of the World").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Automatic upon acquiring the [Elder Scroll](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Scroll_(Dragon) "Skyrim:Elder Scroll (Dragon)") during [Elder Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Knowledge "Skyrim:Elder Knowledge") |
| Location(s): | [Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:Throat of the World") |
| Reward: | [Dragonrend](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonrend "Skyrim:Dragonrend") shout |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =0 (Delphine)  =0 (Esbern) |
| ID: | MQ206 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Elder Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Knowledge "Skyrim:Elder Knowledge") | **Next →** [The Fallen](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Fallen "Skyrim:The Fallen") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Elder Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Knowledge "Skyrim:Elder Knowledge") | | → Next | [The Fallen](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Fallen "Skyrim:The Fallen") | | |

The Nord heroes battling Alduin in a vision produced by an Elder Scroll

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Read the [Elder Scroll](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Scroll "Skyrim:Elder Scroll") at the Throat of the World.
2. Learn how to use the [Dragonrend](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonrend "Skyrim:Dragonrend") shout.
3. Defeat [Alduin](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin").

### The Time-Wound

As soon as you claim the [Elder Scroll](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Scroll "Skyrim:Elder Scroll") from the [Tower of Mzark](/wiki/Skyrim:Tower_of_Mzark "Skyrim:Tower of Mzark"), this quest starts and points you back to the [Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:Throat of the World") where [Paarthurnax](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(dragon) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (dragon)") awaits. Exit the tower by using the lift to the east and pull the handle on the surface, thus providing yet another shortcut to [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach"). You will find yourself a long way from [Alftand](/wiki/Skyrim:Alftand "Skyrim:Alftand") where you initially entered and may wish to loot the abandoned camp just outside the tower entrance. Travel back to the Throat of the World and Paarthurnax will be quite impressed with your efforts: *"You have it. The Kel - the Elder Scroll. Tiid kreh... qalos. Time shudders at its touch. There is no question. You are doom-driven. Kogaan Akatosh. The very [bones of the earths](/wiki/Lore:Earth_Bones "Lore:Earth Bones") are at your disposal. Go then. Fulfill your destiny. Take the Scroll to the Time-Wound. Do not delay. [Alduin](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin") will be coming. He cannot miss the signs."*

Make your way a few feet to the northwest and you will see the Time-Wound, an unnatural ripple of air that distorts light passing through it. Go into the middle, find the Elder Scroll in your inventory, and read it:

### A Glimpse into the Past

*"Know that Gormlaith sent you down to death!"*

*"Which is why I brought the Elder Scroll."*

*"Alduin approaches!"*

*"Begone, World-Eater!"*

*"You are banished!"*

After a temporary blindness, you will regain your vision and find yourself in the [Merethic Era](/wiki/Lore:Merethic_Era "Lore:Merethic Era"), unable to move and forced to watch past events. The strange carvings on the Elder Scroll will still be visible and your vision blurred and tinted red. You will watch as the ancient Nords, [Hakon One-Eye](/wiki/Skyrim:Hakon_One-Eye "Skyrim:Hakon One-Eye") and [Gormlaith Golden-Hilt](/wiki/Skyrim:Gormlaith_Golden-Hilt "Skyrim:Gormlaith Golden-Hilt"), fight a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") atop the Throat of the World. The battle will begin with Hakon on his own, until Gormlaith comes rushing in and jumps on top of the dragon:

**Hakon**: *"Gormlaith! We're running out of time! The battle..."*
**Dragon**: *"Daar sul thur se Alduin vokrii. Today Alduin's lordship will be restored. But I honor your courage. Krif voth ahkrin. Die now, in vain."*
**Hakon**: (attacks) *"For Skyrim!"*
**Gormlaith**: (joins the attack and kills the dragon) *"Know that Gormlaith sent you down to death!"*

After killing the dragon they will sheathe their swords and walk past a [desecrated corpse](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Desecrated_Corpse "Skyrim:Containers"), talking about their victory:

**Gormlaith**: *"Hakon! A glorious day, is it not!"*
**Hakon**: *"Have you no thought beyond the blooding of your blade?"*
**Gormlaith**: *"What else is there?"*
**Hakon**: *"The battle below goes ill. If Alduin does not rise to our challenge, I fear all may be lost."*
**Gormlaith**: *"You worry too much, brother. Victory will be ours."*

At this point, [Felldir the Old](/wiki/Skyrim:Felldir_the_Old "Skyrim:Felldir the Old") will emerge from behind you and join the conversation:

**Hakon**: (To Felldir) *"Why does Alduin hang back? We've staked everything on this plan of yours, old man."*
**Felldir**: *"He will come. He cannot ignore our defiance. And why should he fear us, even now?"*
**Gormlaith**: *"We've bloodied him well. Four of his kin have fallen to my blade alone this day."*
**Felldir**: *"But none have yet stood against Alduin himself. Galthor, Sorri, Birkir..."*
**Gormlaith**: *"They did not have Dragonrend. Once we bring him down, I promise I will have his head."*
**Felldir**: *"You do not understand. Alduin cannot be slain like a lesser dragon. He is beyond our strength. Which is why I brought the Elder Scroll."*

Felldir will then pull out the ancient [Elder Scroll](/wiki/Lore:Elder_Scroll "Lore:Elder Scroll"), much to the surprise of Hakon:

**Hakon**: *"Felldir! We agreed not to use it!"*
**Felldir**: *"I never agreed. And if you are right, I will not need it."*
**Hakon**: *"No. We will deal with Alduin ourselves, here and now."*
**Gormlaith**: *"We shall see soon enough. Alduin approaches!"*
**Hakon**: *"So be it."*

While the Nords draw their weapons, Alduin will land atop the word wall and speak:

**Alduin**: *"Meyye! Tahrodiis aanne! Him hinde pah liiv! Zu'u hin daan!"*
**Gormlaith**: *"Let those that watch from Sovngarde envy us this day!"*

At this point, the Nords will release the [Dragonrend](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonrend "Skyrim:Dragonrend") shout. When they shout, you will automatically learn the shout. In the skies, Alduin will feel mortality rise through his body and will immediately be forced to land:

**Alduin**: *"Nivahriin joorre! What have you done? What twisted Words have you created?! Tahrodiis Paarthurnax! My teeth to his neck! But first... dir ko maar. You will die in terror, knowing your final fate... To feed my power when I come for you in Sovngarde!"*
**Gormlaith**: *"If I die today, it will not be in terror. You feel fear for the first time, worm. I see it in your eyes. Skyrim will be free!"*

The three Nords will then proceed to attack the World-Eater, but to no avail. Alduin will pick up Gormlaith between his teeth and fling her to the right, killing her:

**Hakon**: *"No, damn you! It's no use! Use the Scroll, Felldir! Now!"*
**Felldir**: *"Hold, Alduin on the Wing! [Sister Hawk](/wiki/Lore:Kyne "Lore:Kyne"), grant us your sacred breath to make this contract heard! Begone, World-Eater! By words with older bones than your own we break your perch on this age and send you out! You are banished! Alduin, we shout you out from all our endings unto the last!"*
**Alduin**: *"Faal Kel...?! Nikriinne..."*

A surprised Alduin will futilely breathe fire at Felldir before disappearing into the flow of time, to an unknown era. Felldir, however, knows that the defeat was only temporary:

**Felldir**: *"You are banished!"*
**Hakon**: *"It worked... you did it..."*
**Felldir**: *"Yes, the World-Eater is gone... may the spirits have mercy on our souls."*

### Alduin

Directly after the cutscene, when you arrive back in the present, Alduin will appear at the Throat of the World, shouting: *"Bahloki nahkip sillesejoor. My belly is full of the souls of your fellow mortals, Dovahkiin. Die now and await your fate in Sovngarde!"* Paarthurnax will then interfere, saying: *"Lost funt. You are too late, Alduin! Dovahkiin! Use Dragonrend, if you know it!"*

Alduin battles Paarthurnax at the Throat of the World.

Paarthurnax and Alduin will take flight, attacking each other in the air. Paarthurnax tells you to use your Dragonrend shout if you can, and indeed, when the chance arises, use Dragonrend on Alduin, forcing him to the ground. It can be rather difficult distinguishing between the two dragons if the battle is done at night or while it is snowing. The quest arrow on your compass always points to Alduin, so use that to distinguish between them.

During the battle, Alduin may say some of the following taunts: *"Dovahkiin, you call yourself? Arrogant mortal."*, *"Bahloki nahkip sillesejoor."*, *"I will feast on your soul in Sovngarde!"*, *"You are no match for me, joor!"*, *"Paarthurnax is weak. I am strong."*, *"My time has come again."*, *"Maar saraan ko Sovngarde."*, *"I have feasted on many greater than you."*, or *"You will pay for your defiance!"*

When Alduin is grounded, he may say: *"My teeth to your neck, Dovahkiin!"* When he is grounded, you must attack him as much as you can before he takes flight again. This may take a few tries, since he has a huge health pool and does reasonable damage. Be wary of Alduin's "Dragon Storm Call" shout, which causes fiery meteors to rain from the sky, causing both fire and physical damage. Note that [Clear Skies](/wiki/Skyrim:Clear_Skies "Skyrim:Clear Skies") will cancel the meteor shower, and has such a short recharge time that it won't interfere with using Dragonrend on him. In particular, using Dragonrend immediately when it recharges will keep Alduin grounded for the whole fight. When Alduin's health drops to zero, he says: *"Meyz mul, Dovahkiin. You have become strong. But I am Al-du-in, Firstborn of Akatosh! Mulaagi zok lot! I cannot be slain here, by you or anyone else! You cannot prevail against me. I will outlast you... mortal!"* He will then fly off, completing the quest.

## Notes

- Having a follower stand within the Time-Wound when you read the Elder Scroll may prevent Alduin from landing on the word wall in the cutscene.[*verification needed*]
- It is not possible to harm Alduin while he's in the air. He is immune to all forms of damage except when he's under the Dragonrend shout effect (i.e. grounded). Therefore, you cannot defeat Alduin without using Dragonrend on him, regardless of how powerful your weapons and spells might be.
- Inadvertently using Dragonrend on Paarthurnax and therefore grounding him often makes Alduin hover in one place in the air while attacking Paarthurnax, thus making it easier to strike him with Dragonrend, although it is better to ground Alduin alone.
- Alduin may remark *"You may have picked up the weapons of my ancient foes, but you are not their equal!"* when you use Dragonrend against him.
- Even after completing this quest, the Elder Scroll will still be marked as a quest item, making it impossible for you to drop it or place it in a container, though it will remain weightless. The only way to remove it from your inventory is to sell it to [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub") in the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") library, although if you do, and you install the [Dawnguard add-on](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"), you will have to buy it back from him for another quest.
- Reading the Elder Scroll at the Time-Wound removes all active blessings, including the [Blessing of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Blessing_of_Talos "Skyrim:Blessing of Talos"). To shorten your shout cooldown for the fight with Alduin, you need to wear either an [Amulet of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_Talos "Skyrim:Amulet of Talos") or [Storm-Bear Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm-Bear_Armor "Skyrim:Storm-Bear Armor")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War_Champions "Skyrim:Civil War Champions").
- During the cutscene Gormlaith, Hakon or Felldir may look at you, as if you were there.
- If [Survival mode](/wiki/Skyrim:Survival_Mode "Skyrim:Survival Mode") is active, you may wish to save the game before reading the Elder Scroll, as it is possible to die immediately after exiting the cutscene due to cold.

## Bugs

- Alduin may become invincible during the fight.
  - According to the patch notes, this bug was supposed to have been fixed by version 1.9.26.0.8 of the [Skyrim Official Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"). However, there have still been confirmed reports of this bug occurring, specifically if you exit dialogue with Alduin prematurely after returning from the vision in the Time Wound, or if you die during the fight with Alduin and reload the game.
  -  Open the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console"), click on Alduin, then use the command `disable` followed by `enable`. This may allow Alduin to be damaged normally.
  - Saving immediately before combat starts, then fast-traveling away and returning, may fix this.
  - As of 1.9.32.0, the game creates an autosave after exiting the Merethic-era cutscene, right before the conversation with Alduin.
- The cutscene in the Merethic era may not trigger or complete, leaving you stuck there.
  - Doing other quests and then returning may fix this.
  -  If Gormlaith gets stuck and is unable reach the first dragon to kill it, you can manually kill the dragon using the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") by clicking on it and entering `kill`. This will allow the cutscene to progress.
  -  If Alduin does not land, use the console commands `prid 4377e` followed by `moveto cda03` to move Alduin to the landing position.
  -  Another possible fix after getting stuck is to open the console and enter `setstage mq206 32`. This should let you regain control of the camera and a dragon should land, enabling the cutscene to continue. You could also enter `setstage mq206 70` to learn the Dragonrend shout directly, then enter `setstage mq206 100` to end the cutscene and begin the fight with Alduin.
- Fixing the stuck cutscene bug may leave you with blurred vision.
  - This can be fixed by using vision altering effects. Examples of these include visiting a new dragon wall and learning a new shout or using the [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery") perk [Eagle Eye](/wiki/Skyrim:Eagle_Eye "Skyrim:Eagle Eye").
  -  This can be fixed by opening the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") and entering `sisme 0`.
- Fixing the stuck cutscene bug may bring the Merethic Alduin out with you, resulting in two Alduins: the real one flying above you which starts talking, and the Merethic one still crippled on the ground which starts fighting instantly. **?**
  -  This can be fixed by opening the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console"), clicking on the Merethic Alduin on the ground (or entering `prid 4377e`), then entering `disable`. This should be done before defeating the real Alduin and progressing the quest, or the Merethic Alduin will keep regaining strength and start fighting again after you walk down the Throat of the World.

## Quest Stages

| Alduin's Bane (MQ206) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | I've located the Elder Scroll that was used to cast Alduin forward into our time by the Nord heroes of old. If Paarthurnax is right, if I read it near the Time-Wound I will get a vision of the past, when the ancient Nords used the Dragonrend Shout against Alduin. *Objective 10:* Read the Elder Scroll at the Time-Wound |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Learn the "Dragonrend" Shout from the Nord heroes |
| 70 |  | *This is a hidden state, used to teach the player the Dragonrend shout. it does not adjust the quest text, status, or objectives, and is only used to award the Dragonrend shout during the Time-Wound cutscene.* |
| 100 |  | I read the Elder Scroll near the Time-Wound, and learned the Dragonrend Shout in a vision of the Nord heroes fighting Alduin in the distant past. Now I need to use Dragonrend to defeat Alduin in the present time. *Objective 30:* Defeat Alduin |
| 220 | ☑ | I read the Elder Scroll near the Time-Wound, and learned the Dragonrend Shout in a vision of the Nord heroes fighting Alduin in the distant past. When I returned from the vision, Alduin attacked me, and I used Dragonrend to bring him down and defeat him. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 1, 5, 15, 30, 32, 33, 35, 40, 42, 48, 50, 52, 60, 75, 80, 82, 85, 87, 88, 89, 90, 120, 140, 160, 180, 200, 230, 240.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MQ206 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MQ206`.
