# Skyrim:Alduin's Wall

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Main.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Main.png) | **Locate the prophecy within [Sky Haven Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Sky_Haven_Temple "Skyrim:Sky Haven Temple").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Esbern](/wiki/Skyrim:Esbern "Skyrim:Esbern") |
| Location(s): | [The Ratway](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ratway "Skyrim:The Ratway"), [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood"), [Sky Haven Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Sky_Haven_Temple "Skyrim:Sky Haven Temple") |
| Reward: | [Dragonbane](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonbane "Skyrim:Dragonbane") |
| ID: | MQ203 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [A Cornered Rat](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Cornered_Rat "Skyrim:A Cornered Rat") | **Next →** [The Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:The Throat of the World") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [A Cornered Rat](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Cornered_Rat "Skyrim:A Cornered Rat") | | → Next | [The Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:The Throat of the World") | | |

Alduin's Wall

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Escort [Esbern](/wiki/Skyrim:Esbern "Skyrim:Esbern") to [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood").
2. Talk to Esbern.
3. Gain entrance to [Sky Haven Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Sky_Haven_Temple "Skyrim:Sky Haven Temple").
4. Learn the secret of Alduin's Wall.

### Blades Reunited

From [The Ratway](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ratway "Skyrim:The Ratway") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"), you need to travel with Esbern back to [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood") so he can meet with [Delphine](/wiki/Skyrim:Delphine "Skyrim:Delphine"). Make your way out of the Ratway by backtracking the way you came in, avoiding or defeating the Thalmor agents and various underworld criminals you may encounter along the way. The Esbern dialogue option "Do you know the way out of here?" will cause Esbern to lead the way through the Ratway rather than follow you (however, this can be glitched). Once outside, travel back to Riverwood and into the [Sleeping Giant Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping_Giant_Inn "Skyrim:Sleeping Giant Inn").

Upon arriving at the inn, you will be greeted by Delphine, who is surprised to see Esbern alive. After a brief reunion between the two former [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades"), Delphine will wish to speak to the two of you in private. Delphine will lead you to the secret cellar, where Esbern announces that his intention is to find an ancient Blades prophecy. He will go on to say the group must leave for [Sky Haven Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Sky_Haven_Temple "Skyrim:Sky Haven Temple"), a Blades headquarters built up around an ancient [Akaviri](/wiki/Lore:Akavir "Lore:Akavir") military camp in [the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach"). Of particular importance within that location is a structure from the [First Era](/wiki/Lore:First_Era "Lore:First Era") known as Alduin's Wall, which may tell how to defeat [Alduin](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin").

Delphine soon realizes that Esbern's description of the temple's location matches her knowledge of the [Karthspire](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthspire "Skyrim:Karthspire"), and the Blades agree to set out for that location. Delphine tells [Orgnar](/wiki/Skyrim:Orgnar "Skyrim:Orgnar") that the Inn is now his and bids him farewell. At this point, you can choose to either travel with the Blades or alone, heading towards the marker Delphine placed on your map. If you choose to travel alone, it may be easier to take a carriage to [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") and then head east, as Delphine recommends. You can also take the longer route through [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold"), though this is generally easier if you have the Blades with you.

### The Karthspire

Whether you went as a group or solo, when you arrive at the [Karthspire Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthspire_Camp "Skyrim:Karthspire Camp") you will find yourself up against a horde of [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"), and possibly a [hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven"). Both Delphine and Esbern will arrive and assist you (and probably aggravate the entire camp in the process: if you want to make sure they don't do that, you may have to ask them to "wait here" a considerable distance away.) Though you can stand and fight, if the battle begins to overwhelm you, it is simple to retreat into the Karthspire caverns themselves (but see the [Bugs](#Bugs) section).

You will now need to journey through the interior of the Karthspire, defeating the three Forsworn, including a [Forsworn Briarheart](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_Briarheart "Skyrim:Forsworn Briarheart"), and making your way to the beginning of the Akaviri ruins.

### Sky Haven Temple

Heading up the stone steps on the right you will be confronted with a trio of three-sided pillars, each side inscribed with a symbol. According to Esbern, they are of Akaviri origin, but the one that matters most to you is the symbol meaning 'Dragonborn'. This symbol resembles two dragon heads facing each other and an arrow pointing down. Activate all three pillars until this symbol is facing you. This will lower the bridge to your left, allowing you and the Blades to continue.

In the next chamber you will be confronted with a floor of pressure plates, inscribed with the same three symbols as the pillars. Once again the Dragonborn symbol is the key; stepping only on these tiles to reach the other side. Stepping off of the route will cause a fireball to be launched, so moving slowly is advisable. If you prefer, you can use the [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") shout to move across without triggering the trap.

Once safely on the other side, pull the chain to allow the Blades to cross, and exit the chamber. You will need to travel across a pair of bridges, and then into the entrance chamber of Sky Haven Temple. Esbern heads for a large stone head built into the far wall, which, according to Esbern, is the visage of [Reman Cyrodiil](/wiki/Lore:Reman_Cyrodiil "Lore:Reman Cyrodiil"). In fact, the entire temple is some sort of shrine to him. In front of the head is a large carved circle, which Esbern declares to be a "blood seal", requiring the blood of a Dragonborn to function. Activating the circle prompts you to cut your hand, dripping blood on the circle. The stone head then retracts, and an opening is revealed.

Delphine and Esbern take a few moments in the following tunnel to inspect the Akaviri carvings and light the braziers, but you may wish to run ahead and view the temple proper. Upon arriving, Esbern is immediately attracted to a large relief on the far wall, Alduin's Wall. He moves over to inspect it, taking several moments to fully identify it. The wall depicts the history of [Alduin](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin") and the [Dragon Cult](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Cult "Skyrim:Dragon Cult"), and details a prophecy regarding their defeat. Ultimately, he proclaims that the ancient Nords actually used a shout to defeat Alduin, and Delphine turns to you asking if you know of such a shout.

Alduin's Wall relief

At this point, your best source of information is likely the [Greybeards](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards"), however much Delphine may dislike them. Esbern will go on to explain that the last panel speaks of Alduin's return and his contending with the last Dragonborn at the end of time. From here, take a moment to explore the Temple to locate the leveled sword [Dragonbane](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonbane "Skyrim:Dragonbane") found in a room almost straight opposite Alduin's Wall.

Bid farewell to the two Blades, both of them enraptured by Sky Haven Temple, and leave the building. Your next destination is [High Hrothgar](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Hrothgar "Skyrim:High Hrothgar"), home of the Greybeards.

### Achievements

One [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") is unlocked when you complete this quest:

-  **Alduin's Wall** (20 points/Bronze)

## Notes

- Dragonbane is a [leveled item](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Items "Skyrim:Leveled Items"), so it's better not to enter Sky Haven Temple until level 46 if you want the best version of the weapon.
- The one-handed skill book *[Mace Etiquette](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace_Etiquette "Skyrim:Mace Etiquette")* can be found in the same room as Dragonbane.
- After reaching stage 60 of this quest, [Nahagliiv](/wiki/Skyrim:Nahagliiv "Skyrim:Nahagliiv") will be resurrected by Alduin at a dragon mound west of Rorikstead.
- Esbern and Delphine can follow you as companions in addition to any other followers you may have. They are high level and [essential](/wiki/Skyrim:Essential_NPCs "Skyrim:Essential NPCs"). However, Esbern and Delphine will constantly tell you to take them to the quest destination, and Esbern has a fondness for area-effect spells that may cause fights with other followers.
- It is possible to encounter an Elder Dragon or stronger at Karthspire, even if you aren't high enough level to encounter them elsewhere. Also, once you start the quest, the Forsworn at Karthspire Camp will be much more dangerous.
- [Alduin's Wall](/wiki/Lore:Alduin%27s_Wall "Lore:Alduin's Wall") prophesied the events of *[Arena](/wiki/Arena:Arena "Arena:Arena")*, *[Daggerfall](/wiki/Daggerfall:Daggerfall "Daggerfall:Daggerfall")*, *[Morrowind](/wiki/Morrowind:Morrowind "Morrowind:Morrowind")*, *[Oblivion](/wiki/Oblivion:Oblivion "Oblivion:Oblivion")*, and *[Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim")*.

## Bugs

- A tripwire in The Ratway Vaults may reset and block your way out.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.
  - Use Unrelenting Force through Esbern to activate the trap.
- Esbern may get stuck in the book animation at the beginning of the quest.
  - Running into him or hitting him with [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") may fix this.
  -  `setstage MQ203 60` can be used as a partial solution for this and will advance the quest to stage 60 ("Gain entrance to Sky Haven Temple").
- If Esbern is leading you out of the Ratway, he may freeze in the large central room due to a pathfinding loop. **?**
  - This is apparently recoverable only by loading an earlier save.
- Even if you say that you wish to travel together, if you take too long or go in a direction that isn't towards Karthspire, Delphine and Esbern may go off on their own anyways as if you'd asked to travel separately. **?**
- If you have already explored the temple entrance and lowered the bridge when this quest is started, the quest might get stuck. After activating the Blood Seal, instead of following you into the Temple, Delphine and Esbern will run back to the first puzzle and wait for you to complete it; however, it has already been completed, thus making the NPCs wait indefinitely.
  -  Open the command console and type `setstage MQ203 140`. This will get the NPCs to move across the bridge. It is also possible to use the `moveto player` function to move both of them to your location once you're at the top.
  -  If the above still doesn't work, open the console and type `setstage MQ203 280`. This finishes the quest for you and starts the next one.
  - The position of Delphine and Esbern when you enter Sky Haven Temple appears to matter when this bug is encountered. Basically, both Delphine and Esbern must be past the area previously closed off by the face when you advance into Sky Haven Temple. To achieve this, load a saved file (or auto-save) before activation of the Blood Seal. Once you activate the Blood Seal, while Esbern talks and you are able to move after activating the Blood Seal, immediately "equip" the three-word version of [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") and move directly next to either Delphine or Esbern looking at the now opened entrance. Both Delphine and Esbern can be "shouted" into the entrance area, will not attack when shouted, and will follow you into Sky Haven Temple advancing the quest.
  - If the "shout method" above doesn't work, use this workaround: Just before the three of you leave the Inn at Riverwood, choose the option to travel together. Go outside, and then fast travel directly to Sky Haven Temple. You will land outside the skull entrance along with the two of them. Let them go through the motions, and then slice your hand when the time comes. Once the door opens, let them go through their dialogue sequence. Walk first up the stairs—and they will follow you.
- Esbern and Delphine may get stuck in combat mode if you do not kill all of the Forsworn at Karthspire Camp.
  - If you wait for a long time (10+ hours), this may reset their stance and they will continue up the stairs, however it does not appear to work every time.
  - Instead of waiting, leaving the cave with Sky Haven Temple and then fast traveling back to Sky Haven Temple also should continue the quest.
  - Killing all of the Forsworn before entering Sky Haven Temple should avoid this entirely.
- Esbern may not complete examination of Alduin's Wall.
  - If you have a follower with you when you enter the interior of the Karthspire, they will not follow you, but they may reappear when you enter Sky Haven Temple proper. If this happens, Delphine may fail to follow Esbern up the steps or engage Esbern in dialogue, preventing the quest from completing. Reloading a save and telling your follower to wait outside Karthspire or simply go home should avoid this.
  - It is scripted that Delphine and Esbern equip torches and light basins. If Delphine does not equip her torch, she may not follow Esbern up the stairs, and Esbern will not examine the wall when spoken to. Force Delphine to equip her torch by opening the command console, clicking Delphine to get her ID, and typing `equipitem 0001D4EC 1 left`. Delphine should then move to light a basin and the scripting will continue.
  - You can also try to move the NPCs inside Sky Haven Temple manually. Open the command console and click on Esbern to get his ID. Walk into the temple and up to the wall, and enter the command `moveto player` to teleport Esbern to you. Repeat this process with Delphine. Once you teleport an NPC it will start walking to where it is supposed to be, and it should fix the issue.
  - If that fails, make sure both Esbern and Delphine are on the landing next to the wall, then check the current stage of the quest with `getstage mq203`. If it is at 250, advance to 260 with `setstage mq203 260`. You will know it worked if Delphine then proceeds with the dialogue asking about a shout that can bring a dragon down out of the sky.
  - You can try to going up the stairs and taking the door to Skyrim. Fast travel across the map then back to Sky Haven Temple. Delphine should be standing next to Esbern at the wall and the quest will continue.
  - If all else fails, you can use `setstage MQ203 280` to finish the quest
- Delphine may not light all the braziers that she's supposed to. **?**

## Quest Stages

| Alduin's Wall (MQ203) | | |

| 50 |  | *Objective 20:* Talk to Esbern |
| 60 |  | I found the Blades loremaster Esbern and brought him to Riverwood to talk to Delphine. He believes that the secret to defeating Alduin will be revealed by Alduin's Wall, an artifact created by the ancient Blades. We need to go to Sky Haven Temple to find Alduin's Wall and see what it can tell us. *Objective 30:* Gain entrance to Sky Haven Temple |
| 200 |  | *Objective 40:* Learn the secret of Alduin's Wall |
| 280 | ☑ | I found the Blades loremaster Esbern and brought him to Riverwood to talk to Delphine. He believed that the secret to defeating Alduin would be revealed by Alduin's Wall, an artifact created by the ancient Blades. We went to the hidden Blades stronghold of Sky Haven Temple, and found Alduin's Wall inside. It showed that Alduin was defeated in the past by some kind of Shout. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 1, 5, 6, 20, 25, 30, 40, 48, 65, 70, 75, 80, 100, 110, 120, 140, 150, 180, 185, 210, 230, 250, 260, 290, 300.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MQ203 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MQ203`.

# Skyrim:Alduin

## Overview

| Perks | [Reduced Damage 0.5](/wiki/Skyrim:Reduced_Damage_0.5 "Skyrim:Reduced Damage 0.5") | | |
| [Essential](/wiki/Skyrim:Essential_Creatures "Skyrim:Essential Creatures") | Yes, until stage 100 of [Dragonslayer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonslayer "Skyrim:Dragonslayer") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [MQ101AlduinFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:MQ101AlduinFaction "Skyrim:MQ101AlduinFaction"); [Used by dragonrend shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Used_by_dragonrend_shout "Skyrim:Used by dragonrend shout") | | |

Alduin

The dragon [Viinturuth](/wiki/Skyrim:Viinturuth "Skyrim:Viinturuth") with Alduin, right after being resurrected

**Alduin**, or the **World-Eater**, as he is known to the residents of [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim"), is an immensely powerful [Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon"), and the main antagonist of the [Main Quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Main_Quest "Skyrim:Main Quest"). He is depicted as a malevolent force who destroys the world periodically, and the [Nords](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") believe that his reappearance heralds the end of time. He is the self-proclaimed First-Born of [Akatosh](/wiki/Lore:Akatosh "Lore:Akatosh"). His name can be separated into "Al-Du-In", which means "Destroyer-Devour-Master" in Dragon Language.

He has a 50% resistance to fire and a 25% weakness to frost, and knows the [Fire Breath](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Breath "Skyrim:Fire Breath"), [Frost Breath](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Breath "Skyrim:Frost Breath") and [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") shouts, as well as the [Dragon Storm Call](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Storm_Call "Skyrim:Dragon Storm Call") shout unique to him.

## Resurrection of Dragons

During the quest [A Blade in the Dark](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Blade_in_the_Dark "Skyrim:A Blade in the Dark"), Alduin resurrects the dead dragon [Sahloknir](/wiki/Skyrim:Sahloknir "Skyrim:Sahloknir") from his burial place, revealing how the rest of the dragons have returned after being slain centuries ago. After this quest, you may get to see the rare occasion where Alduin resurrects another, leveled dragon.

When resurrecting other dragons, Alduin can be spotted from a distance, and more easily heard thanks to his roars. It's easy to distinguish Alduin from other dragons, as he will stay far in the distance, flying around, unlike normal wild dragons (who will fly right to you). Alduin won't leave this location until you approach [*verification needed*], and as soon as you get close enough, he will say "(dragon name) *zil gro dovah ulse!*" then use the shout *"Slen Tiid Vo!"*. A new dragon will appear (having been resurrected) and respond to Alduin, after which Alduin flies away and the resurrected dragon attacks you. It is possible to interrupt the resurrection by attacking Alduin, which causes him to become hostile and fly away [*verification needed*].

Alduin will have a brief conversation during resurrection. He will say the name of either [Vuljotnaak](/wiki/Skyrim:Vuljotnaak "Skyrim:Vuljotnaak"), [Viinturuth](/wiki/Skyrim:Viinturuth "Skyrim:Viinturuth"), or [Nahagliiv](/wiki/Skyrim:Nahagliiv "Skyrim:Nahagliiv"), depending on which dragon he is resurrecting:

:   **(dragon name):** *"Alduin, thuri!"*
:   **Alduin:** *"Alok, (dragon name). Tiid boaan."*

## Related Quests

- **[Unbound](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound "Skyrim:Unbound")**: Escape [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") custody and a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") attack.
- **[A Blade in the Dark](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Blade_in_the_Dark "Skyrim:A Blade in the Dark")**: Prove you are Dragonborn to [Delphine](/wiki/Skyrim:Delphine "Skyrim:Delphine") by slaying the dragon [Sahloknir](/wiki/Skyrim:Sahloknir "Skyrim:Sahloknir").
- **[Alduin's Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Wall "Skyrim:Alduin's Wall")**: Locate the prophecy within [Sky Haven Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Sky_Haven_Temple "Skyrim:Sky Haven Temple").
- **[Alduin's Bane](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Bane "Skyrim:Alduin's Bane")**: Exploit the Time-Wound to learn [Dragonrend](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonrend "Skyrim:Dragonrend") and defeat Alduin at the [Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:Throat of the World").
- **[The Fallen](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Fallen "Skyrim:The Fallen")**: Capture and interrogate [an ally](/wiki/Skyrim:Odahviing "Skyrim:Odahviing") of Alduin.
- **[Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde_(quest) "Skyrim:Sovngarde (quest)")**: Seek out Alduin within [Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde_(place) "Skyrim:Sovngarde (place)").
- **[Dragonslayer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonslayer "Skyrim:Dragonslayer")**: Put an end to the World-Eater.

### Unbound

Moments before you are to be executed in [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen"), Alduin lands in the town and begins to unleash carnage, incidentally allowing you to escape execution with [Ralof](/wiki/Skyrim:Ralof "Skyrim:Ralof"). His movement throughout the town will follow you as you progress. First, he will break open the watchtower containing Ralof and [Jarl Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak"), killing a [Stormcloak Soldier](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Soldier "Skyrim:Stormcloak Soldier"). Next, he will kill [Torolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Torolf "Skyrim:Torolf") with his Fire Breath shout near [Hadvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hadvar "Skyrim:Hadvar"). Alduin will then land on a wall as you and Hadvar pass near it, before taking to the skies and moving freely throughout the town, Shouting at various soldiers.

While destroying the town, Alduin may speak in the [Dragon language](/wiki/Lore:Dragon_Language "Lore:Dragon Language"):

:   *"Hin sil fen nahkip bahloki."*
:   *"Nust wo ni qiilaan fen kos duaan."*

Throughout [Helgen Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen_Keep "Skyrim:Helgen Keep"), the battle with Alduin in the town rages on, causing door blockages and cave-ins within the dungeon. After at last escaping, Alduin can be seen soaring away, flying over [Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(place) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (place)") to an unknown location.

### A Blade in the Dark

While resurrecting Sahloknir in Kynesgrove:

:   **Alduin:** *"Sahloknir, ziil gro dovah ulse! Slen Tiid Vo!"*

When the dragon, Sahloknir, is whole once more, he has a conversation in the dragon language with Alduin:

:   **Sahloknir:** *"Alduin, thuri! Boaan tiid vokriiha suleyksejun kruziik?"*
:   **Alduin:** *"Geh, Sahloknir, kaali mir.*

Turning to you:
*"Ful, losei Dovahkiin? Zu'u koraav nid nol dov do hi. You do not even know our tongue, do you? Such arrogance, to dare take for yourself the name of Dovah. Sahloknir, krii daar joorre."*

After ordering Sahloknir to kill you, Alduin flies away.

#### Time Wound

While the Nords draw their weapons, Alduin will land atop the word wall and speak:

**Alduin**: *"Meyye! Tahrodiis aanne! Him hinde pah liiv! Zu'u hin daan!"*
**Gormlaith**: *"Let those that watch from Sovngarde envy us this day!"*

At this point, the Nords will release the [Dragonrend](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonrend "Skyrim:Dragonrend") Shout. When they Shout, you will automatically learn it. In the skies, Alduin will feel mortality rise through his body and will be forced to land:

**Alduin**: *"Nivahriin joorre! What have you done? What twisted Words have you created?! Tahrodiis Paarthurnax! My teeth to his neck! But first... dir ko maar. You will die in terror, knowing your final fate... To feed my power when I come for you in Sovngarde!"*
**Gormlaith**: *"If I die today, it will not be in terror. You feel fear for the first time, worm. I see it in your eyes. Skyrim will be free!"*

The three Nords will then proceed to attack the World-Eater, but to no avail. Alduin will pick up Gormlaith between his teeth and fling her to the right, killing her:

**Hakon**: *"No, damn you! It's no use! Use the Scroll, Felldir! Now!"*
**Felldir**: *"Hold, Alduin on the Wing! [Sister Hawk](/wiki/Lore:Kyne "Lore:Kyne"), grant us your sacred breath to make this contract heard! Begone, World-Eater! By words with older bones than your own we break your perch on this age and send you out! You are banished! Alduin, we shout you out from all our endings unto the last!"*
**Alduin**: *"Faal Kel...?! Nikriinne..."*

A surprised Alduin will futilely breathe fire at Felldir before disappearing into the flow of time, to an unknown era.

#### Present

Directly after the cutscene, when you arrive back in the present, Alduin will appear at the Throat of the World, shouting:

:   **Alduin:** *"Bahloki nahkip sillesejoor. My belly is full of the souls of your fellow mortals, Dovahkiin. Die now and await your fate in Sovngarde!"*
:   **Paarthurnax:** *"Lost funt. You are too late, Alduin! Dovahkiin! Use Dragonrend, if you know it!"*
:   **Alduin:** *"Suleyki mulaag, Paarthurnax. My power has waxed, while yours has waned. Aav uv dir. Join me or perish with your mortal friends."*
:   **Paarthurnax:** *"Unslaad hokoron! Never again!"*

Alduin battles Paarthurnax at the Throat of the World

Paarthurnax and Alduin will take flight, attacking each other in the air. During the battle, Alduin may say some of the following taunts:

:   *"Dovahkiin, you call yourself? Arrogant mortal."*
:   *"Fen du hin sille ko Sovngarde!"*
:   *"I will feast on your soul in Sovngarde!"*
:   *"You are no match for me, joor!"*
:   *"Paarthurnax is weak. I am strong."*
:   *"My time has come again."*
:   *"Maar saraan ko Sovngarde."*
:   *"I have feasted on many greater than you."*
:   *"You will pay for your defiance!"*
:   *"You may have picked up the weapons of my ancient foes, but you are not their equal!"*

When Alduin is grounded he may say:

:   *"My teeth to your neck, Dovahkiin!"*

When Alduin's health drops to zero, he says:

:   *"Meyz mul, Dovahkiin. You have become strong. But I am Al-du-in, Firstborn of Akatosh! Mulaagi zok lot! I cannot be slain here, by you or anyone else! You cannot prevail against me. I will outlast you... mortal!"*

He will then fly off to [Skuldafn](/wiki/Skyrim:Skuldafn "Skyrim:Skuldafn") to regain his power.

### Dragonslayer

After traveling to [Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde_(place) "Skyrim:Sovngarde (place)") and discovering Alduin's Soul Snare, the player will have to navigate through the fog in search of the [Hall of Valor](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Valor "Skyrim:Hall of Valor"). Alduin appears at multiple points within the mist, either lurking on ground-level or soaring overhead. If you take too long, Alduin will swoop down and kill a Stormcloak Soldier and an [Imperial Soldier](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Soldier "Skyrim:Imperial Soldier").

Returning to the outdoors of Sovngarde from the Hall of Valor with the three ancient Nord heroes will launch an attempt to dispel Alduin's Soul Snare. After using [Clear Skies](/wiki/Skyrim:Clear_Skies "Skyrim:Clear Skies"):

:   **Alduin:** *"Ven Mul Riik!"*
:   **Gormlaith:** *"Again!"*
:   **Felldir:** *"We can shatter his power if we Shout together!"*

After Shouting again:

:   **Alduin:** *"Ven Mul Riik!"*
:   **Hakon:** *"Does his strength have no end? Is our struggle in vain?"*
:   **Gormlaith:** *"Stand fast! His strength is failing! Once more, and his might will be broken!"*
:   **Felldir:** *"His power crumbles - do not pause for breath!"*

As he flies in:

:   **Alduin:** *"Face me, then! Zu'u Alduin!"*

With his fog shield dissipated, Alduin will have no choice but to face you in open combat. He is immune to damage until hit by Dragonrend. Alduin is functionally very similar to most other dragons, his only significant difference being a tendency to crawl backwards while Shouting, creating distance between him and his attacker. With the three Nord heroes on your side (and potentially [Tsun](/wiki/Skyrim:Tsun "Skyrim:Tsun"), if Alduin attacks him), Alduin should go down fairly easily. Avoid his fire breath, as it can be deadly even for high level players. If you are having trouble defeating him, range counters him fairly well.

During the battle, Alduin may use the following taunts, issued to either you or the Nord heroes:

:   *"You are persistent, Dovahkiin. Pruzah ol aar. A fine slave you would have made."*
:   *"Dovahkiin, hin kah fen kos bonaar."*

    

    The death of Alduin
:   *"Zu'u lost daal."*
:   *"I have already defeated your friends once. Beyn. I do not fear them."*
:   *"Kel drey ni viik."*
:   *"Di kiirre fen alok."*
:   *"Daar Lein los dii."*
:   *"Pahlok joorre! Hin kah fen kos bonaar."*
:   *"Zu'u Alduin, zok sahrot do naan ko Lein."*
:   *"Zu'u lost kriaan hi ont, nu hin sille fen nahkip suleyki."*
:   *"Dovahkiin, you should not have come here. Nu hin sil dii."*
:   *"Zu'u ni faas gaaffesejul."*

When Alduin's health is fully depleted, he will enter a hunched state and become immune to all damage, other than the player. Be sure to heal if you are on low health, as the meteors can still kill you and Alduin will never recover. After dealing the final blow, Alduin will writhe and thrash, screaming:

:   **Alduin:** *"Zu'u unslaad! Zu'u nis oblaan!*

After crying out, Alduin explodes, leaving behind a wispy, golden-glowing black skeleton which soon fades away. With Alduin dead, Sovngarde returns to its ethereal state and the main story of Skyrim comes to an end.

## Notes

- Alduin has a special passive ability, "AbAlduinInvulnerability" in the editor, which renders him invulnerable to harm so long as he is not affected by Dragonrend (or, as the conditions on the effect detail, "is allowed to fly").
- If you encounter Alduin during the resurrection of a dragon, he can be hit with any long-ranged attack. However, it appears that he is not actually hit, as no health bar appears. He does appear as hostile at that moment, showing as a red dot on your compass. The red dot will disappear after Alduin flies away again.
- During the resurrection of a dragon, Alduin will occasionally Shout, darkening the sky.
- Alduin has a unique Shout called Dragon Storm Call, which is very similar to [Storm Call](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm_Call "Skyrim:Storm Call"), and causes fiery meteors to rain from the sky.
- If you deal enough damage to him when he is resurrecting a dragon, he will crash land on the ground, then take flight again and fly off.
- Alduin is voiced by [Daniel Riordan](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Daniel_Riordan "wikipedia:Daniel Riordan").
- [Adam Adamowicz](/wiki/General:Adam_Adamowicz "General:Adam Adamowicz") and [Jonah Lobe](/wiki/General:Jonah_Lobe "General:Jonah Lobe") designed [Alduin](/wiki/Lore:Alduin "Lore:Alduin") by using the texture of meteorites as a basis.
- There's a very small chance that Alduin will use Unrelenting Force on you if you try to damage him while he is resurrecting a dragon.
- The version of Alduin encountered in the past during [Alduin's Bane](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Bane "Skyrim:Alduin's Bane") (BaseID `4377F`, RefID `4377E`), is a static level 100 and boasts 6905 health.
- If the [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") add-on is installed and you defeat Alduin before starting [At the Summit of Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:At_the_Summit_of_Apocrypha "Skyrim:At the Summit of Apocrypha"), [Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Miraak_(person) "Skyrim:Miraak (person)") will be impressed and say *"Felling Alduin was a mighty deed, and I thank you for it. He would have proved troublesome to me."*
- It is impossible to loot Alduin, even though the option presents itself while his body dissipates. However, it is possible to harvest [dragon heartscales](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Heartscales "Skyrim:Dragon Heartscales") from him.
- Alduin's soul is not absorbed. You can later discuss the ramifications of this with [Arngeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Arngeir "Skyrim:Arngeir") unless you have antagonized him by killing [Paarthurnax](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(dragon) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (dragon)").
- Alduin is the highest level dragon in the game; boasting a max level of 100.
- Alduin's damage scales as the player levels up; at level 100 his breath is equivalent to an ancient dragon. Interestingly, his bite damage remains static, always being that of a regular dragon.
- Alduin is the only dragon in the game that can use both fire and frost breath.

## Bugs

- When encountering Alduin raising a dragon as a random encounter, chasing him off before he completes the resurrection causes the dragon burial mound to become stuck in the 'bonfire of energy' state.
  -  This can be fixed using the console, at least as far as the visual effects go: look upwards at the 'bonfire', open the console, click on the fire effect and use the *disable* command. Look at the middle of the dragon mound, click on it, and use the *disable* command again. This will make both the special effect and the mound cover disappear.
- After learning [Dragonrend](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonrend "Skyrim:Dragonrend") during [Alduin's Bane](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Bane "Skyrim:Alduin's Bane"), Alduin will sometimes be invincible.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.9, fixes this bug.
  - Escaping the battle by running down the Throat of the World and fast-traveling back appears to make him vulnerable to damage again.
- Alduin's death cry during [Dragonslayer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonslayer "Skyrim:Dragonslayer") may be too quiet for you to hear if you're too far away.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.2, fixes this bug.

Alea Quintus

Alea unmasked

**Alea Quintus**, a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H"), is one of the three people that may be selected from and killed to gain entry into the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") during the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:With_Friends_Like_These... "Skyrim:With Friends Like These..."). She is the mother of six children. She does not act scared when spoken with; rather, she says that she has no time to deal with this and demands to be released. Furthermore, Alea states that she may have made enemies with the take-no-nonsense attitude she has had to adopt in order to raise her children.

She wears a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#0001be1a "Skyrim:Clothes") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#0001be1b "Skyrim:Clothes"). She, like the other two captives, also wears an [execution hood](/wiki/Skyrim:Execution_Hood "Skyrim:Execution Hood").

## Related Quests

- **[With Friends Like These...](/wiki/Skyrim:With_Friends_Like_These... "Skyrim:With Friends Like These...")**: Repay your debt to [the Family](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood"), and show you are willing to kill on command.

## Quest-Related Dialogue

When approached for the first time:

:   *"I don't have time for this nonsense. I've got a home to keep and children to feed. Now let me out of here!"*
:   *"Cowards! Stealing a woman from her home! For shame!"*
:   *"Get these things off of me!"*
:   *"By the gods, when I get out of here you're dead! You hear me? Dead!"*
:   *"Aggghh! Re...lease me!"*

If you kill another captive and talk to Alea, she will say:

:   *"What's happening? Damn it, what are you doing?"*

Speaking to her:

:   **Who are you?**
:   *"None of your damned business who I am! If you're going to kill me, just do it already! As [Mara](/wiki/Lore:Mara "Lore:Mara") is my witness, if I didn't have this damned hood on right now I would spit right in your face..."*
:   **Would someone pay to have you killed?**
:   *"Excuse me? What kind of question is that?"*

:   :   **One last time: Would. Someone. Pay. To. Have. You. Killed? (Intimidate)**
    :   *"I'm kneeling here with my hands bound and a sack over my head, and you have the gall to ask me that? What do you think, genius?"*

:   :   **It's all right. Just tell me what I need to know. (Persuade)**
    :   *"I'm a woman living in Skyrim with six children and no husband. I don't have the time or patience to be 'nice.' Do some people look down on me? Have I made some enemies? You're damn right."*

If you kill Astrid, you can initiate conversation with Alea to free her:

:   *"You cut these bindings this minute! You hear me? You cut these bindings right now!"*
:   **(Cut the captive's bonds)**
:   *"Well it's about damn time. Capturing a woman from her home, keeping her bound like an animal. Ridiculous..."*

Talking to her after this will have her respond:

:   *"I don't know who you are, or what's going on here, but you ought to be ashamed of yourself."*

## Notes

If you kill her, [Astrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Astrid "Skyrim:Astrid") will remark:

:   *"Ah, the feisty goodwife. Quite the mouth on her. Someone must have wanted her dead... right?"*
:   *"Hmm. The fearless wife and mother, and the [underhanded Khajiit](/wiki/Skyrim:Vasha "Skyrim:Vasha"). Had to be one of them, right? Interesting choice."*
:   *"The [blubbering barbarian](/wiki/Skyrim:Fultheim_the_Fearless "Skyrim:Fultheim the Fearless") and the tenacious mother. Must have been one of them, right?"*
:   *"Well, well, aren't we the over-achiever? Three possibilities, three victims. Must have been one of them, right? So why take chances..."*

| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [BYOHDisallowGamesFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:BYOHDisallowGamesFaction "Skyrim:BYOHDisallowGamesFaction"); [BYOHRelationshipAdoptableFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:BYOHRelationshipAdoptableFaction "Skyrim:BYOHRelationshipAdoptableFaction"); [BYOHUrchin\_AlesanJobFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:BYOHUrchin_AlesanJobFaction "Skyrim:BYOHUrchin AlesanJobFaction"); [CrimeFactionPale](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionPale "Skyrim:CrimeFactionPale"); [DawnstarWindpeakInnFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:DawnstarWindpeakInnFaction "Skyrim:DawnstarWindpeakInnFaction"); [TownDawnstarFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:TownDawnstarFaction "Skyrim:TownDawnstarFaction") | | |

Alesan

**Alesan** is a [Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard "Skyrim:Redguard") [child](/wiki/Skyrim:Child "Skyrim:Child") who lives in [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"). He makes money by bringing food to the miners of [Quicksilver Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Mine "Skyrim:Quicksilver Mine") and [Iron-Breaker Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron-Breaker_Mine "Skyrim:Iron-Breaker Mine").

He sleeps on a bedroll at the [Windpeak Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Windpeak_Inn "Skyrim:Windpeak Inn") every night between 9pm and 8am. He wakes up to go straight to work, running through the town and delivering food from the inn workers, [Karita](/wiki/Skyrim:Karita_(bard) "Skyrim:Karita (bard)") and [Thoring](/wiki/Skyrim:Thoring "Skyrim:Thoring"), to the local miners: [Gjak](/wiki/Skyrim:Gjak "Skyrim:Gjak"), [Karl](/wiki/Skyrim:Karl "Skyrim:Karl"), [Lond](/wiki/Skyrim:Lond "Skyrim:Lond"), and [Borgny](/wiki/Skyrim:Borgny "Skyrim:Borgny"). At 6pm, he switches to feeding the chickens outside the inn, and can be seen carrying a handled basket.

He wears a set of [child's clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Child%27s_Clothes#000467bf "Skyrim:Child's Clothes") and [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shoes#000e80a8 "Skyrim:Shoes") and carries two loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), along with an [assortment of random food and toys](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Child "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Dialogue

If the time is between 8am and 6pm, he will be busy doing his job, and will tell you such as he runs past you:

:   *"Sorry! Gotta run!"*
:   *"One side, comin' through!"*
:   *"Move it, move it!"*
:   *"I'm late! Gotta run!"*

If you approach him when it is at least 6pm, he may complain by saying:

:   *"I'm so tired..."*
:   *"Whew! I'm worn out."*

:   **What's the hurry?**

    :   *"I'm running food and supplies to the miners. Don't pay much, but they let me sleep by the fire in the inn most nights."*

:   **Where are your parents, kid?**

    :   *"They're... dead. My pa was a sailor. Took me with him on his last trip. After he got sick, they... put us off here and left without us. He... died a few days later. I've tried to make do since then, but... it's been hard. Real hard."*

You will then have a dialogue option to [adopt](/wiki/Skyrim:Child#Adoption "Skyrim:Child") him. You can only go through with the adoption if you have a [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses") with a child's bed and container.

After you end conversation with him:

:   *"Nice talkin' with you."*

## Notes

- Alesan is the only [child](/wiki/Skyrim:Child "Skyrim:Child") in Dawnstar.

## Bugs

- If you adopt him, Alesan may sometimes not be able to receive gifts.
  -  The [Unofficial Hearthfire Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Hearthfire_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Hearthfire Patch"), version 2.0.2, fixes this bug.
- If you adopt him, Alesan can get stuck in a loop, entering and exiting the cellar repeatedly, similar to [Lydia](/wiki/Skyrim:Lydia "Skyrim:Lydia") sitting and rising from the chair in [Breezehome](/wiki/Skyrim:Breezehome "Skyrim:Breezehome"). **?**
  - Talking to Alesan and having him do something may fix this.
- Alesan's inventory can slowly become clogged up with baskets he never uses for anything due to a bad scripting setup. This means if you adopt him it could be impossible to give him gifts.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.5, addresses this issue. The script causing this has been removed and the baskets will be removed from his inventory.

# Skyrim:Alessandra

## Overview

| Alessandra (RefID: 00019DD9) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Home City | [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") | | |
| Location | [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Riften) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Riften)") | | |
| Race | [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") | Gender | Female |
| Level | 10 | Class | [Priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Priest "Skyrim:Priest") |

| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | **[Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration")**, **[Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech")**, [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy"), [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration"), [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting"), [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") | | |

| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [CrimeFactionRift](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionRift "Skyrim:CrimeFactionRift"); [TownRiftenFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:TownRiftenFaction "Skyrim:TownRiftenFaction") | | |

Alessandra

*"This is all I know how to do... prepare and inter the deceased."*

**Alessandra** is an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") [priestess](/wiki/Skyrim:Priest "Skyrim:Priest") of [Arkay](/wiki/Lore:Arkay "Lore:Arkay"), who is solely and bitterly responsible for tending to [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften")'s [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Riften) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Riften)"). She is quite uncomfortable about her line of work, due to some unfinished business in the past. During the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Pilgrimage "Skyrim:Pilgrimage") she will ask you to sort things out and give her inner peace.

She spends all day surrounded by the dead. She wakes up at 7am and starts the day with a one-hour breakfast. She will then work for twelve hours, mostly tending to the body of a dead [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_(dead)#Nord2 "Skyrim:Nord (dead)") on the table. At 7pm she takes a quick one-hour dinner, then proceeds to work until her bedtime at midnight. She sleeps in a room in the adjoining [Temple of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Mara "Skyrim:Temple of Mara").

She wears a set of [monk robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Monk_Robes "Skyrim:Monk Robes") with a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000bacd7 "Skyrim:Boots"). She wields a leveled [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") (up to [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven "Skyrim:Elven") quality at level 20) and carries a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic") and an assortment of [lower-class items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Poor "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"). She knows several spells as well, specifically [Frostbite](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite "Skyrim:Frostbite"), [Ice Spike](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Spike "Skyrim:Ice Spike"), [Oakflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Oakflesh "Skyrim:Oakflesh"), and [Lesser Ward](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Ward "Skyrim:Lesser Ward").

## Related Quests

- **[Pilgrimage](/wiki/Skyrim:Pilgrimage "Skyrim:Pilgrimage")**: Help Alessandra make peace with her dead father.
- **[Spread the Love](/wiki/Skyrim:Spread_the_Love "Skyrim:Spread the Love")**: Distribute religious [literature](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warmth_of_Mara "Skyrim:The Warmth of Mara") to the citizens of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").

### Pilgrimage

If you speak to her and ask her about her work, she will explain the unfortunate situation:

:   **You tend the graveyard?**
:   *"If you're trying to ask if I tend the hall of the dead alone, then the answer is yes. You think anyone around here is going to lift a shovel to help me? Guess again. 'Leave the dirty work to old Alessandra.' Look, I didn't ask for this job, I got stuck with it thanks to my father."*
:   **How's your father to blame for your job?**
:   *"My father was a Priest of Arkay. All my life was spent around the dead, being forced to learn the proper burial rituals and prayers. I never had any friends; who'd want to spend time with 'the little weird girl who hangs around dead people?' So I grew up with a miserable trade. This is all I know how to do... prepare and inter the deceased."*
:   **How can you make peace with your father?**
:   *"I'd like to make the journey to the Hall of the Dead in Windhelm*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *and give my ceremonial dagger to Andurs, the caretaker. I believe once it's interred with my father's remains I'll be at peace with his memory."*

You now have a choice to help her or not:

:   **Good luck with that.**

    :   *"Yes. Perhaps one day I'll be able to make the journey, but for now I need to tend the dead."*

:   **I can bring it for you.**

    :   *"I hadn't asked you because I was afraid you'd say no. I appreciate your help. Here, I'm entrusting you with the dagger. Bring it to Andurs and he'll take care of the rest."*

Once you offer to help her you can ask her about the dagger:

:   *"Anything else before you make the journey?"*
:   **What's special about the dagger?**
:   *"A Priest of Arkay is entrusted with a ceremonial dagger once they've completed their training. It usually*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *given by the head priest who sanctified the ritual. In my case, the head priest happened to be my father. The thing is, I never wanted to follow in his footsteps... I*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *some ways I still don't."*
:   **But you ended up doing it anyway**
:   *"I had to for honor's sake, but I had waited too long. My father died before he could see my training to completion. When I finally became a priest, they gave me the new high priest's dagger, but I already owned my father's. So you see, I have to return it. It breaks tradition, and I need to tell him that I finally did what he wanted."*

She will send you on your way with:

:   *"Be cautious, the pilgrimage to the Shrine is not an easy one."*

In [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), local [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Whiterun) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Whiterun)") priest [Andurs](/wiki/Skyrim:Andurs "Skyrim:Andurs") definitely knows about Alessandra's problem. When you hand him the [ceremonial dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Alessandra%27s_Dagger "Skyrim:Alessandra's Dagger"), he will be grateful: *"She finally decided to return it to her father. Bless her heart. I will make sure this finds its way to his tomb as soon as possible. Thank you for bringing it, my child."*

When you return to Alessandra in Riften, she will immediately say:

:   *"The pilgrimage is complete, I can feel it."*
:   **I gave the dagger to Andurs.**
:   *"I felt a caress on my cheek some time ago... I thought it to be a trick of the wind, but I think it was a message from my father. We've made peace with one another without even uttering a single word and I'm content for the first time in my life. I thank you. Here, please accept this as a token of my appreciation for your selfless action."*

She will then hand you a reward (see [this section](/wiki/Skyrim:Pilgrimage#Bugs "Skyrim:Pilgrimage")) and will start to greet you with:

:   *"I'm feeling much better thanks to your efforts."*

### Spread the Love

She will accept a pamphlet from the temple:

:   **Here, sister. Blessings of Mara upon you.**
:   *"Oh, a new pamphlet from Dinya? I'll be glad to read it. Thanks."*

## Dialogue

When you enter her workplace, she can potentially say:

:   *"Come to laugh at the grave tender?"*
:   *"I can see that disapproving look in your eye."*
:   *"I'd ask you maintain civility while you're here."*

## Bugs

- Alessandra says Andurs is in Windhelm, but he is actually in Whiterun.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.6, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Alethius

## Overview

| Alethius (RefID: 000C370B) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Location | [Nchuand-Zel Excavation Site](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel "Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel") | | |
| Race | [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") | Gender | Male |
| Level | 1 | Class | [Citizen](/wiki/Skyrim:Citizen_(class) "Skyrim:Citizen (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000C370B | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000C370C |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 0 (**Dead**) | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 50 |
| Voice Type | [MaleCondescending](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleCondescending "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleCondescending") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [CrimeFactionRift](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionRift "Skyrim:CrimeFactionRift"); [TownIvarsteadFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:TownIvarsteadFaction "Skyrim:TownIvarsteadFaction") | | |

Alethius

**Alethius** is a deceased [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") whose corpse can be found just before the entrance to [Nchuand-Zel](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel "Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel"), within the Nchuand-Zel Excavation Site underneath [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep") in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). He wears a full set of [Imperial armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Light_Armor "Skyrim:Imperial Light Armor"), and carries a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Alethius%27s_Notes "Skyrim:Alethius's Notes") that begins the quest [The Lost Expedition](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lost_Expedition "Skyrim:The Lost Expedition"). He was assigned to guard the research expedition into Nchuand-Zel, but met his untimely death, likely by [Nimhe](/wiki/Skyrim:Nimhe "Skyrim:Nimhe"), the giant [frostbite spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider") guarding the entrance to Nchuand-Zel, whose lair is just above Alethius's body.

## Related Quests

- **[The Lost Expedition](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lost_Expedition "Skyrim:The Lost Expedition")**: Recover the journals from the expedition in [Nchuand-Zel](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel "Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel").

## Notes

- His note is written to someone named Salonia, and [two](/wiki/Skyrim:Salonia_Carvain "Skyrim:Salonia Carvain") [NPCs](/wiki/Skyrim:Salonia_Caelia "Skyrim:Salonia Caelia") with that first name exist in Skyrim. However, neither of them appear to have any connection to him.
- It's possible that he was created with [Bassianus Axius](/wiki/Skyrim:Bassianus_Axius "Skyrim:Bassianus Axius") as a base, as they share the same voice type and it would explain Alethius' otherwise random faction inclusions.

## Bugs

- Due to the fact that he's part of the [Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") crime faction, should you resurrect and re-kill him, then you could theoretically receive a bounty in that hold.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.6, addresses this issue. He has been removed from the crime faction.

# Skyrim:Alexia Vici

Alexia Vici

**Alexia Vici** is an elderly [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") [citizen](/wiki/Skyrim:Citizen_(class) "Skyrim:Citizen (class)").
She is only present during the [wedding](/wiki/Skyrim:Bound_Until_Death "Skyrim:Bound Until Death") of her daughter, [Vittoria Vici](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici"). She is also the aunt of [Emperor Titus Mede II](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II_(real) "Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (real)").

Alexia wears a set of farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#000261c0 "Skyrim:Clothes") along with a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000261bd "Skyrim:Boots").

## Related Quests

- **[Bound Until Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Bound_Until_Death "Skyrim:Bound Until Death")**: Assassinate [Vittoria Vici](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici") at her own wedding.

### Bound Until Death

At the wedding, Alexia can be found in a political debate with [the groom's](/wiki/Skyrim:Asgeir_Snow-Shod "Skyrim:Asgeir Snow-Shod") [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") father, [Vulwulf Snow-Shod](/wiki/Skyrim:Vulwulf_Snow-Shod "Skyrim:Vulwulf Snow-Shod"):

:   **Vulwulf**: *"Typical Imperial rot. You speak of Skyrim like you know the land, know its people. You're from [Cyrodiil](/wiki/Lore:Cyrodiil "Lore:Cyrodiil")! You know nothing about us! Nothing!"*
:   **Alexia**: *"Oh, I know enough. I know those trouble-making Stormcloaks refuse to submit to [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") authority. Such seditious behavior. Why it's treason!"*
:   **Vulwulf**: *"And when the elves marched into your beloved Cyrodiil, and everyone took up arms against them, wasn't that treason? Against the [Dominion](/wiki/Lore:Aldmeri_Dominion "Lore:Aldmeri Dominion")? Huh?"*
:   **Alexia**: *"Why that's not the same thing at all. The Dominion were invaders. Conquerors. We had to fight them, to preserve our own way of life."*
:   **Vulwulf**: *"My point exactly."*

She is clearly unhappy with her daughter's marriage, as she can be found saying:

:   *"What my daughter sees in that... barbarian, I'll never know."*
:   *"The thought of paying a dowry to that, that... Stormcloak turns my stomach."*
:   *"My nephew, the Emperor. Too busy to attend the wedding of his beloved cousin. We won't stand for this slight, I assure you."*

If spoken directly to:

:   **Having a good time?**
:   *"I most certainly am not. I've just lost my daughter to a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") beast, and my nephew Titus is too busy playing Emperor to even show up."*

When Vittoria Vici dies, Alexia can be found screaming:

:   *"My daughter! Dead! Noooooo!"*

## Notes

- Alexia has six different AI packages which she never uses due to her only appearing during the quest.

# Skyrim:Alfarinn

## Overview

| Alfarinn (RefID: 0009B7C8) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Home City | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") | | |
| Store | [Windhelm Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm_Stables "Skyrim:Windhelm Stables") | | |
| Race | [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") | Gender | Male |
| Level | 6 | Class | [Warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Warrior_(class) "Skyrim:Warrior (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0009B7C8 | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0009B7AB |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 108 | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 50 |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 67 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | **[One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed")**, [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block"), [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor"), [Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") | | |
| Class Details | [CombatWarrior1H](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H") | | |

| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [BanditFriendFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:BanditFriendFaction "Skyrim:BanditFriendFaction"); [Blood-Kin of the Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood-Kin_of_the_Orcs "Skyrim:Blood-Kin of the Orcs"); [Carriage System Vendors](/wiki/Skyrim:Carriage_System_Vendors "Skyrim:Carriage System Vendors"); [CrimeFactionEastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionEastmarch "Skyrim:CrimeFactionEastmarch"); [Faction that is friends with all Creatures](/wiki/Skyrim:Faction_that_is_friends_with_all_Creatures "Skyrim:Faction that is friends with all Creatures"); [Friends with PredatorFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:Friends_with_PredatorFaction "Skyrim:Friends with PredatorFaction") | | |

Alfarinn

**Alfarinn** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H"), and the [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") [carriage](/wiki/Skyrim:Carriage "Skyrim:Carriage") driver.

Alfarinn wears a set of farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#000261c0 "Skyrim:Clothes"), a pair of [gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Gloves#000261c1 "Skyrim:Gloves"), and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000261bd "Skyrim:Boots"). He is equipped with an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe").

## Related Quests

- **[Prophet (Dawnguard)](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet_(Dawnguard) "Skyrim:Prophet (Dawnguard)")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Find and rescue [a Moth Priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dexion_Evicus "Skyrim:Dexion Evicus") from the [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Vampire_Clan "Skyrim:Volkihar Vampire Clan").
- **[Prophet (Vampire)](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet_(Vampire) "Skyrim:Prophet (Vampire)")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): The time of prophecy has arrived! Locate [a Moth Priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dexion_Evicus "Skyrim:Dexion Evicus") for the [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Vampire_Clan "Skyrim:Volkihar Vampire Clan").

## Dialogue

:   **What do you know about Windhelm?**
:   *"It's an old city, I can tell you that. The Palace of the Kings is ancient. It's not the friendliest place for outsiders. The [Dark Elves](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") were all forced to live in a slum called the Grey*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *Quarter. The [Argonians](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian "Skyrim:Argonian") can't even live inside the walls. They're all stuck out on the docks. Still, [Candlehearth Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall")'s got decent food and cheap bunks. You could do worse."*

Alfhild Battle-Born

**Alfhild Battle-Born** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmer_(class) "Skyrim:Farmer (class)") and a member of [Clan Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle-Born "Skyrim:Battle-Born") living in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). [Jon Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:Jon_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Jon Battle-Born") is her brother, and her parents are [Olfrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Olfrid_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Olfrid Battle-Born") and [Bergritte](/wiki/Skyrim:Bergritte_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Bergritte Battle-Born"). She is married to [Idolaf](/wiki/Skyrim:Idolaf_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Idolaf Battle-Born"), with whom she has a son, [Lars](/wiki/Skyrim:Lars_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Lars Battle-Born"). She maintains [Battle-Born Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle-Born_Farm "Skyrim:Battle-Born Farm") outside Whiterun and will buy [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat"), and [gourds](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd") for a [harvesting job](/wiki/Skyrim:Gather_Wheat "Skyrim:Gather Wheat") well done.

At 6am, she goes to the [Temple of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Temple of Kynareth"), and then goes to the farm at 10am. She stays there until 8pm when she goes home, and goes to sleep at midnight. On Tirdas and Turdas, she goes to listen to [Heimskr's](/wiki/Skyrim:Heimskr "Skyrim:Heimskr") sermon at 3pm.

Alfhid wears a set of farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#000209a6 "Skyrim:Clothes") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000209a5 "Skyrim:Boots"), and is equipped with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"). She carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_House_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Key to House Battle-Born") to the [House of Clan Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Battle-Born "Skyrim:House of Clan Battle-Born"), a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Battle-Born_Farmhouse "Skyrim:Key to Battle-Born Farmhouse") to Battle-Born Farm, and a selection of [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Gather Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Gather_Wheat "Skyrim:Gather Wheat")**: Get paid to gather crops. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Dialogue

When approached, she will often comment on the ongoing feud between the Battle-Born and [Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Gray-Mane") clans but takes a different view of the feud than her husband and father, saying:

:   *"This war's as stupid as our feud with Clan Gray-Mane."*
:   *"Need something? Unlike the rest of my family, I've got work to do."*

She may also reveal that her son [Lars](/wiki/Skyrim:Lars_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Lars Battle-Born") often gets bullied:

:   *"My boy Lars has been getting beat senseless, and by a [girl](/wiki/Skyrim:Braith "Skyrim:Braith"), no less!"*

She will also tell you about her brother Jon's interests:

:   *"My brother Jon's got the right of it - join the [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College") and avoid this pointless war."* She will add, *"Too bad he died before he had the chance."* if Jon is dead.

She exits conversation with either:

:   *"I'll see you."*
:   *"It's back to work, then."*

## Conversations

Alfhild and her mother, Bergritte, can be heard discussing reading material:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Alfhild**: | *"So, what book should I read to you tonight?"* |
| **Bergritte**: | *"How about '[The Lusty Argonian Maid](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lusty_Argonian_Maid "Skyrim:The Lusty Argonian Maid")'?"* |
| **Alfhild**: | *"Mother!"* |
| **Bergritte**: | *"You've got no sense of humor, you know that? Why don't you pick up where you left off with '[The Real Barenziah](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Real_Barenziah "Skyrim:The Real Barenziah")'."* |

# Skyrim:Alftand

## Overview
