The green-hooded Alik'r Mercenary

An Alik'r Mercenary is a [Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard "Skyrim:Redguard") mercenary who is encountered at a camp southeast of [Fort Greymoor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Greymoor "Skyrim:Fort Greymoor") during the quest [Gift of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Gift_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Gift of Kynareth"). He is a member of a band of the Alik'r following [Majid the Mad](/wiki/Skyrim:Majid_the_Mad "Skyrim:Majid the Mad") that stole the [Lord's Mail](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord%27s_Mail_(item) "Skyrim:Lord's Mail (item)"). He is hostile and will attack on sight.

The Mercenary wears a set of green [Redguard Clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard_Clothes "Skyrim:Redguard Clothes") and a unique green [Redguard Hood](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard_Hood "Skyrim:Redguard Hood"), as well as a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots"). He uses the spells [Steadfast Ward](/wiki/Skyrim:Steadfast_Ward "Skyrim:Steadfast Ward"), [Fast Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fast_Healing "Skyrim:Fast Healing") and either [Firebolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Firebolt "Skyrim:Firebolt"), [Ice Spike](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Spike "Skyrim:Ice Spike") or [Lightning Bolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Lightning_Bolt "Skyrim:Lightning Bolt"), carries a random amount of [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), and has a 25% chance to carry a [lockpick](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick"). He must be killed to safely access the chest containing the Lord's Mail.

The mercenaries and Majid can be a tough fight, so prepare accordingly.

## Related Quests

- **[Gift of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Gift_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Gift of Kynareth")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord%27s_Mail "Skyrim:Lord's Mail"): Recover a legendary [Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") [artifact](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord%27s_Mail_(item) "Skyrim:Lord's Mail (item)") and obtain the blessing of [Kynareth](/wiki/Lore:Kynareth "Lore:Kynareth").

# Skyrim:Alik'r Prisoner

## Overview

The Alik'r Prisoner in jail

The **Alik'r Prisoner**, a [Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard "Skyrim:Redguard") [scout](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatScout "Skyrim:CombatScout"), is one of [Kematu's](/wiki/Skyrim:Kematu "Skyrim:Kematu") men who came to [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") to find [Saadia](/wiki/Skyrim:Saadia "Skyrim:Saadia"). The Alik'r, led by Kematu, claim to have been sent after Saadia for speaking out against the government. This unlucky man was arrested for thievery and is being held in [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach") in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). The Alik'r Prisoner wears an [Alik'r hood](/wiki/Skyrim:Alik%27r_Hood "Skyrim:Alik'r Hood"), [Hammerfell garb](/wiki/Skyrim:Hammerfell_Garb "Skyrim:Hammerfell Garb"), and a pair of [Redguard boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard_Boots "Skyrim:Redguard Boots").

## Related Quests

- **[In My Time Of Need](/wiki/Skyrim:In_My_Time_Of_Need "Skyrim:In My Time Of Need")**: Find a [Redguard woman](/wiki/Skyrim:Saadia "Skyrim:Saadia") who is on the run from [her past](/wiki/Lore:Taneth "Lore:Taneth").

### In My Time Of Need

Upon talking to him through the cell door:

:   **I need to find Kematu. Where is he hiding?**
:   *"You have a death wish, then? If you know that name, you must know to meet him would be to meet your end. But it seems we both have needs, friend. Perhaps we can help each other out."*

:   **What is it that you need?**
:   *"I have dishonored my brothers by being captured, and so they have left me here. My life with the Alik'r is over now, but I have no wish to die in this gods-forsaken land. If I can be released from prison, I may start over. See to that, and I'll tell you what you want to know."*

:   **How much to pay your fine?**
:   *"100 gold will secure my release. You can afford that, can't you? I suppose you'd better hope you can, if you want the information. Get the money into the hands of one of these guards, and I'll tell you what you want to know."*

After paying the nearby guard, you can tell the prisoner that his fine has been paid:

:   :   **Your fine's been paid. Now tell me about Kematu.**
    :   *"Very well. Kematu is west of Whiterun. It's an unassuming little cave called [Swindler's Den](/wiki/Skyrim:Swindler%27s_Den "Skyrim:Swindler's Den"). You realize if you set foot in there, you're never coming back out. They'll kill you. But that's your problem, not mine."*

:   :   **I don't have that much gold.**
    :   *"Then we have nothing more to say to one another."*

:   **Why did they leave you here?**
:   *"Because I was clumsy enough to be captured. Kematu always says we're supposed to be the best of the best. I wasn't."*

Once you have paid the prisoner's fine and gotten the information out of him, the prisoner will then inform the guard about the fine, though the guard will not take him seriously:

:   **Prisoner**: *"Guard! My fine's been paid, now set me free!"*
:   **Guard**: *"Sorry, my ears aren't so good. You say somethin'?"*
:   **Prisoner**: *"I said my fine has been paid! Now let me out!"*
:   **Guard**: *"Right, right... Oh, look at that. I seem to have lost my keys. Might take me a while to find them. You just sit tight. I'll get around to it eventually."*
:   **Prisoner**: *"Curse you!"*

He will remain in the prison constantly, and is never actually released regardless of anything you do.

## Notes

- If you ask Saadia for suggestions on how to find Kematu during the quest, she will mention the capture of this prisoner: *""I heard one of them was just arrested trying to sneak into the city. If he's locked up in the jail, perhaps you can get it out of him."*
- In the game's DialogueViews files, early versions of the prisoner's dialogue for the quest can be found. One notable altered line being: *"All right, this should be enough. The Alik'r Base is west of Whiterun, north of Granite Hill. It's an unassuming little cave. You realize if you set foot in there, you're never coming back out. They'll kill you. But, it's your hide."* Seeing as the town of [Granite Hill](/wiki/Lore:Granite_Hill "Lore:Granite Hill") didn't make it into the final game, his line was changed accordingly.
- Even if you open his cell door, he will not attempt to escape.

## Bugs

- His cell door cannot be opened.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.4, addresses this issue. The door will now open with the Whiterun Jail Key like all the others.

# Skyrim:Alik'r Warrior

## Overview

**Alik'r Warriors** are [Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard "Skyrim:Redguard") mercenaries from [Hammerfell](/wiki/Lore:Hammerfell "Lore:Hammerfell"). According to the [official game guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide"), they are part of a group known as the **Alik'r Coterie**.

They are on the lookout for a [suspected traitor](/wiki/Skyrim:Saadia "Skyrim:Saadia") from Hammerfell, although it is unclear why. According to their leader, [Kematu](/wiki/Skyrim:Kematu "Skyrim:Kematu"), they were hired by the noble houses in [Taneth](/wiki/Lore:Taneth "Lore:Taneth") to track down a Redguard woman who supposedly sold out the city to the [Aldmeri Dominion](/wiki/Lore:Aldmeri_Dominion "Lore:Aldmeri Dominion"), causing the fall of Taneth to the invading Aldmeri Dominion armies. According to the accused woman herself, she publicly spoke out against the Aldmeri Dominion, who then hired the Alik'r to track her down. It is never fully explained, and it is up to you to pass judgment and choose who to help during the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:In_My_Time_Of_Need "Skyrim:In My Time Of Need").

Whiterun

These two **Alik'r Warriors** are both [Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard "Skyrim:Redguard") [scouts](/wiki/Skyrim:Scout "Skyrim:Scout") and show up in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") during [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising"). They both wear [Hammerfell garb](/wiki/Skyrim:Hammerfell_Garb "Skyrim:Hammerfell Garb") with a pair of [Redguard boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard_Boots "Skyrim:Redguard Boots") and wield the rare, curved [scimitar](/wiki/Skyrim:Scimitar "Skyrim:Scimitar") sword. One of them also wears an [Alik'r hood](/wiki/Skyrim:Alik%27r_Hood "Skyrim:Alik'r Hood").

## Dialogue

When you return to Whiterun after being tasked to slay [Mirmulnir](/wiki/Skyrim:Mirmulnir "Skyrim:Mirmulnir"), you will find the warriors in a heated debate with a [Whiterun Guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Guard "Skyrim:Whiterun Guard"):

**Guard**: *"Look, you've already been told you're not allowed here. Turn around and go back the way you came."*
**Alik'r**: *"We're causing no trouble. All we ask is to look for her."*
**Guard**: *"I don't care what you're doing, after what happened you're lucky I don't toss you in jail. Now get lost."*
**Alik'r**: *"We will be back. This is not over."*

*"Do you have news of our quarry?"*

After the conversation, the unhooded Alik'r will actively seek you out and say:

:   *"You there. We are looking for someone in Whiterun, and will pay good money for information."*

From this point forward, both of them will have the same dialogue options; when asked who they are looking for, they will start the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:In_My_Time_Of_Need "Skyrim:In My Time Of Need") with the response:

:   *"A woman -- a foreigner in these lands. Redguard, like us. She is likely not using her true name. We will pay for any information regarding her location. We are not welcome here in Whiterun, so we will be in [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead") if you learn anything."*
:   **Why are you looking for this person?**
:   *"It's none of your concern. All you need to know is that we're paying for information. If that doesn't interest you, feel free to walk away."*

Lastly, they will repeat: *"We're looking for a fugitive who comes from Hammerfell. A Redguard woman. She may be somewhere in this city."* The final words will be: *"If you locate her, find us in Rorikstead."*

Both warriors will then obey the guards' orders and leave Whiterun, walking all the way to Rorikstead. Once there, they will check in at [Frostfruit Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostfruit_Inn "Skyrim:Frostfruit Inn") and await news from you. If you enter the inn, they will anxiously keep asking:

:   *"Do you have news of our quarry?"*

Once you have located the [suspected Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Saadia "Skyrim:Saadia"), provided you didn't make an agreement with [Kematu](/wiki/Skyrim:Kematu "Skyrim:Kematu"), returning to the Frostfruit Inn will give you a new dialogue option, namely to tell them you have seen her:

:   *"You have? Where? Tell me now!"* If you ask what is in it for you, they will promise: *"Money, if that is what you wish. Now tell me where she is!"* When you tell them, you will be asked for one last favor: *"We cannot go after her, not without drawing attention. You must bring her to us. Lead her to the Whiterun stables, outside of the city. We will wait for you there."* As soon as you leave the inn, both warriors will be disabled and disappear from the game.

Wilderness

*"Listen, wench, we're on to you."*

These two **Alik'r Warriors** can be found wandering the roads of Skyrim, in search of the suspected female Redguard. They will both show up in the wilderness under the same circumstances as their two Whiterun companions. They both wear the same outfit: [Hammerfell garb](/wiki/Skyrim:Hammerfell_Garb "Skyrim:Hammerfell Garb") with a pair of [Redguard boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard_Boots "Skyrim:Redguard Boots") and an [Alik'r hood](/wiki/Skyrim:Alik%27r_Hood "Skyrim:Alik'r Hood"). In combat, they rely on their [scimitar](/wiki/Skyrim:Scimitar "Skyrim:Scimitar").

When you [encounter](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Alik.27r_Accusation "Skyrim:World Interactions") them, they will be in the middle of interrogating a [Redguard Woman](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard_Woman "Skyrim:Redguard Woman"), accusing her of being the suspected traitor from Hammerfell:

**Alik'r #1**: *"Listen, wench, we're on to you. We know who you are, so you'd better come with us right now!"*
**Woman**: *"I don't know who you think I am, and I don't care. Leave me alone!"*
**Alik'r #1**: *"I don't have time for this foolishness. Now come along quietly and we won't have to get rough."*
**Alik'r #2**: *"Brother, I think she's telling the truth..."*
**Woman**: *"I'm not going anywhere. Now back off before I do something drastic."*
**Alik'r #2**: *"She doesn't have the scar."*
**Alik'r #1**: *"What? Oh... you're right."*
**Alik'r #2**: *"We've made a mistake. Now move along before that mouth of yours gets you into trouble."*
**Woman**: *"Next time you're looking to pester someone, make sure it's the right person!"*

After the conversation, you can ask them who they are looking for and get the response: *"We're looking for information about a woman -- a foreigner in these lands. She's a Redguard, like us. We believe she may be hiding in Whiterun, but we're checking everywhere to be sure."*

Swindler's Den

Six **Alik'r Warriors** can be found inside [Swindler's Den](/wiki/Skyrim:Swindler%27s_Den "Skyrim:Swindler's Den") during the quest [In My Time Of Need](/wiki/Skyrim:In_My_Time_Of_Need "Skyrim:In My Time Of Need"), all of them protecting their leader, [Kematu](/wiki/Skyrim:Kematu "Skyrim:Kematu").

They all wear the standard [Hammerfell garb](/wiki/Skyrim:Hammerfell_Garb "Skyrim:Hammerfell Garb") with [Redguard boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard_Boots "Skyrim:Redguard Boots") and an [Alik'r hood](/wiki/Skyrim:Alik%27r_Hood "Skyrim:Alik'r Hood"). In combat, they rely on their [scimitar](/wiki/Skyrim:Scimitar "Skyrim:Scimitar").

When you reach the room where they hide, three of them will relax in the northern side of the room, while the other three will have their scimitars drawn, prepared to fight. Depending on your conversation with Kematu, the six warriors will either leave you alone or attack. If you leave peacefully, they will be disabled from the game once you finish the quest.

## Related Quests

- **[In My Time Of Need](/wiki/Skyrim:In_My_Time_Of_Need "Skyrim:In My Time Of Need")**: Find a [Redguard woman](/wiki/Skyrim:Saadia "Skyrim:Saadia") who is on the run from [her past](/wiki/Lore:Taneth "Lore:Taneth").

## Notes

- During the quest, you will learn about another member of the Alik'r, namely the [Alik'r Prisoner](/wiki/Skyrim:Alik%27r_Prisoner "Skyrim:Alik'r Prisoner") who was caught sneaking into Whiterun and now serves his time in the dungeon of [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach").
- Whiterun Guards will occasionally mention them by saying *"Have you seen those warriors from Hammerfell? They've got curved swords. Curved. Swords."* and *"As if Skyrim didn't have enough outsiders. Now we've got mercenaries from Hammerfell struttin' about..."*

## Bugs

- The first two Alik'r warriors will appear back in Whiterun after the related quest is over, remaining there permanently.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
- The World Interaction for the second two Alik'r harassing a woman should stop appearing once the quest completes, but does not.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.

Alor House

**Alor House** is the home of [Fethis Alor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fethis_Alor "Skyrim:Fethis Alor") and his daughter [Dreyla Alor](/wiki/Skyrim:Dreyla_Alor "Skyrim:Dreyla Alor") in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").

It is in the marketplace between the path to [Raven Rock Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock_Mine "Skyrim:Raven Rock Mine") to the west and [The Retching Netch](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Retching_Netch "Skyrim:The Retching Netch") to the southeast.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Dreyla Alor](/wiki/Skyrim:Dreyla_Alor "Skyrim:Dreyla Alor")  [Fethis Alor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fethis_Alor "Skyrim:Fethis Alor") [General Goods](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "General Goods") |

## Related Quests

- **[Pain in the Necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Pain_in_the_Necklace "Skyrim:Pain in the Necklace")**: Find [East Empire pendants](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Pendant "Skyrim:East Empire Pendant") for [Fethis Alor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fethis_Alor "Skyrim:Fethis Alor").

### Exterior

In front of the entrance is where Fethis Alor generally sells his wares, with a narrow table holding five bottles of [sujamma](/wiki/Skyrim:Sujamma "Skyrim:Sujamma") nearby. To the left of the entrance is a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"), a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack"), and an open box containing two more bottles of sujamma. To the right of the entrance are two ash yam urns, a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block"), another woodcutter's axe, and two [scathecraw](/wiki/Skyrim:Scathecraw "Skyrim:Scathecraw") plants. The entrance has an apprentice-level lock.

### Alor House

The entrance leads into the upper floor of the house. Along the south wall are three straw bales, an ingredient barrel, a fish barrel, two meat barrels, two food barrels, one of which has a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") on top, an open box containing a copy of *[Words of the Wind](/wiki/Skyrim:Words_of_the_Wind "Skyrim:Words of the Wind")*, and a table holding two bottles of sujamma, a bottle of [shein](/wiki/Skyrim:Shein "Skyrim:Shein"), two bottles of alto wine, three bottles of wine, and a *[note](/wiki/Skyrim:Dearest_Dinya "Skyrim:Dearest Dinya")* to Dreyla. Near the west wall is a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") on a stand in front of the fire, with two chairs nearby. Along the north wall are three food barrels, a meat barrel, three unusable barrels, three crates, a sideboard holding a large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and copies of all seven volumes of *[The Poison Song](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Poison_Song "Skyrim:The Poison Song")*, five sacks, an ash yam urn, and two loose pieces of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood") on a wood pile. In the middle of the room, stairs lead down to the lower floor, with three straw bales, two ash yam urns, and a bench around the sides of the stairs.

At the bottom of the stairs, to the left of a doorway are two unusable barrels. Beyond the doorway is an area with rooms beyond doors to the southeast and northeast and a crafting area ahead in an alcove to the west. In the main area is a tanning rack, three sacks, a meat barrel, many unusable barrels, one of which has a food urn on top, and many crates. In the alcove to the west are four crates, a table holding a bottle of sujamma, a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"), a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), an open box containing seven [iron ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot"), and a chair.

The room to the southeast is Fethis Alor's bedroom. Along the north wall is an owned double bed with a chest at its foot, and a sideboard holding a bowl of [cabbage potato soup](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage_Potato_Soup "Skyrim:Cabbage Potato Soup"), a [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Stamina"), a bottle of sujamma, and copies of *[The Red Year, Vol. I](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Red_Year,_Vol._I "Skyrim:The Red Year, Vol. I")* and the [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Hallgerd's Tale](/wiki/Skyrim:Hallgerd%27s_Tale "Skyrim:Hallgerd's Tale")*. Near the east wall are three unusable barrels, two chairs, and a table holding three loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), an [East Empire Company strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Strongbox "Skyrim:East Empire Company Strongbox"), a [steel war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_War_Axe "Skyrim:Steel War Axe"), and a copy of *[The Axe Man](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Axe_Man "Skyrim:The Axe Man")*. Along the south wall is a fish barrel, a set of shelves holding two empty [petty soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem") and a large coin purse, with three letters to Fethis Alor titled *[first letter from EEC](/wiki/Skyrim:First_Letter_from_EEC "Skyrim:First Letter from EEC")*, *[second letter from EEC](/wiki/Skyrim:Second_Letter_from_EEC "Skyrim:Second Letter from EEC")*, and *[third letter from EEC](/wiki/Skyrim:Third_Letter_from_EEC "Skyrim:Third Letter from EEC")* on the floor in front of the shelves, and two ingredient urns.

The room to the northeast is Dreyla Alor's bedroom. Along the north wall are two unusable barrels and a bench. Near the east wall is a meat barrel, an owned single bed, a table holding a copy of *[Bone, Part I](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone,_Part_I "Skyrim:Bone, Part I")* and a bottle of shein, and a chair. Along the south wall are two meat barrels, a set of shelves holding a chest, copies of *[The House of Troubles](/wiki/Skyrim:The_House_of_Troubles "Skyrim:The House of Troubles")* and all three volumes of *[History of Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:History_of_Raven_Rock "Skyrim:History of Raven Rock")*, three [lockpicks](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick"), three [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"), and two [green apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"), and a sack.

# Skyrim:Altar of Thrond

## Overview

| --- | --- | --- | --- |

Altar of Thrond

The **Altar of Thrond** is a [landmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Landmarks "Skyrim:Landmarks") west of the [Temple of Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:Temple of Miraak") next to a small cave containing [hagravens](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven"). It contains only one zone, *[Altar of Thrond Cave](#Altar_of_Thrond_Cave)*.

## Residents

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| | Resident Hagravens | | --- | | **[Ettiene](/wiki/Skyrim:Ettiene "Skyrim:Ettiene")**  **[Fallaise](/wiki/Skyrim:Fallaise "Skyrim:Fallaise")**  **[Isobel](/wiki/Skyrim:Isobel "Skyrim:Isobel")** | |

### Exterior

Altar of Thrond

The normal approach to the altar is from the southwest. Two [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bushes and five [blue mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower") are near and around the altar. There is blood splattered on the ground as you approach the altar, with a [sacrifice](/wiki/Skyrim:Sacrifice "Skyrim:Sacrifice") lying dead upon the altar.

### Altar of Thrond Cave

Dead alchemist

Upon entering the cave, you are in an ice tunnel heading north, with a set of [bone chimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Chimes "Skyrim:Bone Chimes") hanging from the ceiling in front of you, and more patches of blood on the ground. There are five more bone chimes along the tunnel. The tunnel turns to the east near a lit brazier on the ground on your left, then opens into a large cavern with three tall rock pillars. There are various ledges around the cave, and an altar in front of you with a dead [alchemist](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemist "Skyrim:Alchemist") laid out on top. Beside the alchemist is an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel") and a piece of [human flesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Human_Flesh "Skyrim:Human Flesh"). Behind the altar is a barrel of meat, and farther behind is a campfire with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") sitting on a pile of rocks with another piece of human flesh beside it.

There is an earthen ramp to the left of the fire that rises to the east and then turns south to reach a tent. It belongs to [Isobel](/wiki/Skyrim:Isobel "Skyrim:Isobel"), one of three hagravens living here. She is found standing in front of the tent, unless she has been alerted to your presence. Inside is a bedroll, an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"), and two apothecary's satchels on the ground to the right of the lab. To the right of the tent, along the southern wall of the cave is a [moonstone ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Moonstone_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Moonstone Ore Vein").

Fallaise

Heading north from the first tent, you will pass a barrel with a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and three loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") on top and a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") beside it. A second tent, [Fallaise's](/wiki/Skyrim:Fallaise "Skyrim:Fallaise"), is next. Again, unless she has been alerted to your presence, she will be found just in front of her tent. Inside is an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter"), a food barrel, and an adept-locked chest. To the right of this tent is a [silver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Silver Ore Vein"), and behind the vein, in the northwest corner of the cave, is a [quicksilver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore Vein").

Following the path from the second tent to the east and then south, you will reach a third tent. This belongs to [Ettiene](/wiki/Skyrim:Ettiene "Skyrim:Ettiene"), who is also standing in front of the tent unless she has been alerted. Inside is a bedroll and an unlocked chest. There is a quicksilver ore vein to the left of the tent when looking at the front of the tent. Heading due north from this tent to the northeast corner of the cave, you'll find a novice-locked chest in a small raised alcove.

## Notes

- The three hagravens inhabiting the cave are the three sisters [Ettiene](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Ettiene_of_Glenmoril_Wyrd "Bloodmoon:Ettiene of Glenmoril Wyrd"), [Fallaise](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Fallaise_of_Glenmoril_Wyrd "Bloodmoon:Fallaise of Glenmoril Wyrd"), and [Isobel](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Isobel_of_Glenmoril_Wyrd "Bloodmoon:Isobel of Glenmoril Wyrd") from the *[Bloodmoon](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Bloodmoon "Bloodmoon:Bloodmoon")* expansion for *[Morrowind](/wiki/Morrowind:Morrowind "Morrowind:Morrowind")*.
- This cave is an excellent base of operations after the hagravens have been destroyed. It does not respawn, has numerous storage containers and chests, and also has cooking, enchanting, and alchemy stations. Also, before completing the quest [Cleansing the Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn_Quests#Cleansing_the_Stones "Skyrim:Dragonborn Quests"), when sleeping in the bed here, you will not be randomly teleported to one of the [All-Maker Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:All-Maker_Stones "Skyrim:All-Maker Stones").
- In [Survival Mode](/wiki/Skyrim:Survival_Mode "Skyrim:Survival Mode"), this dungeon will not warm you up, unlike most interior locations. You need to stand near the cooking fire or either of the two braziers to warm up.
- The Altar of Thrond also [appears](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Altar_of_Thrond "Bloodmoon:Altar of Thrond") in *[Bloodmoon](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Bloodmoon "Bloodmoon:Bloodmoon")*.

## Bugs

- It may not be possible to mine the quicksilver ore veins, even after mining the other ore veins. The ore shows as mineable and the camera view changes properly, but nothing happens if you attempt to mine the veins, and a few moments later you will regain control of your character.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
  - You can work around this bug by equipping a pickaxe and hitting the vein manually.
- You may fall through the map upon entering the cave.
- It may be possible to mine the quicksilver ore veins to yield three ore samples, but not be released from the mining animation even after pressing the E-key.
  - The console command  `pushactoraway 14 100`  will break the animation loop.
  - Moving backwards may also break the loop. [*verification needed*]

# Skyrim:Alteration Ritual Spell

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-College of Winterhold.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-College_of_Winterhold.png) | **Acquire [Kahvozein's Fang](/wiki/Skyrim:Kahvozein%27s_Fang "Skyrim:Kahvozein's Fang") and use it to get [heartscales](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Heartscales "Skyrim:Dragon Heartscales") from a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") for [Tolfdir](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir "Skyrim:Tolfdir").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Tolfdir](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir "Skyrim:Tolfdir") |
| Location(s): | [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)"), random dungeon |
| Reward: | [Dragonhide](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonhide "Skyrim:Dragonhide") spell tome, ability to purchase Master level [Alteration Spells](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration_Spells "Skyrim:Alteration Spells") |
| ID: | MGRitual05 |
| --- | |
| |  | | --- | | **Prerequisites:** Level 90 [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") | | **← Previous** [Good Intentions](/wiki/Skyrim:Good_Intentions "Skyrim:Good Intentions") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | Prerequisites: | Level 90 [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") | | ← Previous | [Good Intentions](/wiki/Skyrim:Good_Intentions "Skyrim:Good Intentions") | | |

A dragon skeleton, ideal for harvesting heartscales

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Tolfdir](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir "Skyrim:Tolfdir") in the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") when your Alteration skill is 90 or higher.
2. Find [Kahvozein's Fang](/wiki/Skyrim:Kahvozein%27s_Fang "Skyrim:Kahvozein's Fang").
3. Harvest [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") [heartscales](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Heartscales "Skyrim:Dragon Heartscales").
4. Return to Tolfdir.

### Kahvozein's Fang

To initiate this quest, you must have an [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") skill of 90 or higher. Speak with [Tolfdir](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir "Skyrim:Tolfdir") and ask if there is anything new that he can teach you. He tells you that he has been working on a new spell but, to complete his research, he needs [heartscales](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Heartscales "Skyrim:Dragon Heartscales"). These must be cut from a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon")'s skeleton and can only be done using a dagger called [Kahvozein's Fang](/wiki/Skyrim:Kahvozein%27s_Fang "Skyrim:Kahvozein's Fang"). He asks you to retrieve the blade, which can be found in a radiant [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") dungeon.

Possible dungeons are listed below:

| Dungeon | Category | Region |
| --- | --- | --- |
| [Forelhost](/wiki/Skyrim:Forelhost "Skyrim:Forelhost") | Nordic Ruins | [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") |
| [High Gate Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Gate_Ruins "Skyrim:High Gate Ruins") | Nordic Ruins | [The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") |
| [Lost Valkygg](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Valkygg "Skyrim:Lost Valkygg") | Ruins | [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") |
| [Ragnvald](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragnvald "Skyrim:Ragnvald") | Nordic Ruins | [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") |
| [Valthume](/wiki/Skyrim:Valthume "Skyrim:Valthume") | Nordic Ruins | [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") |
| [Volskygge](/wiki/Skyrim:Volskygge "Skyrim:Volskygge") | Nordic Ruins | [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") |

### The Heartscales

Once you have the dagger, you must either slay a dragon or locate a dragon corpse in order to retrieve the heartscales. If you intend on hunting down a live dragon, it is not necessary to slay it using Kahvozein's Fang. You need only equip the dagger in your right hand (it won't work with your left hand) and loot the creature's corpse. The heartscales will automatically be added to your inventory.

Once you have the scales, bring them back to Tolfdir. He will reward you with the [Dragonhide](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonhide "Skyrim:Dragonhide") spell tome, and will now sell the [Mass Paralysis](/wiki/Skyrim:Mass_Paralysis "Skyrim:Mass Paralysis") spell tome.

## Notes

- It is possible to find Kahvozein's Fang in a dungeon and collect heartscales from a dragon's corpse before the quest is given.
- You can harvest heartscales even if the dragon disintegrates.
- Once the quest is complete, you can continue to use the Fang to collect a heartscale from each dragon corpse, in addition to the standard dragon loot. These scales can't be used for crafting, but are no longer quest items and can be sold to vendors.
- While it is not required to complete [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising") to start this quest, completing it is necessary in order to find a dragon suitable for heartscale harvesting. Although the [Skeletal Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeletal_Dragon "Skyrim:Skeletal Dragon") can be found and defeated beforehand, it does not yield scales of any kind. Heartscales cannot be harvested from [Krosulhah](/wiki/Skyrim:Krosulhah "Skyrim:Krosulhah")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") either, nor can they be collected from [Mirmulnir](/wiki/Skyrim:Mirmulnir "Skyrim:Mirmulnir"). An exception to the last point can happen if a Draugr Overlord is lured near one of the Blackreach lifts, using Dread Zombie to get it inside. Once inside, it can be attacked and its Unrelenting Force Shout will release [Vulthuryol](/wiki/Skyrim:Vulthuryol "Skyrim:Vulthuryol"), whose soul will be absorbed and its heartscales looted.
- Resetting your Alteration skill level after accepting the quest will prevent you from turning in the heartscales until you reach Alteration level 90 again.

## Bugs

- In your quest log, this quest is mistakenly decorated with the [Side Quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Side_Quests "Skyrim:Side Quests") knotwork (as displayed in the quest header), instead of the correct [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)") knotwork that is shown on all other college quests. This does not have any known effect on gameplay. In particular, this quest is *not* considered to be a Side Quest for the purpose of the [Sideways](/wiki/Skyrim:Sideways "Skyrim:Sideways") [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements").

  **Mod Notes**: The quest Type is "None" instead of "Mages Guild"

  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.1, fixes this bug.
- After retrieving the heart scales, it is possible that you will not be able to talk to Tolfdir and you will be unable to finish the quest.
  -  You can complete the quest by using the console command `player.setstage 000D0755 200`.
- The dagger's name is misspelled "Kavohzein's Fang" in both the Quest List objective and the map objective text.

## Quest Stages

| Alteration Ritual Spell (MGRitual05) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | Tolfdir is working on a new Master Alteration spell, and has asked for my help. He wants to study dragon heartscales, but in order to collect them I'll first need to obtain a special dagger known as Kahvozein's Fang. *Objective 10:* Use Kavohzein *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]*'s Fang to collect Heartscales |
| 20 |  | At Tolfdir's request, I've used Kahvozein's Fang to collect dragon heartscales. Hopefully this will help him to create the new Alteration spell he's been working on. *Objective 20:* Bring Dragon Heartscales to Tolfdir |
| 200 | ☑ | I've assisted Tolfdir in his research by collecting dragon heartscales, which he needed to figure out a new Alteration spell. As a reward for helping him, he's given me the first copy of the tome. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 30, 40.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MGRitual05 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MGRitual05`.

# Skyrim:Alva's House

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Home: Alva's House ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Alva%27s+House)) | | |
| # of Zones | 2 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| MorthalAlvasHouse, MorthalAlvasHouseCellar | |
| Region | |
| [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") | |
| Location | |
| [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Cooking Pots/Spits](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") | 1 |

Alva's House

**Alva's House** is a small house located in [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") that is home to [Alva](/wiki/Skyrim:Alva "Skyrim:Alva") and [Hroggar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hroggar "Skyrim:Hroggar").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Alva](/wiki/Skyrim:Alva "Skyrim:Alva")  [Hroggar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hroggar "Skyrim:Hroggar") |

## Related Quests

- **[Laid to Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Laid_to_Rest "Skyrim:Laid to Rest")**: Investigate a tragic house fire, and discover an insidious plot against the town.

### Exterior

It is the next house along the jetty from the [Guardhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Guardhouse "Skyrim:Guardhouse"). There are two flights of stairs leading up to the decking at the front of the house, which has a wooden bench and two [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels on it. The door is normally adept-locked.

### Alva's House

On your left when entering is a food barrel beside a long wooden table which holds two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a sample of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries"), two [pine thrush eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg"), a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") and several loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"). Above the table, hanging from the ceiling are two [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, three bunches of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"). To the right of the table is a basket containing two [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek") and hanging from a rack above are three [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"). In the northern corner are two barrels, one of which is a fish barrel. There is a large double bed against the northeast wall and a table holding two bottles of [Black-Briar mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead") is to the right of it. At the foot of the double bed is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") which contains leveled items. Next to this against the southeast wall is a tall wardrobe containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"), with a [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute") leaning against it on the right.

Opposite the door to the cellar is a fireplace with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") in front and a collection of common books and a copy of *[2920, Sun's Dusk, v11](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Sun%27s_Dusk,_v11 "Skyrim:2920, Sun's Dusk, v11")* on the mantlepiece. To the left of the fireplace is a flight of stairs down to the cellar. This is the only house in [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") to have a cellar. To the right of the fire are several barrels and sacks of food. Against the southwest wall is a square wooden table and two chairs. On the table is a copy of *[Immortal Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Immortal_Blood "Skyrim:Immortal Blood")*, five loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"). In the western corner and along the southeastern wall is a single bed with an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") at the foot of the bed, which contains leveled items.

### Alva's Cellar

Alva's Cellar

Upon entering the cellar you will see an open coffin on a raised section in the middle of the room, during the day it will have [Alva](/wiki/Skyrim:Alva "Skyrim:Alva") slumbering inside, as well as *[Alva's journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Alva%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Alva's Journal")* (see [notes](#Notes)). Around the room against the northeast wall are several straw bales. In the eastern corner are a couple of barrels and a round wooden table holding two [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") flowers. Against the southeast wall are several crates and barrels, some of which contain foodstuffs.

## Notes

- If you haven't started the relevant [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Laid_to_Rest "Skyrim:Laid to Rest") *[Alva's journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Alva%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Alva's Journal")* will be missing from the coffin. Once the quest progresses to the point of needing proof for the Jarl, then Alva's Journal will appear in the coffin, even if you have already killed Alva.

## Bugs

- On the right side of Alva's cellar, after going through the door, there is a hole where the barrels are. A bucket will repeatedly fall and respawn.

# Skyrim:Alva

## Overview

Alva

**Alva** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") sent by [Movarth Piquine](/wiki/Skyrim:Movarth_Piquine "Skyrim:Movarth Piquine") to [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") to transform some of the townsfolk into vampires while using the rest as cattle.

She is good friends with [Lami](/wiki/Skyrim:Lami "Skyrim:Lami") (the proprietor of the [Thaumaturgist's Hut](/wiki/Skyrim:Thaumaturgist%27s_Hut "Skyrim:Thaumaturgist's Hut")), and is the lover of [Hroggar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hroggar "Skyrim:Hroggar"), who is also her thrall (and therefore may not willingly love her).

Normally, she will spend her day at either the [Moorside Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Moorside_Inn "Skyrim:Moorside Inn") or the lumber mill. This changes once you talk to [Thonnir](/wiki/Skyrim:Thonnir "Skyrim:Thonnir") during [Laid To Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Laid_to_Rest "Skyrim:Laid to Rest"), as she will begin sleeping in a coffin in the basement of her house during the day (from 6am to 10pm) while Hroggar guards the house. At that point, Alva will leave her house only at night and wander around, most likely looking for people to turn.

She wears a set of [tavern clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Tavern_Clothes "Skyrim:Tavern Clothes") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000d1921 "Skyrim:Clothing"), and is equipped with a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"). She carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Alva%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Alva's House") to [her house](/wiki/Skyrim:Alva%27s_House "Skyrim:Alva's House"), at least one leveled [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") with a small chance of up to four, and a significant amount of leveled gold, ranging from 50 to 250 gold.

She knows the spells [Vampiric Drain](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampiric_Drain "Skyrim:Vampiric Drain") and [Reanimate Corpse](/wiki/Skyrim:Reanimate_Corpse "Skyrim:Reanimate Corpse"), which she will use when in combat.

During the quest [Laid to Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Laid_to_Rest "Skyrim:Laid to Rest"), she is normally killed by you if she is in the house when you break in to get [her journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Alva%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Alva's Journal"). If she is not in the house, it is not necessary to kill her to complete the quest. If she is not killed she will be found in [Movarth's Lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Movarth%27s_Lair "Skyrim:Movarth's Lair") later on.

Some other town members in Morthal will mention Hroggar's love for her and say they suspect he killed his wife and child to be with her, as he got together with her almost right after his house burned down.

## Related Quests

- **[Laid to Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Laid_to_Rest "Skyrim:Laid to Rest")**: Investigate a tragic house fire, and discover an insidious plot against the town.

## Dialogue

If you have not yet discovered her secret, Alva will be quite flirtatious towards you if you are male, saying:

:   *"Well, aren't you the handsome one. You and I should spend some time together."*

If you are female, she will instead remark:

:   *"Well, aren't you the pretty one. I bet all the men chase after you."*

However, if you have [vampirism](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampirism "Skyrim:Vampirism"), she will drop all pretense and try to warn you off with

:   *"I know you for what you are. This town's blood is ours. Leave it! Now we must return to our roles lest the sheep suspect the wolves."*

She may also make ominous comments about the town's fate, saying:

:   *"The people here work so hard, and they never allow themselves a moment of fun. It's such a pity. It won't last forever though."*
:   *"These people are like cattle. All they do is work, sleep and eat."*
:   *"Gathering plants, picking mushrooms, brewing potions. It all gets so dreary after a while. This town needs something exciting to happen."*

## Conversations

She can be seen having this conversation with Hroggar in her house if you sneak inside:

:   **Hroggar**: *"How are you feeling?"*
:   **Alva**: *"I feel wonderful, just like every night."*
:   **Hroggar**: *"Do you need anything? Are you hungry?"*
:   **Alva**: *"Oh Hroggar, you know I'm always hungry. Don't worry, I'll eat when I need to."*
:   **Alva**: *"Oh, look! We have company!"*

When at the Moorside Inn, Alva will often try to seduce locals, likely with dubious intentions. [Benor](/wiki/Skyrim:Benor "Skyrim:Benor") is one of these unlucky few:

:   **Alva**: *"I'm bored, Benor. Nobody wants to have any fun with me."*
:   **Benor**: *"If you leave that kinslayer Hroggar, I would be happy to keep your company."*
:   **Alva**: *"Hroggar doesn't have to know if we sit together. Or drink together. I doubt he would even care."*
:   **Benor**: *"You tempt me mightily, Alva. But I won't cuckhold*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *another man, even on*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *murderer like Hroggar."*

Benor's friend and resident housecarl [Gorm](/wiki/Skyrim:Gorm "Skyrim:Gorm") will get a similar offer:

:   **Alva**: *"Would you like to buy a lady a drink?"*
:   **Gorm**: *"What would Hroggar say if he heard I was drinking with you?"*
:   **Alva**: *"Forget about Hroggar. He's always so tired lately. I need someone with a little fire in their blood."*
:   **Gorm**: *"After all you've put that man through. You should be more loyal to him."*

She will even try to seduce the innkeeper, [Jonna](/wiki/Skyrim:Jonna "Skyrim:Jonna"):

:   **Alva**: *"Why, good evening Jonna!"*
:   **Jonna**: *"What can I getcha, Alva?"*
:   **Alva**: *"What can't you get me, sweetie?"*
:   **Jonna**: *"Umm... Did you want somethin' to eat?"*
:   **Alva**: *"Eat? No, I don't think I'm... hungry. Not now, at least."*
:   **Jonna**: *"Right. Okay, tell me if you change yer mind."*

## Notes

- If Alva is not killed before raiding [Movarth's Lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Movarth%27s_Lair "Skyrim:Movarth's Lair"), she will be found there, fighting against other vampires, and will not be hostile toward you. Attacking her there will be considered a crime.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.6, addresses this issue. She is no longer hostile towards the other vampires and is hostile towards you instead.
- After the end of Laid to Rest, Alva is supposed to be removed from the Morthal crime faction, but isn't.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.8, addresses this issue. The script call was doing it wrong.
- If she is not killed in Movarth's Lair at the end of Laid to Rest, she will be found back in Morthal a few days later. Attacking her is considered a crime at this point.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.9, addresses this issue. She will no longer return to Morthal once she goes to Movarth's Lair.
- Both [Lami](/wiki/Skyrim:Lami "Skyrim:Lami") and [Hroggar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hroggar "Skyrim:Hroggar") have a high disposition towards Alva. If she is killed, their disposition towards the player will be reduced to -2.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.3, addresses this issue. Their disposition towards Alva will be reset to 0, but only after the player picks up the journal in the basement.
- Alva is one of the few NPCs to recognize you as a vampire regardless of the stage of vampirism.
- She is not actually a vampire by race, and her race is instead that of a normal Nord. This means that her appearance will not change with [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") installed. However, she will still use the Vampiric Drain spell, and the [Sun Damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Sun_Damage "Skyrim:Sun Damage") and [Turn Undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Turn_Undead_(effect) "Skyrim:Turn Undead (effect)") effects do work on her.
- If you have already killed [Laelette](/wiki/Skyrim:Laelette_the_Vampire "Skyrim:Laelette the Vampire"), Alva will comment *"I hear you put Laelette out of her misery."*

Alvasorr the Rat

**Alvasorr the Rat** is a [Khajiit](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit "Skyrim:Khajiit") priest of Namira, who is found in [Arcwind Point](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcwind_Point "Skyrim:Arcwind Point").

Alvasorr wears a set of [Falmer Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Armor "Skyrim:Falmer Armor") and the [Dismal Visage](/wiki/Skyrim:Dismal_Visage "Skyrim:Dismal Visage"). He has a [Falmer Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Bow "Skyrim:Falmer Bow") and the unique Falmer axe [Namira's Itch](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Itch "Skyrim:Namira's Itch"), and carries up to 10 [Falmer Arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Arrow "Skyrim:Falmer Arrow"). He knows a level-dependent elemental attack spell, a healing spell, a ward spell and an armor spell.

Alvide

**Alvide** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") camped out in [Dayspring Canyon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dayspring_Canyon "Skyrim:Dayspring Canyon"). She came to [Fort Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Fort Dawnguard") for protection from the [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") but the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)") won't let her in. She came with her husband [Barknar](/wiki/Skyrim:Barknar_(Dawnguard) "Skyrim:Barknar (Dawnguard)") who also lives in the camp.

Like the other refugees, Alvide will show up in Dayspring Canyon during the quest [Beyond Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Beyond_Death "Skyrim:Beyond Death"). With no access to the fort, she will do very little but wander around, at times chopping some firewood or use the [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot"). She never sleeps. She wears a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic#0001be1a "Skyrim:Belted Tunic") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0001be1b "Skyrim:Boots").

## Dialogue

She is worried about her situation, potentially saying:

:   *"What if the vampires come here, after the Dawnguard? We'll be stuck right in the middle."*
:   *"Barknar insisted we come here, said we'd be safe. He also said we'd be inside the walls."*
:   *"At least Barknar and I are here together."*
:   *"I hope we can go home soon. I don't like it here."*

## Notes

- Strangely, Alvide lacks any kind of schedule. She will simply idle where she was put.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 1.2.3, addresses this issue. She has been given a default sandbox package.
